O vos, tres chiers filz, je vos ai acomplit cest livre qui est li derriens de la science de medicine ensamble l’emplissement de lui, et ai fait la fin per ses expositions et par ses declarations.	You, three sons, I have fulfilled this book that is behind the science of medicine the fulfillment of it, and made the end through its exposures and by its declarations.
Et m’est venu en vision que je le vos acomplisse avec cest traitier, qui est partie de l’uevre de mains, c’est a savoir «cyrurgie».	And I came to my mind that I have fulfilled this with the cautery, which is from hands' work, it is known as "surgery".
Et por ceu que l’uevre de mains est fortraite en nostre region et est etraingie dou tout en tout, si est perie li science et decopee, et n’est riens demorez de li fuers que les petites descriptions en livres des anciens que les mains ont muees.	And because the work of hands is troubled in our region and is neglected in every way, if it is perished by science and knowledge, and there is nothing left but the small descriptions in books written by the ancients that the hands have seen.
Et de ceu est venue li error et li vanitez, et sont closes les ententions et est aloignie li science.	And this has led to the error and ignorance, and the intentions are closed and the science is alienated.
Or me semble que je la vuel vivifier ensamble l’ordination de cest traitier selonc la voie d’exposition et de declaration et de l’abreviation;	I seem to think that I could revive this assembly of the order of this treatment according to the way of exposure and declaration and abbreviation.
et venrai ensamble les formes des ferremens de cautere, et des autres estrumens de l’uevre avec l’ajostement de la declaration et de preparation de li, sicom il est mestier.	and I will come together the forms of the fire-cauterizing instruments and other tools of the work with the assistance of the declaration and preparation of the patient, as it is their craft.
Et por la raison de ceu que nuls boins maistres de mains n’est trovez en nostre tens, est li ars de medicine eslongié.	And because no skilled hands masters are found in our time, the art of medicine is extended.
Et covient celui qui s’en entremet sormonter en la science d’anathomie, si com Galiens dit, tant qu’il saiche la juement des menbres, et les formes et les conjunctions et les separations d’aus, et aient connissance des osses et des nerf et des brais et le nombre d’ous, et le demenement et des voines movans et des reposans, et dou leu de lor issue.	And he who enters the science of anatomy, as Galen says, must know the judgment of the members, and the forms and conjunctions and separations of the parts, and have knowledge of the bones, nerves, and teeth, and the number of joints, and the movement and resting of the limbs, and the fruit of their issue.
Et por ceu dist Ypocras que li nons avec le non est mout, et avec l’uevre est poc;	And because Ypocrates says that the non-drugs are not enough, and with the work they are few.
et meismement en l’art de main.	and in the art of hand.
Nos vos disons en l’introite de cest livre que qui n’est conissans des choses devant dites, si se gart qu’il ne chiece en error et qu’il n’ocie les homes;	We say in the introduction of this book that those who are not acquainted with things before said, if they attempt it, they may err and harm men.
ensi que j’ai veut maintes fois plusors de ces qui s’entremettent de ceste science et si s’abandonent sen science et sens experiment.	I have wanted many times to write about these who become involved in this science and if they abandon this science and sense experiment.
Car je vis un fol mire qui copa I apostume de scrophules ou col d’une femme, et copa les arteres dou col;	I see a man who cuts off the penis of a woman, and cuts the veins of her leg.
por coi tant de sanc issit hors que li femme cheit morte entre ses mains.	and so much blood comes out that the woman dies in her hands.
Et vis I autre mire qui traït une piere d’un home d’eaige, et li piere estoit grans;	And I see another man who operates on a hernia of an old man, and the hernia was large.
si emporta avec li une piece de la vessie, et fut mors li hons dedens III jors.	if he takes with him a piece of the bladder, and the old man died in three days.
Et je i avoie ja esteit apelez por lou traire, et vis la disposition dou malaide et la grandor de la piere, et soi bien s’on lou tailloit il en morroit.	I have already been called upon to treat this wound, and I see the position of the helper and the size of the wound, and if it was not cut well, it would die.
Et vis I autre mire qui prist en cure I duc de nostre terre qui avoit la jambe brisie, et avec la briseure ot plaie;	And I see another man who treated the duke of our land who had a broken leg and with the fracture caused pain.
et li mires plains d’ignorance estraint la brisure sus la plaie as esteles par fort lieure, et ne lassa a la plaie point de xalain, et le lassa ensi I termine;	And the patient's ignorance tightens the wound on the wound as it is seen in short time, and does not leave the wound any pain, and leaves it at the end of the term.
et li comanda qu’il ne la desliast mie;	and he orders that it should not slip away.
et demora ensi que li jambe fut toute enflee et li piez et vint a perdition.	and waited until the leg was entirely swollen and the foot, and it came to ruin.
Je fuis apelez por venir a lui, et me hastai por venir deslier la jambe;	I was called to come to him, and I hurried to come and cut off the leg.
et quant je l’oi desloie si fut em pais et ne sentit point de dolor.	and when I cut it away, if it was in pain and did not feel any pain.
Mais toute voie li corruptions estoit ja confermee ou membre, et ne la poi saner;	But all the ways of corruption were already confirmed or member, and could not be healed.
et ne cessa li corrution d’aler par le membre tant que li membres fut dou tout perdus.	And the corruption spreads throughout the member as long as the limb is completely destroyed.
Et vis I autre mire qui effondra I apostume enchancreit, et puis enflama per le malice de sa signorie.	And see another mirror that will fall and be enchanted, and then inflamed by the malice of his lordship.
Car chancre, quant il est purs d’umor melancolique, ne covient mie qu’on i(l) touche de fer s’il n’est en teil leu c’on puisse toute oster ce que est corrumpus.	For chancre, when it is free of melancholic humor, only then does it happen that if it is not in part the limb can be completely healed what is corrupted.
Et por ceu, treschier filz, vos est besoig que vos sachiez que oevre de mains est devisee en II divisions:	And therefore, dear children, you should know that the work of hands is divided into two divisions:
c’est asavoir, huevre ou il a peril en plusors dispositions;	It is to know, how or it has risk in other arrangements.
et je mostrerai en chescun leu de cest livre ou il a paour et peril.	And I will show in each part of this book where there is danger and fear.
Por coi il est besoig que vos vos en gardez, si que li fol mire ne puissent mal parler de vos.	Therefore, it is important that you keep yourself informed, so that the foolish do not speak ill of you.
Si prenez vos armes en cusenson, et entreprenez vos malaides legierement et fermement, et usez de la millor voie si que per la graice de Deu vos venez a salut et soiez loez;	If you take your weapons in hand, and lightly but firmly use your hands, and use the best way if for the grace of God you come to salvation and be wise.
et lassiez les maladies espoantables de grief saniteit;	and let the distressing diseases of grief be cured.
et ostez vos armes de ceu que vos fait douter, et aiez foit en vos si que vos puissiez venir de cestui monde a l’autre de gloire.	and doubt your weapons of this that you do fear, and be sure in yourself so that you can come from this world to another for glory.
Galiens dist en aucuns de ses amonestemens:	Galen's words are not understood in any of his instructions.
«Ne prenez mie en cure male maladie, que vos ne soiez apelez fol mire.	Do not trust in the care of a sick person, lest you be called a foolish man.
» J’ai deviseit cest traitier selonc III chapitres.	I have found this treatment in three chapters.
Li premiers chapitres est des cauteres de feu et dé cauteres de medicine ague, et est li chapitres ordenez de lou chief jusques as piez;	The first chapter is about fire cautery and medical cautery, and it is the ordered chapter for the head until the feet.
et des formes des estrumens, et des ferremens de cautere, et de tout ceu qui est necessaire en l’ueuvre.	and of the forms of stitches, and of the sutures of cautery, and of all that is necessary in the work.
Li secons chapitres si est de taillier et de percier, et des ventouses et des plaies, et des estractions des saiettes, et des semblans choses;	The second chapter is about cutting and sawing, and ventouses and wounds, and the extraction of arrows, and similar things.
et est li chapitres ordenez et les formes des estrumens.	and it orders the chapters and the forms of the stitches.
Li tiers chapitres est de restorer les dislocations et des torcions, et des semblans choses;	The third chapter is about restoring dislocations and twists, and similar things.
et est ordeneiz des lou chief jusc’as piez, et des formes des estrumens.	and it orders the use of different tools and the forms of stitches.
Ainsois que nos nos remembriens de l’uevre, il covient que je die la qualiteit de l’aide et dou nuisement de chescune complexion.	However, if we remember our work, it is necessary that I give the quality of the aid and no harm to any complexity.
Je dis que li qualiteis de l’aide, et dou nuisement, est li plus longe parole et subtilz science et li secrez reponus;	I say that the quality of aid, and indeed, is the longest word and the most subtle science and the secret remedy.
et de ceu parlerent li plusors des saiges, et s’acorderent a ceu;	and they spoke of more things than the arrows, and they agreed to this.
et me soffisent poc lor paroles, car je redous la longesce.	The patient's hair is instructed to be let grow long and even for the fire cautery treatment. If pricked at the base, the eyes must be held steady to prevent movement until growth occurs.
Je dis que cautere aide universement a toute complexion ou il a matiere, fuer que II complexions:	I say that fire cautery helps in curing all complexions, regardless of their nature or type.
c’est a savoir complexion chaude sens matere, et complexion seche sens matere.	It is known that fire cautery can cure hot complexions with moisture and dry complexions with dryness.
En complexion chaude et seche ensamble matiere, deviserent aucun et dirent que cautere i est grans aide;	In hot and dry complexions, there is no other remedy or treatment than fire cautery, as it is the greatest help.
et li autre dirent le contraire:	And they say the opposite:
que cautere ne vaut a maladie que vient de chalor et de sechour.	That fire cautery is only effective for diseases caused by heat and dryness.
Car li nature dou feu si est chaude, et ne doit mie estre cureiz de chaude maladie par chalor, ne per sechour;	For the nature of hot fire is that it is very hot, and it should not be cured by hot disease through chilling or by any other means.
et dist cil qui dist lou contraire que cautere fait grant aide a maladie chaude et seche que vient en cors des homes.	And that which says the opposite that cauterization gives great aid to hot disease and dryness that comes in the course of men.
Car quant tu comperes le cors de l’ome et sa moistor a la complexion dou feu, tu trueves le cors froit.	For when you perceive the heart of the patient and its moisture on the complexion, you know the heart is burning.
Et je m’acorde a ceste parole.	And I concur with this statement.
Car je l’ai troveit aucune fois per experiment.	For I have never found it before by experiment.
Et toute voie, ne s’en entremette mie fuers que cil qui l’a esproveit, et qui conoit par lonc usaige le chapistre des cauteres, et la diversiteit des complexions des homes, et les dispositions et les causes de lor maladies, et les sorvenues et l’espaice dou tens;	And all ways, no one should interfere with this more than he who has experienced it and knows by long practice the chapter of cauterizations, and the diversity of complexions of men, and their dispositions and causes of their diseases, and their symptoms and the spasms of tens.
des autres complexions n’avons nos mie paour, meismement em maladies froides et moistes.	of other complexions we have no knowledge, just as in cold and moist diseases.
Et tuit li mire s’asemblerent et s’acorderent au cautere.	And they were found to resemble and agree with the cauterization.
Et sachiez, filz, que cautere ensamble feu si est des secrez des cures, et de plus grant bonteit que cautere de medicine ardant.	Understand, children, that cauterization is similar to fire if it is a secret of the arts, and above all, it is an ardent medicine.
Car li feus est simples, et ne vient mie fuers que au membre qui est cuis, et ne nuit a autre membre se poc nom.	For the fire is simple, and it only causes harm to the member that is cooked, and does not harm other members.
Les medicines ardans vienent de membre a autre en aloignant, et font venir au membre maladies de grief sanation;	The heating medicines come from one part of the body to another by moving, and they bring about the relief of symptoms of sorrow to health.
et par aventure ocit lou malaide.	by chance, the patient meets.
Li feus por sa hautece et por la bonteit de sa substance ne fait mie ceu, s’il n’i a superfluiteit.	The doctor has high hopes and the goodness of his substance does not do much, if it is not deficient.
Et ceu vos ai je troveit par experiment et par la longesce dou servise et de l’estude que j’ai mis en l’art, et esteit sus la verteit des choses;	And I found this by experiment and by the length of service and study I have given to the art, and it has proven true.
et por ceu je m’escuse de la longesce de la parole, car il ne me plait mie que je vos oste le secreit qui est reponus ou feu, et la qualiteit de l’uevre, coment il deboute les maladies des cors, si com li philosophe le dit en demostrant;	And I apologize for the length of the speech, because it pleases me only to show you the secret that is hidden or fire, and the quality of the work, as the philosopher says when demonstrating.
or le recevez en vos pensees.	1. For the fire cautery, instruct the patient to let the hairs grow long and even; and if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.
Et sachiez, fil, que il s’acorderent en quel tens doient estre faites les cauteres, et eslirent prientens.	1. Understand, son, that the cauters should be made in such a way that they are appropriate, and they should be pried.
Et je dis que cautere est covenable en tous tens, por ceu que li nuisemens sorvenans est desoz mis par l’aide dou cautere;	I say that cauterization is useful in all cases, because the pain is relieved by the aid of cauterization.
et meismement se li cauteres est por dolors necessaires fors et hastans que ne puent atendre le tens que plus grans malice ne veigne au membre.	And I say that cauterization is used for necessary pain and hastens that cannot wait for the time when the greatest harm comes to the member.
Et n’i pensez onques, chier fil, si com font li fol mire;	And do not think otherwise, foolish man, if they do it as the physician does.
car a la maladie qui est sanee par cautere n’a point de revenue;	For in the disease that is cured by cauterization, there is no return.
et il le dient ensi;	And he says therefore:
mais il n’est mie si com il cuident, por ce que cauteres nen est que medicine qui mue la complexion, et seche les humors que sont cause de la dolor, et vaut mues que medicine por le hastement de sa valor, et por la vertut de son oevre et de sa signorie.	but it is not so if they are careful, because cauterization is only a means of burning that dries the complexion, and drying the humors that cause pain, and is worth more than other medicines for hastening one's valor, and for the virtue of one's work and signory.
Et possans chose est que li maladie viegne aucune fois selonc la complexion dou malaide et lou leu de la maladie et sa vertut;	And there is something that the disease grows once according to the complexity of the patient's condition and the strength of the disease and its virtue.
et sont assemblees en lui les superfluitez par l’aquisition des viandes et des semblans choses, se ce n’est cauteres administrez em leu ou il ait poc de superfluitez et de moistor, si com cauteres de dens por la dolor, et les semblans choses, et teil dolor ne revient mie;	and the excess is assembled in him by the acquisition of meat and similar things, if it is not cauterized, then administered to the patient or he has little excess and moisture, like cauterization of teeth for pain, and similar things, and part of the pain does not return;
mais ce avient poc.	but this is rare.
Et mout de gens n’entendent mie por coi cauteres est apelez li derriens de medecine, et c’est voir;	But few people understand that cauterization is called the end of medicine, and it's true;
mais il ne croient mie que cauteres vaille aprés medicine, mais lor ententions est fause, et est cauteres li derriens de medicine por ceu que quant nos aministrons manieres de cures en aucune maladie et elles ne valent, adonc administrons nos le cautere, et il vaut.	The patient only believes that cauterization is useless after medicine, but they understand it is false, and it is a cauterization of medicine because when we administer remedies for any disease and they do not work, we then use cauterization, and it works.
Adonques apert bien que cauteres est li derriens de medicine, ne mie selonc l’entention des folz mires.	2. Therefore, it is well that cauterization is called surgery, but not according to the attention of fools.
Li ancien dirent que cauteres d’estrument d’or est muedres que de fer, et ne dirent ceu fuers que por la qualiteit de l’or et por la hautece de sa substance;	The ancients said that cauterization with instruments of gold is as harmful as with iron, and they did not know that it was because of the quality of the gold and the high nature of its substance.
et dirent que li leus de cautere ne fait mie porriture, mais ceu n’est mie voir car je l’ai esprovei, et ai troveit que c’est voir en aucuns homes;	They said that cauterization does not make any wound worse, but it is true to see that I have experienced it and found that it is seen in some men.
et cauteres d’or vaut mues que de fer, si com il lou dirent.	Et cauteres d'or valent mieux que de fer, si com ils le disent.
Et toutevoie quant tu chaufes estrument d’or, tu ne seis mie quant il est chaus par la color de l’or, et s’est tantost refroidiez;	And all voy you see the instrument of gold is heated, you do not know when it is heated by the color of the gold, and it has cooled down.
et s’on le chaufe trop;	And if you heat it too much.
si font au feu;	If they make in the fire.
et ensi i a assez d’empechement.	And then it is enough prevention.
Et por ce usons nos de cautere de feir que nos l’avons mues apparilliet a nostre oevre.	And that is why we use fire cautery in our work, because it has been proven to be effective.
Or vos ai ordeneit cest chapitre des lou chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que li voie soit plus legiere a trover.	Or you have ordered this chapter of the little finger nails, because it is easier to find.
dou cautere olivaire	Olive oil cautery.
Cist cauteres vaut a moistor et a froidor sus lou cerveil, et en i a dous c’on fait par la cause d’une maladie qui est apelee «soda», et par la cause de maintes humors qui dessendent dou chief as eulz, et as oreilles, et por multitude de songes et dolor de dens et dolor de gorge, et meismement a toutes maladies qui vienent de froidor si com paralisie et sode et apoplexie et semblans maladies.	Olive oil cautery is used on moist and cold hands, and it is done for the disease called "soda," and for many humors that descend from the little finger as ears, and eyes, and numerous sleeplessness and toothache and throat pain, and also for all diseases that come from cold, such as paralysis, apoplexy, and semblances of disease.
Li forme de cest cautere si est que li malaides soit espurgiez par medicine solutive mondifiant le chief III nuis ou IIII, selonc ceu que li vertus et li eaige et li acostumance dou malaide le puet soffrir;	The form of this cauterization if it is that the patient has been purged by solvent medicine changing the head, III nuis or IIII, according to which virtue and strength and accustomed habit of the patient he can bear.
et puis fai rere lou chief dou malaide.	And then repeat the chief of the male patient.
Et puis le fai seoir croisiet entre tes mains, et mettre ses mains sor som peis;	And then make the patient sit cross-legged between your hands, and put your hands on their shoulders.
aprés met la racine de ta palme sus la racine de son neis entre ses II eulz;	After, place the root of your palm tree between the roots of his two legs.
et lai ou venra tes dois moiens, si saigne d’enche puis eschaufe le cautere qui est apelé «olivare», de coi ci est li forme:	And if your two hands come together, bleed slightly, and clean the fire cautery called "olivare", which is shaped like this:
Et le met sor le leu signiet d’encre, et fai en dessendant et en estraignant ta main poc et poc en trestornant;	And place it on the joint of the elbow, and pull and stretch your hand little by little, and twist.
puis lieve ta main isnelement, et rewarde le leu se tu vois l’os I sol petit;	Then gently release your hand, and reward the elbow if you see the first bone a little small.
et se tu ne lou vois, si rencomence le cautere tant que tu voies l’os si com je lou t’ai dit;	If you do not see it, if the cauterization resumes as soon as you see the bone, like I have shown you.
aprés pren I poc de seil, et met en awe et molle coton dedens, et met sor le leu, et li laisse III jors;	After taking a piece of silk and rolling it, and tying it around the wrist with soft cotton thread, and putting it on, and leaving it for three days.
aprés met sus cotun moilliet en burre;	After making the silk thread even and smooth.
et laisse sus tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	And leave it until the burn is cool.
aprés cure la plaie de l’oignement qui est apelez «tetrafarmaçon», tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treating the wound with the ointment called "tetrafarmacone", as long as it is healthy.
Et se dirent li ancien, que quant plus demoure overte li plaie, plus s’espurge;	And tell him, the older the wound, the more it will bleed.
et por ce si aide mues.	For this reason, seek help immediately.
Et dirent aucun de ces que on doit tant lassier le cautere que partie de l’os soit arse, et puis rese on ceu qui est ars de l’os, et soit curez.	And no one of these says that you should stretch the cauterization so much that part of the bone is raw, and then remove what is raw of the bone, and treat it.
Et dient li autre c’on doit le cautere tant lassier sus, et bouter si fort c’on abaite de l’os ausi large comme I vertoil que les femmes mettent en lor fusez por ceu que les humors issent mues hors;	And one should continue to shave as much as possible, and press firmly until the bone is thin as the women do in their ears for the reason that the humors come out outside.
et doit on lassier la plaie longement overte;	And one should continue to shave the overturned wound.
aprés le doit on curer et sodeir.	Afterwards, one must cure and soothe it.
Et ces II manieres de cauteres ne me semblent mie estre bones dou tout en tout, fuers qu’en aucuns homes ou il ait voie de paor;	These two methods of cauterization seem to be the best in general, because in no man is there fear or doubt.
et mues me semble que je lou doie laissier;	And it seems to me that I should leave it alone.
car li chiés li est afoiblis par les solutions continuees de nature, si com nos le tesmoignons ens autres membres;	For the head of the shoulder is dislocated due to continuous solutions of nature, as we have experienced in other parts.
et meisme quant li chiés dou malaide est foibles par nature, et li premiere semblance de cautere est plus salve et muedre por moi, et de celi use je oevre en donques emsamble salut.	And similarly, when the head of the shoulder is weak due to nature, and the first appearance of the cautery is more salving and drying for me, and I use it accordingly, I assemble the salutation.
de l’anciainne dolor dou chief	1. of the ancient pain of the head
Quant en tout le chief vient dolor croniques, et dure longement, si doit user li malaides yeris et pilules qui sont apelees «cochie», et d’espurgement de chief et d’oiles et d’emplastres;	Throughout the entire head comes chronic pain, and lasts a long time, if it must use the drugs called "cochies" and pills, and purging of the head and oils and plasters.
et s’on li fait le cautere que nos avons devant dit, et il ne vaut.	And if we make the cautery as we have mentioned before, it is not worth it.
Pren warde se li chiés dou malade est de fort nature, et qu’il ne soit trop froit;	The head of the patient's shoulder is severely dislocated, and it cannot be moved.
adonques le cauterize desoz celui cautere un poc que nos avons dit desus.	Therefore, the fire cautery should be applied to this area that we have previously mentioned.
Aprés fai cautere sus chescune corne dou chief jusc’a l’os, si com devant avons dit, et fai I cautere ou leu qui est apelez «vasselz»;	After performing the fire cautery on each of the patient's corneas, as we have previously described, and then performing the fire cautery on the area called "vaselines,"…
et est I leus en coi on met ventouses;	and it is these that are then covered with a ventouche.
et alige ta main si que tu ne voises mie jusc’a l’os:	and clean your hand if you do not see the bone.
li malaides sent trop plus grant dolor en cest cautere que as autres, et je em parlerai aillors;	The patient feels much greater pain in this fire cautery than in others, and I will speak to you about it further.
et covient que li cauteres des cornes soient plus subtis que cil dont on cautere la moieneteit dou chief, et c’est li forme:	et covrent que li cauteres des cornes soient plus subtis que cil dont on cautere la moieneteit dou chief, et c'est li forme:
dou cautere dou chief	For the fire cautery, instruct the patient to let the hairs grow long and
Quant en une partie dou chief vient dolor sodaine, et est estendue li maladie jusc’a l’oil, et li chiés est espurgiez par medicines mondifians, et on a fait les autres cures que j’ai dit en la division des maladies, et tout ceu ne profite mie:	When one part of the body suddenly hurts, and it spreads throughout the illness, and the head is purged with altered medicines, and the other cures mentioned in the division of diseases have been done, but none of them help.
adonques li fai cauteres selonc II manieres, c’est a savoir de medicine ague et de feir.	And I made the cauterization in two ways, that is, with medicinal ignition and with iron.
Li cauteres de medicine ague si est que tu preignes une doce d’alz, et oste l’escorce et le recope I poc as II chiés, et puis fent la temple ou li dolor tient en teil maniere que tu puisses reponre la doce d’alz desoz le cuir;	If the cauterization is with medicinal ignition and you burn a dose of alum, it will scorch and rupture the skin, and then they make the temple where the pain holds in a certain way so that you can replenish the dose of alum on the wound.
et quant elle sera reponuee si le lie et l’estraint bien et le laisse ensi XII houres;	When it is corrected and held firmly, and left alone for twelve hours.

aprés met coton moilliet en abin d’uef ou en jus de persillion sus l’oil;	after wipe with soft cloth around the eye or with persillon oil on the oil:
aprés chaufe le cautere qui est teilz:	After heating the cauterizing tool that is divided into parts:
et est chevez au chief si com li forme d’une penne de vouteul, ensamble la queil soit li cautere;	and it is bent at the head if it forms like a quill of feather, assemble the cautery so that it is the one bent.
se tu vues, si soit apointé des l’un chief dusc’a l’autre, et se tu vues, si soit ausi com une tente;	if you see, if it is pointed at the head and if you see, if it is like a tent.
mais toutevoie, cist qui est chevez vaut mues por ton ovraige.	but still, this one that is bent must be straight for your work.
Aprés presse la fistule s’ele est overte, et en trai la porriture, et la seche;	After pressing the fistula it will be stretched, and in the dough, and it is dried.
et s’ele est close, si la oevre, et trai fuers la bowe;	and if it is closed, then the work, and it must be made into a mold.
aprés met sus le cautere chaut forment, et tien ta main au cautere a la partie dou neif ensus de l’oil, que ta mains ne faice folie;	After the fire cautery is applied, and hold your hand on the cautery at the part where the oil is seeping out of the wound, so that your hands do not get burned.
et met le cautere en la graisse de l’oil, et la corromp.	and place the cautery in the grease of the oil, and corrupt it.
Se tu viens au comencement dou cautere jusc’a l’os, si serait bien.	If you come to the beginning of the cauterization at the bone, it would be good.
Se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere encor une fois, et autre se tu en as mestier, et le laisse III jors;	If this does not work, then reapply the cautery again, and if you have the chance, leave it for three days.
aprés i met sus coton moilliet en burre, et lou cure de l’oignement desiccatif tant qu’il soit sanez, et se XL jors passent qu’il ne soit sanez, si met sus medicine ague corrosive tant que li os soit descovers;	After that, apply moist cotton wool to the wound, and apply the desiccating ointment as soon as it is clean, and if after forty days it is not clean, then apply an acidic corrosive medicine as soon as the bone is exposed.
et lou reis selonc ceu que il venrait en son chapistre.	And the traveler follows according to what comes in his chapter.
Et i a une maniere de cautere de fistule que aucun des anciens dirent.	And there is a way of cauterizing fistulas that no ancient ones knew.
Entens a fistule, et fens le leu;	Understand the fistula, and feel the leg.
aprés met en la fendure I camahan subtil de coi ci est li forme:	After putting the needle in the fistula, the subtle change is that there is a form:
et i font a la quantiteit d’une .З. de plonc;	and they make a quantity of one .З. of puncture;
et tien ta main ou camahan fermement, et ne se mueve li malaides nes point, que li plons fondus ne corre a son oil;	and hold your hand firmly on the needle, and do not move the patient until the punctures are closed and the wound does not open, that the holes do not touch their oil.
et covient c’on mette sus l’oil a malaide coton moilliet en abin d’uefz ou en awe:	and it is necessary to put on the oil with cotton wool softened in the corner of the eye or in the ear.
li plonc si art lou leu de fistule, et lou saine per mervillouse saniteit.	When the head of the shoulder is dislocated due to moisture, and it is reset but cannot stay in place, repeatedly dislocating with slight movement as we have experienced, then you must first reset the dislocation.
Et se li fistule est sanee per le cautere que nos avons dit, c’est boin.	If the fistula is healed by the cauterization we have described, that is good.
Se ce non, si covient aministrer pertus au neif, et ramener la fistule au cors dou neif selonc ceu qu’il covient en som propre leu.	If not, then it is necessary to administer purgatives to the newborn, and bring the fistula back to the center of the umbilicus according to what is appropriate for the specific case.
des crevaices en levres	cracks in the lips
Mout de fois avienent crevaices en levres que sont apelees «poil», et meismement en levres des enfans.	Often there are cracks in the lips that are called "splits," and also in the lips of children.

de l’aposteme de la goule	of the abscess of the gall
Quant apostume vient en la racine de la goule ou en l’uve, ou ou palais, ou as racines des dens, aprés fait porriture et ront et est enveillis et devient fistule;	When abscess comes from the root of the gout or the vein, or the tooth, or the roots of the teeth, after making a purge and vomiting and it becomes watery and turns into a fistula.

adonques covient il que tu aies I cautere selonc la quantiteit de la fistule;	Because it is necessary that you have a cauterization according to the size of the fistula.
aprés le bote ou pertus de la fistule, et tien ta main tant que li fer chaus viegne au font de li, et ou derrien leu;	After the plug or stopper of the fistula, and hold your hand until the fire comes out of the mouth, and when it's done.

et s’il est curez ensi, c’est boin;	And if it is cured once or twice, it's good.

de la dolor des dens	of the pain of the teeth
Quant dolor de dens vient por froidor, ou il i a froidor ou veir, et les cures de medicine ne valent, adonc i ait mestier de cautere selonc II manieres:	When pain in the tooth comes from cold, whether it is cold or not, and the remedies of medicine are insufficient, then it has to be managed in two ways:
et cautere de burre et cautere de feu.	And cauterize with salt and fire.
Cautere de burre si est telz que tu preignes burre de vaiche, et le bout en une cuillier de fer ou d’arain;	If you can only find salt, then cauterize with it, and make the end as sharp as possible, either with a iron or a steel tip.

et ensi fai sovent tant que sa vertus viegne a la racine de la dent, et se tu vues si moille laine et coton en burre froit, et met sus le dent doillant, et met sus I fer chaut tant que li feus viegne au chevement dou dent.	And often until the virtue reaches the root of the tooth, and if you see that the cotton and thread are burning, and put the iron handle on it as soon as the fire reaches the point of the tooth.
Li cauteres ensamble feu si est telz que tu preignes uns cainne de fer ou d’arain, et soit grosse si que li feus ne viegne a la bouche dou malaide;	The first sentence to translate is: "Li cauteres ensamble feu si est telz que tu preignes uns cainne de fer ou d’arain, et soit grosse si que li feus ne viegne a la bouche dou malaide;

fai ceu sovent, car li dolor sera ostee celui jor meisme ou l’endemain.	Do this often, as the pain will be relieved either immediately or the next day.

des scrophules	The first sentence to translate is "des scrophules
Quant les scrophules sont de fleume et de moistors froides, et ne sont obeissans a digestion par medicines, adonques eschaufe le cautere cheveit de coi ci aprés vient li forme, et ait II aovertures por les fumees a issir au cautere de l’autre partie;	When the scrofulous boils are full and cold, and do not respond to medication for digestion, therefore, wash the fire cautery with soap after it comes out, and there will be openings for the smoke to exit from the other side.

Li forme de la cainne:	The form of the collar:

de la toust	Of the entire

de la dislocation de l’ajutoire	of the dislocation of the shoulder.

Quant en l’estomac vienent froidures et mout de moistors tant qu’il l’estraient a sa complexion, et sont multipliet li catharre a lui, et es manieres de cures acostumees et il ne profite mie, adonc covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son dos, et estende ses jambes et ses mains.	When coldness and moisture come to the stomach and it is pulled out of its complexion, and the purges are multiplied for him, and the customary cures are made, and he does not benefit, then it is necessary that the patient be laid on his back, and his legs and hands are extended.

dou cautere de pleuresin	Dou cauterization of plasters

de la mice	of the mouse.

Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take the linen and oil it, and put it in the socket that is between the thumb and little finger and the other which is called the fossil.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	After drying the goat hoof, and burning it until it is charred, and then putting it on wool, and leaving it as long as it remains stained.
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	and then reapply, and continue to apply as long as you feel by touch that it is going towards the hoof, and that the pain is subsiding.
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	And these methods of cauterization are called "beaver cauterization".
de la dolor dou dos	Of the pain in the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether by touching or drumming or from too much evacuation, or from the expansion of cold matter, none of these appearances warrants cauterization, rather it is for the one who has come from the infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	It is necessary after the patient has been freed from the fetid or other pills, that the doctor places his hand on the patient's back, where the pain holds, and makes three lines with a knife, and in each line, cauterizes or more according to the skill and quantity that the patient can bear.
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	And it is done with the cauterization according to the point called "points".
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	And if you see, make three or four cauterizations at the cauterization clavicle according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	This disease often affects many children, and the signs of its beginning are that they constrict their eyes when they are born, and cry.
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	and you thrust your spine into the floor and into its appearance that comes from the other spines.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and you see it cured, if it is burned at the fire cautery according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	If the cautery darkens each part of the spine evenly.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see, if it is burned at the spine with the fire cautery pricking two or three lines, and they are points close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After healing the wound as much as it is healthy according to what we have said, and if you do not want to perform a burn in silk that is in the spine of the neck.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When pain from joints due to moisture expands to every part of the body and when pain comes in the foot, which they call "gout" properly, and when it is of a cold cause and remedies of medicines do not cure it, it is cured by cauterization in a certain way:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	Make the head of the cauterization at the joint of the foot, and the olive-shaped cauterization according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	If it is necessary that you prick the face with a sharp object, then perform the cauterization on the entire cauterization as claimed "point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	And if the pains come to the knee and other joints, and this happens many times, I advise you to cauterize each knee with three or four points of the cauterizing iron on all the olive cauterization points.
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you have more skill, but do not hold your hand for as long as the pain lasts, it will be too late.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	If the pain descends to the joints and back, apply the cauterization we have described in this chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	And if the pains are in the hands, then make points every two lines.
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	And if there is no pain left, then make points on each joint and on the hair of the hand.
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	When the pain comes suddenly or in the shoulder, if it is cauterized on each part, and I give good government to the patient and prescribe medicine.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you make the midwife give medicine and purge the poison, she will be healthy in the help of God.
de la routure dou syfac	Of the rupture of a sinew
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When a fracture comes in twists, and the bones hang down like rags, and it is new, if it happens that when you see to cure it, it will not take from him the best of his youth.
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	and that he uses things that make the stomach loose, so that the belly descends from it.
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	after you have placed him on his back between your hands, and he commands that he shave his hair as much as the bowels are repaired, and you pull out to his legs, and sign that the fracture is set on the bone, and at all signs that it seems like half of a circle to the corners of the two corns;
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	Then rinse the fire cautery, and it is this form:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	As long as it is white and has a taste.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	Then remove the bung from its base;
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	and it marks your hand as not returning easily;
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	and work well on the thighs of the patient, and put a bandage on him and a sling on his arm, and another on the leg that marks the hands;
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	then place the cautery sign on all your hand, and hold it firmly and as long as you reach the bone, and if you don't reach it the first time, continue another until you touch the bone;
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	and make sure the feces does not come out while you are doing the fire cautery.
que tu ne le brulasses;	and do not burn it.
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	and so that the patient does not die, or other harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And you should know that when you do not come to the bone with the cauterization, your efforts are in vain.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	And it should be done subtly according to the size of the child, and also according to the size of adults.
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	after three days, cure the head of the shoulder as much as possible until the pain subsides.
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	after the treatment of other ointments as much as possible until it is healthy, and apply the cream for 40 days on the back until the pain is well soothing.
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	The translation of the line is: "And it is necessary that his wounds be left open for a long time, so that the wounds do not ooze when he rises from bed.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	The translation of the line is: "And after 40 days, when he wishes to rise, he should tie a well-made bandage around his waist, and every other day.
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	The translation of the line is: "and he should rest well, so that he works quickly and does not have too much intoxication from drinking and smoking, and does not overbake.
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	The translation of the line is: "And when he makes this instruction, it is completely healthy.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say this after the trimming in his chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture of the belly
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When hernias occur in other bellies and are known, and you see that they do not grow anymore, if you want to cauterize, you should do it according to the quantity of the fire cautery, and so it is for the third part of the hernia.
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	After the treatment according to what we have said;
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	And no of the old ones have said that one should cauterize with the fire cautery at III angles according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	But the first sign of the bone is the fracture and draw a line for the length of the rupture, and another for the width, and hold the patient's hand tightly at all points of the cauterization claw.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	However, the first cauterizations are more gentle and milder.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of pain in no member.
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes in any member, whether from cold or wounding, and this pain lasts long, and the cure with medicine is not enough, then it must be cauterized at the cauterization called "points", and the cauterization according to the length of the member, its width, its strength, its virtue, its location of torsions and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	If it is safe with the first fire cautery, it is well;
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If this is the name, continue with another fire cautery on it, because the custom is that one must die in the member that it is nearest, but if you want to do the cauteries as long as the patient is safe.
de meselerie	of malediction
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The curses are never helped by burning once, and at the same time, the disease that comes from the putrefaction of flesh and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	You can see the cauterization, when the disease is at its beginning, and if it is cured according to what we have said in the division, and does not increase or decrease, and you doubt that corruption will spread throughout the patient, therefore I do the cauterization on the head:
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	I emmi the head quite deeply, and the other at the end of the wound.
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	and I suspend it at the two corners, and I pull on the hanger.
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	and I pull so hard on my hand that the cauterization sticks to the bone, and so that the pus comes out quickly, so that the vapors of the large humors can come out.
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	And the cauterization is done on the mouse according to what is before.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	And if the scarring is everywhere sparse.
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	And if the scarring is manifestly present, then you must first cauterize with these cauterizations that we have mentioned or chief, and I cauterize in some places, and II cauterizes at the corner of the elbow, and VI cauterizes at the corner of the back, and I grant at the croupe and I other delez, and II sus the II espaules;
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	And II suspend the knees, and II suspend the tendons of the big toe, and I suspend each joint of the hands and feet, and suspend the holes of the hands.
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	and you cut off the nerves that are under the heel, which you do not burn.
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	and never made a cauterization on the bone, and the other on the stomach, and the other on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	And you advise that the more you do cauterization, the more help you get, and it benefits you.
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	And you advise that the patient does not feel any pain during cauterization if the surgeon feels none, because the corps is already corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	It is necessary that the burn be large and small according to the members and joints, according to what you will find in ways of iron.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After curing the head with flour several times with honey and other remedies as long as it is healthy.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	When the member is inflamed and cured by medicines and ointments and plasters, and it is not healthy, therefore I do cauterization on the member according to its size and thickness.
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	And let there be a small amount of fire cautery inserted into the skin.
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then, the care of wounds as soon as it is safe.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	And never make a cautery on the hand, arm, or back, at the end of which the member becomes quiet and if it is infected.
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	And nothing else happens if it is not known about the limbs and the movements of the muscles in the corpse.
de albaras	2. Of scars
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	When the disease called "albaras" is awakened, and the physician's engine does not work, then let there be a small amount of fire cautery inserted into the skin, according to the quantity of the healthy skin, as long as the blenching is quiet and has its color.
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	Then the treatment of flour and lentils with rose oil and plantain leaves, and salve of colic and almond, of each a part.
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	And make the whole assembly, and bind with a cloth, and apply as needed to the shoulder until it is healthy.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment of syphilis by cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When the sore first appears, and you see it stop, if the cauterization is done at the cauterization point that seems to be a circle, then turn it completely around the entire sore.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	And all say that you make cauterization also at the mileau of a glandulent ulcer.
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	And all say that this is not good, because I doubt that it will not be ulcerated and corrupted, and I have already wanted it to happen never.
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And the most correct thing is that they be cauterized externally, at the cautery called "circle," as we have said in our mouth of cauterization.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	Of the inflammation that cannot be measured
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	When someone has a disease called "adubelati", it delays in dying either due to the excess it causes or because of the greatness of the patient's malady when they are old (that is, too many) and lacks blood, or for tightness.
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	and you see that they are near death.
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	However, the cauterization is done by pricking with small cauters.
aprés le laisse ensi.	after it is left alone.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For it will lag in measuring.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it lagging in measuring, if the cauterization is hot and this form is not suitable,
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the environment of this disease called "adubelati" as long as the cauterization is perceived by the ear, and it is such that the patient feels pain in a certain way that the course of the sweat is agile.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the treatment, if it is perfectly healthy.
li cure dou feu par fer	the cauterization by fire with iron.
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another way of disease is called "corrodens", and it is nothing but a mangy of the limb, because it eats the limbs as much as it does the dry sticks.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	If you see this disease in the shoulder that can suffer from fire cauterization, then sharpen the cauters small and large according to what is needed for the shoulder or the disease.
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	After the cauterization of all parts as much as you remove all corruption, nothing remains of it, that all that is corrupted is not ossified.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	Then let it remain for three days, and put on the burned parts with oil as much as the burned eschar is large, and all the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the care of burns caused by fire.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	And if you see after three days that healthy children are not born, it's bad.
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	and if this does not happen, then resume the cauterization on those who have not yet removed the corrupted hairs.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	And this disease has never been cured by medical care in the place of fire cauterization.
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	but all cauterization with fire is greater help, and I have already said that the cure of the disease by dividing:
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	Take what you have skill in.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	Of the pores that come as pimples
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Often it happens that the pimples are caused by inflammation, which is called "closed" according to our understanding, and it is a large thing that darkens the skin.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the treatment of this disease is done in two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	It is known as fire cauterization, and hot iron cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	If you are shaving, then the fire cautery is like a pen made of iron, and it should be made in such a way that it can penetrate all parts, and have subtle margins.
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	After you put the cautery on the nail, turn your hand completely around the nail until it reaches the end of the nail.
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	And leave the nail for three days until it starts to exude pus.
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Then make a poultice of boiled hazel twigs with silk, and leave the poultice on all night, and the nails will fall off and be separated from their roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then, treat the wound with ointment as soon as it is healthy.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	And if they are converted by defluxion of the core, and many times it happens in hands and feet, then you must have a hot iron cauterization.
et est en teil maniere:	And it is in such a way:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	Take an iron nail or a piece of wire, and put it on the nailhead and the neck, which is to remove warts.
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	And if it boils all over, then he puts a hot wax, and holds your hand well, and presses your hand while turning so that the edge of the nail reaches the root of the nail, and you can find the hot wax way properly at the root.
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	The patient suffers a little from the hot needle for an hour.
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	Then it is left alone, and it will rot completely at all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	I will create another step, as long as you are able to handle all of these, then cure the wounds that have been inflicted with fire.
li cure dou trembler	I will cure you so you do not tremble.
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	When any tremble from cold or nerves, or fever, and it happens that you must apply four cauteries or four on the spine, one cauterization between each spine.

des pustules puans	of pimples that have been inflicted with fire.

un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	A subtle cautery of marten's wax, or if the tip is burned at the fire, or at the cautery of Aristotle's root, or at the lenticular cautery.

quant li artere est copee	When the arrow is seized

ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	Or by cauterization, or by extraction when it is not yet treated, or by tightening the thread, or by medicines placed on which have caused pain;

Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here comes the first sentence to translate:

For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things; where there is doubt and fear, and many die.

de emigrainne	The first line of the text is "de emigrain

When the head aches and is hot, and there are gouts of blood and tears in the temples, and the pain becomes severe, and it is treated with medicines and all sorts of remedies, but they do not help, then we cut the arteries of the temples and cauterize, as we have experienced.

de la gresle	of the grit

de la graisse des eulz	Of the fat of the hairs

des poilz des papieres	of the papers' hairs
