puis estrai I fil, et met desoz la papiere une petite tente de couton et de drapeil, puis seigne sus la papiere une figure d’enche, si com la fuelle de mirte, et toutevoie il covient que li figure soit selonc la quantiteit que tu vues eslever la papiere qui est devisez a toz.	Then, take out the thread and wrap it around the hair, and then place a small tent made of cotton and silk on the paper, as if it were a bow, and if you see that the figure is not according to the quantity you see being raised by the paper that is designed to be so.
Et si a teil qui a mestier c’on cope grant quantiteit de la papiere selonc ceu que li papiere est mollifie;	And if in some part of the body where you have skill, you find that there is a large quantity of paper according to what the paper is molded.
puis fent a tout le spatumile sus les II lignes que tu as signiet, et comence des lou grant larmier jusc’a petit;	Then, following all the lines you have written, and start with the largest possible incision just;
et soit li une des fendures pres des poilz naturez en la groissece d’un raiz, puis boute l’oncine en l’un des II angles dou keur, puis l’escorche toute;	and make it one of the fissures near the natural hairs in its growth, then cut the tendon at one of the two angles, then scrape it all;
puis assemble les II levres a une costure d’une aguille a tout I fil de laine subtil, et essue le sanc, et fai aerdre la superfluiteit des filz sus les II sorcilz a tout aucunes choses gluans, se tu vues faire ce;	then sew the two lips together with a stitch of a needle at the end of the fine hair, and drain the blood, and dry the excess of the threads on the corners of the eyebrows for everything glands, if you see this done;
et se ce non, si n’en aies cure, puis laisse la costure et les filz jusc’a III jors ou IIII;	and if not, then leave the stitch and the threads just as they are, or three to four;
puis cure la plaie sens costure de choses sechans et constrignans, car li papiere se relive au soudement de la plaie et l’assemblement de li, mais li costure est muedre (si com dirent li ancien), et c’est ovraiges sens paor;	Then cure the wound with things that are dry and constricting, for the paper relaxes in the moisture of the wound and its assembly, but the stitching is threadbare (as they say the old ones); it is difficult to bear.
et si a une autre maniere:	And if another way:
et est que tu seignes la papiere d’une figure qui soit ausi com li fuelle de mirte, si com nos avons conteit, a III oncines desevrez selonc la forme qui est ci:	And it is that you sign the paper of a figure that is also like the flesh of meat, as we have experienced, at III bones you will follow the form that is here:
puis cope ceu qui sormonte as petites forces igalment selonc la forme qui est ci:	Then comes the one who surpasses with equal strength according to the form that is here:
Et se tu n’as pooir de tenir les tenailles, et li chose n’est mie igalz, si prent une aguille ou il ait I fil, et la boute emmi la figure;	And if you cannot hold the tacks, and the thing is not equal, then take an awl or if it has one, and pull out the figure.
et boute I autre fil delez lou grant larmier, et lou secont fil delez lou petit, et assemble entre tes dois les filz igalment;	and pull out another wire of the great lariat, and the second wire of the small one, and assemble the two threads correctly.
puis lieve ta main igalment, et lieve tout le cuir sus coi tu as signiet, si com nos avons conteit, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie par costure, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then gently your hand correctly, and gently all the leather wherever you have signed, as we have experienced, then stitch the two lips of the wound with sewing, and treat it until it is healthy.
et se aposteme vient a ton incision, si l’apaise de cerote et de semblans oignement assouajans;	When the abscess comes to your incision, if the pain of cutting and wound healing relieves.
et aucune fois avient que li poil de la papiere sont convertit:	And never has it happened that the hair of the paper is converted.
si covient que tu uses ceu que nos avons dit de l’incision;	If you must use what we have said about the incision.
mais li costure en l’une et en l’autre est plus artificialz.	However, the stitching in both is more artificial.
Li cure des caines si est selonc ceste forme:	The treatment of dogs if it follows this form:
et est que tu convertisses la papiere et la fent dedens selonc ceu que j’ai dit, et puis fai II caines par art, et II liiens subtilz ausi lonc com li papiere et li largesce dou spatumile est;	And if you were to convert the paper and make it according to what I have said, and then make the dogs by hand, and they are as thin and long as the paper and the widest part of the stomach is.
et cope as II chiés de II pars ou tu tiens les filz;	and hold as you hold the heads of the parts where you keep the strings;
puis assemble l’un et l’autre subtilment sus ceu que sormonte de la papiere de l’oil, et estrain les II cainnes des II parties forment;	then carefully assemble the other end of each string with the paper of the oil, and tighten the threads of the two parts;
et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, et li cuir qui iert estrainte morra et nercira et porrira, tant qu’il cherra par lui.	and leave no slack, and the leather that is stretched will become hard and brittle and crack, as long as it is under pressure;
S’il tarde, si le cope a unes forces, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	If it takes time, if the hold is tight, then treat it as soon as it is healthy;
et quant li plaie iert soudee, et si ert levee li papiere, et ne poindront plus li poil;	And when the wound is healed and the paper is lifted, and no more hair will grow;
et c’est li forme des II cainnes que tu feras selonc ceste figure, et selonc ceste quantiteit de lonc et de large:	And this is the form of the second cut that you will make according to this figure and this quantity of length and width:
li ovraiges est telz que tu preignes une aguille subtil, et i boute I fil de soie souef et subtil;	The tissue is such that you need a fine needle, and one end of a silk thread is fine and smooth;
puis assemble les chiés et noe l’un et l’autre subtilment, et soit li longesce des filz une palme de lonc;	Then assemble the heads and knot them gently, and make the length of the threads equal to a palm of length;
puis ordene en la chasse I autre fil subtil de soie briément, et noe les chief dou fil;	Then order in the race the other fine silk thread gently, and tie the heads of the threads;
puis mette li malaides son chief en ton sain;	Then put the patient's head in your hand;
et soit delez lou soleil si que li ovraiges soit declairiez, car c’est uns ovraiges subtilz et menus, puis boute l’aguille a tout la chasse en la racine dou poil ajosteit, et la fai percier en la papiere hastanment tant que tu la traies desus lou poil natureil;	And if the sun is shining so that the cuts are declawed, because they are small and thin, then take the needle and pass it through all the threads in the race at the end of the hair, and draw it through the paper as much as you pull out the natural hair;
puis estrai le poil jusque sus la chasse, et boute en la chasse celui poil, s’il en i a I ou II ou III ou plusors;	Then, remove the hair until the base, and cut off that hair, if there is one or two or three or more.
puis estrai ta main tant que li poilz veigne fuers a tout la chasse en la papiere avec lou poil natureil.	Then, remove your hand as the hair grows to cover all the paper with the natural hair.
Et se li chasse est traite et li poilz ne vient fuer avec li, si trairas la chasse au desoz a tout le fil que tu i as ordeneit, tant que li chasse veigne fuer dou pertus desus et que tu la voies par la vision de l’oil;	And if the hair is treated and the hair does not come with it, then you will cut off the hair at the end of all the thread that you have ordered, as long as the hair grows with pain and you see it by the sight of the oil.
adonques si trairas la chasse et le fil, et clo l’oil et lou laisse clo II jors ou III, tant que li poil s’aerde en son leu et naisse li char sus;	Therefore, if you cut off the hair and the thread, and close the oil and leave it for two or three days, as the hair grows in its place and the wound is born;
et se li poilz est petis, si acompaigne I poil lonc des chevoulz naturez, et soit alevez avec celui ou tu le laisse, tant qu’il soit eslongiez et puis le lieve.	And if the hair is shortened, then accompany it with long hair of its natural length, and let it be cut when it grows out.
de la porriture de l’oil	Of the oil's fat
Quant ceste maladie qui est apelee «aleacrati» ou li porriture vient en l’oil, si en i a de II manieres:	Regarding this disease called "aleacrati" or the discharge comes in oil, if it has two ways:
l’une natureil, et l’autre innatureil.	1. Natural way, and 2. Unnatural way.
Et avient par soudement de plaie, ou de tailleure ou de cautere, et par semblans choses.	And comes by wounding, or cutting, or burning, and in similar ways.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige en li est que tu fendes celle soudure, et dessevre les levres de li, et met dedens tentes de lin, et la lie tant qu’elle soit sanee;	And the way of the healing is to cut off that glue, and clean the lips, and put lint on it, and keep it until it is healthy.
et ne covient mie que tu uses en la cure de li de choses que sechent et restraignent.	And nothing else is needed but to use things that dry and restrict in the treatment of it.
Car se tu fais ceu, si revient li maladie pire que li premiere;	If you do this, it may lead to a worse illness than the first.
mais i oevre de choses amollissans, si com fenugreic;	However, if I do things that are softening, like figs.
et l’arose d’aigue ou altee et semence de lin soient cuites, et oignemens dyaquilon fondut en aucun des oiles, et i envoloupe une tente, et le cure de ceu.	And if the mouth of the wound is open and the seeds of flax are cooked, and the ointments made from dill are not found in any oil, and a tent is made around it, then the treatment for this.
Et li tresors de ta cure si est que tu te dones en garde qu’ele ne soude mie selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant;	And the treasure of your treatment is that you guard it so that it does not sound like according to its form before.
et cist ovraiges que nos avons dit nen est fuers que adresemens de ceste maladie, qu’elle ne reviegne selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant.	And the things we have said are not true that there is no remedy for this disease, that it does not recur according to its form before.
de la char qui vient en l’oil	of the char that comes in the oil
Ceste maladie que est desoz qui vraiement est apelee «axacrati», et est naturelz et accidens.	This disease that is called "acaratia" truly is called "acaratia", and it is natural and accidental.
Li accidens vient de plaie et de fendure et de cautere et de choses semblans;	The accident comes from wounding and cutting and burning and similar things.
et li voie de l’ovraige en li si est que tu preignes un aguille, en coi il ait I fil double, et la fiche en la char, et li fai percier des le senestre larmier tant c’a destre, si que li filz veigne en II chiés de la char;	If you prick with a needle, and it has two threads, and the thread in the chart, and I make it feel on the opposite side of the arm, so that the threads come to the head of the chart.
puis estent la char au desus a tout l’aguille, et la cope a I spatumile large.	Then the chart is at the end of all the needle, and the cap is wide.
Et se li figure de la papiere revient selonc ceu qu’il covient, c’est boin;	And if the limb is drawn back according to the rule, it is correct.
se ceu non, si pren I raseur et le met en la fendure, et torne la papiere, et fent II fendures ou costeit dedens la papiere;	If not, then take the ruler and put it in the wound, and turn the paper, and make two or three wounds according to the thickness of the paper.
et soient li chiés des II fendures des II angles de l’incision que tu as copeit, et soit fais uns angles si que quant elles sont assemblees, que li figure soit ausi com li figure d’une lettre qui a non «I griesche»;	and be the heads of the two flaps of the two angles of the incision you made, and make some angles so that when they are assembled, it looks like a letter that does not have "I griesche";
puis oste celle char, selonc la quantiteit que ses costez est agus desoz, de ceu qui enseut la papiere, puis ajoste les II parties desevrees, et les cout d’un fil de lainne;	then that char, according to the quantity of its cost, which is as much as the paper, then adjust the two loose parts, and the cost of a thread of linen.
puis lou cure de ceu que nos avons dit des medicines mollifians, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then the cure of what we have said about the mollifying medicines and tents, as long as it is healthy.
Et se li maladie vient de fendure ou de costure ou de cautere, si covient que tu fendes une fendure plainne desoz les poilz des papieres, et selonc ceu qui est ci devant;	And if the disease comes from a cut or stitch or cauterization, then it is necessary that you make a flat cut of the hair from the papers according to what is before.
puis desevre entre les II leivres d’une tente, si com j’ai dit;	Then, between the two shoulders of a tent, as I have said.
et doit on faire l’ovraige selonc la forme de la maladie, car elle est mout diverse en forme, et li saiges maistres appareille engien de tout som pooir coment il faice revenir la figure a sa forme natureil;	And it should be done according to the form of the disease, as it is different in form, and the masters' tools are adapted to everything that can come back to its natural shape.
et li malaides meisme, selonc ceu qu’il i covient d’ovraige et d’estrumens em plusors dispositions.	And the patient himself, according to what is needed for cauterization and excision in various positions.
dou soudement de la papiere	I should have said "should" instead of "shouldn't" in the original sentence. Here
Quant ceste soudure avient a mains homes en teil maniere que li papiere desus est sodee avec le blanc de l’oil, et ne puet movoir ne faire ses ovraiges naturez, si covient donques que tu i boutes la pointe d’un raseur desoz la papiere, et la lieve en haut;	When this suture is made by women in a certain way, that the paper of it is dipped in white oil and cannot move or make its natural cuts, then it comes to pass that you should sharpen the point of a razor and smooth the paper, and lie it on top.
et l’estent as pinceures, tant que tu copes ceu qui est aert au spatumile subtil, qui ne soit mie trop agus ne trop trenchans, si que li malaides ne puisse soffrir que li spatumile trop agus ne blecent l’oil;	When using forceps, as long as you cover what is inserted in the subcutaneous fat, which should not be too thick nor too thin, so that the patient does not suffer from too much pain nor excessive bleeding.
et soit ton incision, dont tu escorche celle assemblee, legierement, si que li papiere reviegne selonc sa forme natureil;	And make your incision, where you scrape the one assembled, lightly, so that the paper reshapes according to its natural form.
et est sanee toute celle assemblee, et font aucune fois en l’oil aigue salee, et le leve d’aigue douce, et de coliere;	And the entire assembled piece becomes healthy, and it never has any sharp pain, and it is lifted gently, and warm.
puis met entre la papiere et l’oil une tente de lin, et met sus l’oil laine moillie en abun d’uef;	Then place a layer of linen between the paper and oil, and put on top of the oil soft wool in abundance.
et aprés le tier jor use dou coliere et des choses soudans tant qu’il soit sanez.	And afterwards, after the third day, use a warm poultice and things that are moist, as long as it is healthy.
de l’ungle de l’oil	Of the finger of the oil
Saiches que li ungle est selonc II manieres:	Saws that the nail is cut in two ways:
elle est nervouse et semblans a I dur syfac, et une autre qui n’est mie nervouse, mais est semblans a blainche moistor congelee, que quant on la touche de fer et on la cuide panre as pinceures, si ne puet om;	It is nervous and resembles the hard sycamore, and another that is not nervous but resembles a moist, frozen blister, which when touched with iron and cooked with force, if it cannot be opened;
et l’une et l’autre semblance encomence devers le grant larmier, et croist poc et poc tant qu’ele cuevre toute la veue et toute la lumiere et le movement de l’oil.	and the one and the other resemble the great alarm, and grow larger and larger as it covers all the vision and all the light and the movement of the oil.
Et li maniere de l’incision si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz;	And the manner of the incision is that the surgeon places his finger in the patient's throat, then cuts the tongue.
et lieve la papiere a ta main, puis coil l’ungle as pinceures de petite doubleure, et l’estent au desus;	And gently place the paper in your hand, then use the small tweezers to pick up the needle, and hold it in place.
puis pren une aguille, et i met I poil de cheval, ou de vaiche, ou de buef, et I fil fort;	Then take a needle, and insert a horsehair, or goat hair, or beef hair, and a strong thread.
et double la pointe de l’aguille un poc et la fiche emmi l’ungle, et la perce a tout l’aguille, et lie l’ungle d’un fil et l’estent au desus, et escorche a tout lou poil le costeit de l’ungle qui enseut la prunele et la soie au poil jusc’au chief, puis cope lou remanant en la racine dou larmier a tout lou spatumile subtil et as petites forces, et laisse la char natureil ou larmier, si que par l’incision ne veigne li cors des larmes acostumeement;	And double the point of the needle with your thumb and pull the thread through the finger, and percet the entire needle with the thread and hold it in place with a single thread, and scrape off all the hair from the edge of the finger that touches the silk and the wool at the tip of the finger, then cut away any remaining hair at the root of the nail and subtle skin, and leave the natural or artificial nail, so that by incision there is no flow of tears.
et aucune fois s’estent li ungle a l’oncine soulement, et au fil, si com nos avons dit;	and no time has it been set straight on the finger alone, and as for that, as we have said.
puis l’escorche on a tout le spatumile souef de coi ci est li forme:	Then the scald, we have all the substance soaked, and it is formed like this:
Et garde que li spatumile ne touche la toile charnue et la rompe, et que li prunele ne soit percie;	And be careful that the substance does not touch the rough cloth and break it, and the prunelle is not pierced.
et aprés l’incision giete en l’oil un poc de seil broiet, et dou coliere fait de litargire, et le laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	and after the incision, a pot of oil is poured into it, and a cloth soaked in litargire is left to dry for the next day.
puis le cure de ceu qu’il i covient tant qu’il soit sanez.	And then the treatment of that which must be done until it is healthy.
Et se li ungle n’est mie nervouse, et tu ne pues bouter l’aguille, et li uncines n’i puet entrer, maintes fois est curee ceste semblance d’ungle de medicines;	And if the finger is not nervous, and you do not push the needle, and the joints cannot enter, this appearance of a finger of medicine is often treated.
et naissent sicom j’ai conteit en la division, et se tu la vues coper, si oevre l’oil dou malaide, et pren le spatumile legier poc agut selonc ceste forme:	and if I have told you in the division, and if you see it covered, then do the oil of the female physician, and take the light spumous poultice according to this form:
Et reis l’ungle desus subtilment, et se tu vois qu’elle amenuise point et li rasion i apresse, si distille de ta bouche en l’oil coliere fait de litargire et dou coliere rouge et seil broiet, et estoupe l’oil jusc’a l’autre jor;	And dip the finger subtly, and if you see that it does not soften and the ration is pressed, then distill from your mouth the oil of colde made of litargire and red colde rose and seil broiet, and it stoopes the oil to the other day.
puis rencomence l’autre ovraige selonc ceste meisme oevre, tant qu’elle soit toute ostee.	Then continues the other evacuation according to this same work, as long as it is all complete.
Se aucune chose ne t’est contraire en l’oil, si com aposteme chaus, adonques la lait, et cure premier l’aposteme chaut tant qu’il soit sanez, puis rencomence l’ovraige si com devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	2. If nothing is against you in the oil, as with an abscess, then the milk, and first cure the abscess as soon as it is healthy, then continue the pricking as before, as long as it is healthy.
Et se li apparance de la chair dou larmier nuit en l’oil par grant nuisement, si la sospent a l’oncine, et en cope une partie et non mie tot, que cors de larmes n’i viegne;	And if the appearance of the flesh of the arm is pale in the oil at night due to great exhaustion, and one part only is affected, not the whole, then tears do not appear.
puis distille en l’oil coliere rouge qui est fais de litargire.	Then it is distilled in the cold-pressed red oil that is made from Litargire.
de la char qui naist sus la prunelle	of the wood that was cut down by the prunella
Es eulz d’aucuns homes naist aucune fois char rouge, et cuevre la prunele et restraint sus les papieres et les torne au defuer, et semble une rose de balauste;	Some people have never seen the color red, and they cut the plums and wrap them in paper and hang them up, and it looks like a rose of balsam.
et li ovraiges si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz, et coil toute celle char as uncines convenaubles a ceu, et la sostien a la force;	When the patient is ready, the surgeon places their head in your hand, then operates on the joints, and tightens all loose screws or nails as possible, and holds it in place with your strength.
puis cope la premiere char, et vai tout copant au raseur jusc’a la fin, et te garde que tu ne bleces l’oil a l’ovraige;	Then hold the first joint steady while you tighten all the nails or screws as much as possible, and make sure you don't hurt the patient's arm.

et s’il i demore rien, et li sans chaus te sormonte, et tu doutes aposteme chaut, si laisse l’oil et cure l’aposteme de choses apaisant aposteme chaut;	If it does not cause any harm, and the wound is not infected, and you doubt the aposteme chaut, then leave the oil and cure the aposteme chaut with things that soothe the aposteme chaut.
puis revien a ton ovraige tant qu’il soit sanez, et ensi fai cant chars est ajostee en l’oil par ceste semblance.	Then return to your home as soon as it is healthy, and then make several charms with oil in this way.
Mais toutevoie il covient que tu aliges la cure de chescun oil foible de la voie natureil;	But it is necessary that you apply the cure of every weak oil of the natural way.
et de la voie accident, en ovraige de fer;	and of the accidental way, in the home of iron.
et ne bouter mie ta main en aucun de ces ovraiges tant que tu voies que cist membres soit soffrans celui ovraige.	and do not insert your hand into any of these homes as long as you see that your limbs are weak in this home.
des voines des eulz	of veins of hairs
Sebel sont voinnes rouges que sont covertes sus l’oil, et tolent a la veue son ovraige et afoiblissent l’oil toz jors.	Several veins are red that are covered with oil, and they touch the eye's surface and weaken the oil for all time.
Mestier est donques au premier que tu regardes se li oil, en coi sebel est, est fors, et n’i a autre maladie fuers que lou sebel;	The first sentence translates to: "Therefore, the first thing you should look at is the oil, and if it is wet, then there is no other disease but the oil.
adonques le coil en teil maniere:	However, the treatment is as follows:
comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain, puis sospent celles voines a tout l’oncine selonc sa sapience, et soit li oncines subtilz double selonc ceste forme:	Instruct the patient to cut their hair at the base of the skull, then treat all wounds according to their knowledge, and make sure the scars are not too deep according to this form:
Et soient dui oncine par degrez en I cors selonc ceste forme:	And let it be known that one must cut through the flesh according to this form in degrees of one hand:
puis c’on coil as forces celles voinnes subtilment, et essue lou sanc houre aprés autre, tant que tu voies removoir celles voines fuers de l’oil;	Then you can reset the wounds gently, and remove any remaining oil as needed, until all the wounds are free of oil.
et garde que tu ne blecier l’oil as pointes des spatumiles, et fai cest ovraige a houre de midi devant lou soleil, et soies mout fervans en ton ovraige si que tu ne copes fuer que celles voinnes;	And make sure you do not bleed the oil with sponging, and perform this operation before noon in the sun, and be careful in your operation so that you do not cut any further wounds.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si distille en l’oil coliere vert et rouge por corrumpre ceu qui est demorez dou sebel.	When you have this done, if you distill it in the green and red ointment to corrupt what is decomposed and not well,
Et se tu n’as pooir de coillir tout ceu en celle houre, si fai emplastre sus l’oil de choses apaisans la dolor des eulz, et le laisse aucuns jors tant que li dolors soit apaisie et soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut, puis rencomence selonc ceste maniere qui est devant tant qu’il soit sanez;	And if you cannot distill all of it in that hour, then make a plaster with the oil of things that calm the pain of the limbs, and leave some parts until the pain is calmed and assured of not being infected, then continue according to this method as long as it is healthy.
et c’est li forme des forces:	And this is the form of the forces.
de la fistule de l’oil	Of the oil fistula
Li mire si nomment «arissati» fistule:	The mirror if it calls "arissati" fistula.
quant tu la cures per cautere et par medicine ague ardant selonc ceu que j’ai devant dit, et elle n’est mie sanee, si est engien en li que tu fendes sus l’aposteme, lai ou il doit meurer, et trai toute la moistor que i est, tant que li os soit descovers.	When you cure with cauterization and by applying the burning medicine according to what I have previously mentioned, and it is not well, then it must be removed if it is infected, and all the moisture that is in it, as long as the bone is discovered.
