si covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, et ses chiés soit en ton saint, et reis les dens ou les escorces aperent, tant qu’il n’i demore rien;	If you must make the patient sit still between your hands, and the head is in your holy place, and the teeth or gums are exposed, as long as it does not cause any harm.
et ensi fai de la noiror et de la verdor, et de la jaunice et des autres taiches, tant qu’elles soient mondees;	And I make of the black and yellow, and the green and others, as they are seen.
et s’on oste ceu que i est a la premiere rasion, c’est boin;	and if it is found in the first reasoning, it is good.
se ceu non, si rencomence a rere le secont jor et lou tier, tant que tu aies tout reis;	if not, then resume to read the second chapter and the tie, as long as you have everything ready.
et saiches que li dent ont mestier de diverses formes d’estrumens por reire, selonc ceu que li oevre lou demoustre, por ceu que li raseur dont on reit defuer les dens ont autres formes que cil dont on reit entre les dens;	and you should know that the teeth have the ability to be in various forms of dislocations, according to what is shown by the demonstration, because the razor whose edges are used to cut between the teeth has other forms than those shown in the dissections.
et cestes formes et autres soient avec toi appareillies.	and these forms and others are with you apparent.
Il covient quant tu cures lou dent de sa dolor que tu tardes dou traire tant com tu pues, car ce ne doit om mie faire;	It is necessary when you treat the tooth for its pain that you delay as long as possible until you can, because it should not be hurried.
car c’est une substance mout haute jusc’a donc c’on n’ait point d’excusation dou raier.	For it is a high-sulfur substance, therefore there is no excuse for not doing so.
Adonques quant li malaides est constrains dou traire, si covient que tu soies certains dou dent doillant.	When the patient is confined to bed, if you are certain that they have pain, then.
Maintes fois desoit li dolor lou malaide, et cuide qu’elle soit ou dent saint, et fait traire le boin dent;	Many times the pain of the patient has been relieved, and make sure it is not too hot, and make it boil the bone.
et toutevoie ne se depart mie li dolor per ceu, tant que li malvais estrais, car nos l’avons ja veut faire a ces sainors;	And nothing will depart from the pain until the bone is boiled, because we have already wanted to do this for these healthier ones.
et quant tu es bien certains dou dent doillant, si covient que tu escorches entor lou dent a tout i. spatumile fort por warder la gencive de toutes pars;	And when you are sure of the pain, if it comes that you scorch all over the bone, then shave it as much as possible and protect the genitals of all parts.
puis le mues a tes dois ou as tenailles subtilz au premier poc et poc, tant qu’il soit bien eslochiés, puis i afferme bien les tenailles;	Then the wound should be sewn to your needs or have small needles inserted at first and then they are firmly fastened. Then the needles should be well anchored.
et soit li chiés dou malaide en ton saint entre tes genous, et lou tien bien si qu’il ne se mueve.	And let the patient's head be held firmly in your holy hands, and hold it well so that it does not move.
Aprés estrai lou dent droitement sens brisier, et s’il ne saut fuer, si prent aucun de ces estrumens et le boute dedens de chescune part legierement, et lou remuef si com tu as fait premier.	After removing the tooth sharply with forceps, and if it does not break, then take none of these hooks and gently pull out from each side, and move it as you have done first.
Et se li dens est perciez et mengiez, si covient que tu l’emplisses de drapelz, lai ou li pertus sont;	And if the wound is perceived and cleaned, then it may be necessary to wrap it with cloths, wherever the holes are.
et si l’estraint subtilment as tenailles, que il ne brise a l’estraindre;	And if the extraction is done gently with needles, so that it does not break the extracted part.
et covient mout saigement ovrer entor la gencive por deschaucier lou dent.	And it is necessary to wisely cover over the thigh to remove the tooth's root.
Et te done bien en warde que tu ne le brises, et en remaigne une partie, et reveigne au malaide par la malice de la racine plus grans dolors de la premiere.	And you should be very careful not to break it, and there will remain a part, and the patient suffers from the malice of the root, greater pains in the first place.
Et te warde que tu ne faices mie ensi com font li ignorant sainor, qui par lor haste et par lor hardiesce brisent aucune fois le charreit, et n’i amenistrent mie ceu que nos avons conteit;	And be careful that you do not harm it in the same way as those who, by their haste and their courage, never break the chariot, and never cause any harm to anyone.
mais font venir aucune fois par l’oquison de ceu grant maladie por les racines que i demorent, ou por lou charreit qu’il brisent, si com nos avons sovent veut;	But no one comes to help once by the cough of this great disease, either by the roots that they do not endure, or by the broken part, as we have often wanted.
et quant li dens est trais, si lavez lou leu de vin ou d’aisil et de seil;	And when the wound is bleeding, if you clean the flesh with wine or vinegar and sail,
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, que sovent avient, si emple lou leu de vitriole broiet;	and if they come out of the blood and enter, which often happens, if you use the flesh of green glass,
et se ceu ne vaut, si le cauterize.	and if it does not heal, if it is cauterized.
Les formes des estrumens, a coi om muet les dens premier, soient a longes pointes et a gros mainches, qu’il ne doublent mie quant tu trairas le dent;	The forms of the stitches, whether they are silent at the first wound, are long and wide and have thick fingers, which do not double when you pull on the tooth;
et ce sont les formes:	1. "For the fire cautery, instruct the patient to let the hairs grow long and even; and if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.
Et soient de gros membres si qu’il ne ploient mie au traire, et soient de fer inde bien fait, et soient dentez por mues tenir.	And they be of large members if they do not break when pulled out, and they be well-made iron, and they be teeth to hold tightly.
de la racine des dens	of the root of the teeth
Quant li racine demoure au traire, si covient que tu mettes sor le leu coton moilliet em burre I jor ou II, tant que li leus soit amolis, pues i boute les tenailles qui sont apelees «algefri», de coi li chiés semblet bec de soigne;	When the root of the tooth is exposed to the cheek, if you can manage to put it in the cheek butter of the inner side of the jaw for one or two hours, until it is smooth, then the needles that are called "algefri" will be drawn out, and the head of the shoulder will look well.
et soient dedens faites ausi com une lime et c’est li forme:	and they are made in the same way as a lime and it is in this form.
Et se les racines ne vuellent issir a tout ces tenailles, si covient que tu descuevre la char tot entor la racine, et i met l’estrument qui est apelez «althali», c’est a savoir palainche, de coi ci est li forme:	And if the roots do not wish to come out through all these pricks, then it comes that you dig out the whole of the root, and put in the instrument called "althali", which is a type of tweezer, and its form is like this:
Et soit fors et gros si qu’il ne brise mie, et se li racine saut par ceu, c’est boin;	And if it is too thin and large if it does not break easily, and if the root jumps from this, it is good.
se ceu non, si t’aide de toz les estrumens, de coi les formes vienent ci aprés:	If this does not work, if you use all the means, and if the forms come after this:
Et si s’aide on de cest estrument qui ait II rains, de coi ci est li forme:	And if you help with this instrument that has two prongs, its form is like this:
et d’autres ferremens qui sont devant en la rasion des dens, et de cest estrument qui semble unes grans tenailles, dont ci est li forme:	And of other forceps that are before in the reason of the teeth, and this instrument which seems like large thorns, its form is like this:
Et soit cist estrumens fors qu’il ne puisse brisier, et saiches que mout d’estrumens de dens sont;	And let it be known that it is not possible to break it, and scissors are needed with sharp teeth.
et ausi d’autres estrumens, qui ne sont mie contez;	and also other bones, which are not so strong.
et li saiges maistres subtilz trueve par soi meisme son estrument, selonc ceu que ses ovraiges et li maladie li demoustre, car il i a de teilz maladies ou li ancien n’enseignerent point d’estrument por la diversiteit d’au;s et s’om brise point dou charreit ou des autres os, ou il porrit, si i cerche as estrumens qu’il i covient, que je t’ai dit, et t’aide des gestes, de coi ci est li forme:	and the masters most skilled use their own instruments, according to what their experience and the disease demonstrate, because they have different teachings on the various instruments, and do not break any chariot or other bones, or cut through them, if they seek the bones that I have said, and I will help you with gestures, as follows:
Et soient gros et bien tenant por tenir l’os, qu’il n’eschaipe, mais le puisse tenir et oster;	And let them be thick and well-holding to hold the bone, so it does not slip, but can hold and grasp.
et puis restoure lou leu de medicines convenant a ceu, et s’il ait en l’os porriture, et elle est petite, si la reis a tout cest estrument:	Then restore the patient to the appropriate medicine, and if there is inflammation in the bone, and it is small, then use all of this instrument.
Quant li dent apperent ne mie selonc lou cors natureil, et li forme est laide, et meismement en femmes puceles, si covient que tu saiches se li dens est neis aprés lou dent, et n’est mie en droit leu, et on ne lou puet soier ne limer:	When the tooth appears to not fit according to the natural body, and its form is misshapen, and at the same time in women with pubic hair, if it comes that you must remove the tooth after the dent, and it is not true lest the bone, and one cannot soothe or embrace it:
adonques lou raie;	Therefore, I will reset the dislocation.
et s’il est aers avec lou dent, si prent cest estrument dont ci est li forme, et est semblans a I petit bec, et soit de fer inde agut en som:	And if it is with the tooth, then take this instrument whose form is like this small tooth, and make it of hard steel:
Et lou cope poc et poc em mains jors por la duresce dou dent, et por ceu que tu ne mueves les autres, et s’il est apparans c’on le puisse limer, si lou lime d’une teil lime com ci est li forme:	And the force is little by little with the hands years due to the hardness of the tooth, and because you do not move the others, and if it appears that it can be limed, then the liming of a part of the liming as shown here is the form:
et est ausi com li lime de coi on fait les aguilles;	and it will be as the gnat's leg that we make:
et en lime lou dent poc et poc em mains jors legierement, si qu’il ne se mueve tant qu’il chiece;	and with the gnat's leg, very lightly and often in the hands, so it does not move until it chickens:
puis la plaine en la fin a tout aucun raseur, et se li dens est trop trenchans et il blece la lengue, si covient limer l’aspreteit tant qu’il soit igalz, si qu’il ne blece la lengue ne ne corrompe la parole.	Then the smoothness at the end for all raspers, and if the teeth are too sharp and they bite the tongue, then it is necessary to limn the astringent so that it is even, so that it does not bite the tongue or corrupt the speech.
quant li dent lochent	2. When the beak is dislocated.
Quant li dent devant lochent, ou par percussion ou par cheoir, et li malaides ne puet presser sus ceu qu’il menjue qu’il ne chient, et tu les as curez de medicines restrignans, et ceu ne vaut;	When the tooth in front of the gum, or by percussion or by cheek, and the patient cannot press on it because it hurts, and you cure them with restrictive medicines, and this is not effective.
si les covient restraindre d’un fil d’or, car li filz d’argent devient vert et porrit, mais li ors ne se mue onques;	If the patients are restrained with a gold thread, because the silver threads turn green and slippery, but the gold does not move.
et soit li filz moiens ne trop gros ne trop menus, selonc la quantiteit de l’espaice entre les dens;	And that the silver threads are neither too thick nor too thin, according to the space between the teeth.
et se tu vues adrecier les dens, si pren lou fil et lou boute double entre les II dens sains, puis met les chiés entre les dens meus, s’il en i a I ou plusors, tant que tu veignes saigement jusc’au dent sain d’autre part;	And if you see the teeth erupting, then take the thread and double it between the two healthy teeth, then place the heads between the diseased teeth, as long as you see signs of growth in the healthy tooth on the other side.
puis rencomence la coverture jusc’a la partie ou tu encomensas, et estrains ta main subtilment et saigement, tant qu’il ne se mueve point;	Then the covering resumes just where you left off, and gently and wisely draw your hand subtly, so that it does not move.
et soit ta lieeure a la racine dou dent si qu’il ne puist eschaper.	and make sure your line is at the root of the tooth so that it does not escape.
Puis cope les chiés dou fil a unes tenailles, et les assemble, et les repont entre le dent sain, et le met ensi qu’il ne blece la lengue;	Then secure the heads of the wires with nails, and assemble them, and place them between the healthy tooth and the tooth to be straightened, and make sure it does not damage the tongue.
et puis le laisse ensi estroit tant com il puet demorer, et s’il deslie, ou li filz ront, si l’estraint d’un autre fil;	And then leave it until it is as narrow as possible, and if it does not hold, or the wires break, then tighten another wire.
si demorrait et servira ensi tout son tens, et c’est li forme des dens et li figure de l’adrecement des II dens sains, et des II meus, si com tu vois:	If it delays and serves as intended, and this is the form of the teeth and the shape of the incisor of the two healthy teeth and the two canines, just as you see:
Et quant li dent chiet, si lou remet on en son leu, de fres en fres, si com nos avons dit;	And when the tooth is lost, if it is replaced in its socket, tightly, as we have said:
et ne s’en entremette mie qui n’est saiges et soffrans, et aucune fois fait on la forme d’un dent d’os de vaiche, et lou met on au leu ou li defaute est, et l’estraint on si com nos avons dit, et demore et sert ensi lonc tens.	and does not become loose if it is not sharp and sharp, and never takes the form of a bone tooth of a sheep, and it is placed in its socket or where the defect is, and it is tightened as we have said, and stays there, and serves as intended:
de coper lou liien de la lengue	Of the copper wire of the tongue
Aucune fois est cist liiens qui vient desoz la lengue ou naturez, que on naist ensi;	Never has been found a tooth that comes out of the tongue or nature, that has not been made:
ou par accident de plaie soudee;	If by chance there is a deep wound.
et li ovraiges est telz que tu oevre la bouche dou malaide, et ait sa teste en ton sain, et li lieve la lengue;	And the operation is such that you open the patient's mouth with the scalpel, and the handle remains in your hand, and you hold the tongue.
puis cope lou liien nervous dou large, tant que li lengue soit desloie de son tenement, et se il i a duresce ou nout, et c’est de soudement de plaie, si i boute l’uncine et cope dou large celui liement;	Then cut the nerve as wide as possible, until the tongue is dislodged from its place, and if it snaps or tears, and that is a sign of pain, then cut the other side equally.
et garde que li fendure ne soit mie trop em parfont, por l’artere qui est desoz;	And make sure the blade does not go too deep, for the artery is dry.
et quant tu as fait, si leve le leu d’aigue rose et d’aisil, ou d’aigue froide, puis met desoz la lengue une tente de lin;	And when you are done, if the lip is red and sore, or cold, then place the tongue in a tent of linen.
et la teigne li malaides chescune nuit, que li leus ne puisse soder.	and the patient's skin is scraped every night, which cannot be soothed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si met sor le leu vitriole broiet;	And if the blood flow comes, then put on the leu with vitrol and broiled wheat.
et se li sans te vaint, si le cauterize au cautere lentiginout, qui est boin a ceu;	And if it is not burned, then cauterize at the slow cautery, which is good for this.
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez,	Then the treatment of another cure until it is healthy.
et se tu lou vois de fusse color ou noir ou dur, si que li malaides ne lou sent, si n’i touchier point, car c’est chancre;	And if you see that the skin has turned red or black or hard, and the patient does not feel it, if it is not touched, because it is gall.
et s’il est declinans a blenchor, et il i a moistor, si i giete l’oncine, et lou fent d’un spatumile subtil, et lou delivre d’une part et d’autre;	And if it declines to blenchor, and it is moist, if it gushes blood, and the skin is made with a subtle sponge, and the discharge is from both sides;
et se li sans te vaint a ton ovraige, si met sus vitriole broiet tant qu’il soit estainchiez, puis revien a ton ovraige tant que tu traies tout fuer;	and if you do not want to cause pain in your work, then use vitrol on the wounds as soon as they are cleaned, and return to your work as soon as you have finished everything.
puis leve lou leu d’aisil et de seil, et le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then lift the shoulder joint and the tendon, and treat other wounds as soon as they are healed.
des apostemes de la gorge	gums of the throat
Aucune fois vient dedens la gorge boces qui sont apelees «godath», et les apele on proprement les II amandres, et quant tu les cures, si com nos avons dit en la division, et elles ne sont sanees, si pren garde:	No time comes when the gums called "godath" come out, and they are properly called the second teeth. When you treat them, as we have said in the division, and if they are not healed, keep a close watch on them.
se c’est apostemes dur de petit sens et de fusse color, si ne lou touchier mie de fer.	If it is an abscess of hard consistency and small size, and of a pale color, and not touched with iron.
Et s’il est rouges et li racine est grosse, si ne lou touchier mie de fer, ausi por lou decorrement de sanc;	And if it is red and the root is large, and it is not touched with iron at all, then for the dislocation of the shoulder.
mais lou laisse tant qu’il soit meur, et adonques tu lou partiras, ou il rompirait par soi;	but it does not leave until it is dead, and therefore it will depart, or it will break on its own.
et s’il est de blainche color reont, et li racine est subtilz, si aies apareilliet l’estrument por coper, mais regarde premierement se li apostemes chalz repose et est apaisiez.	And if it is of a greenish color and the root is small, and you have prepared the instrument with copper, but first check if the abscess is closed and calmed.
Adonques fai seoir lou malaide devant lou soleil, et ses chiés soit en ton sain, et li oevre la bouche et lou preigne li serjans entre ses mains, et presse la lengue desoz a tout l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme;	Then make the patient lie down in the sun, and their head should be in your hands, and they open their mouth and swallow the salve between their hands, and press the tongue evenly all over the instrument, and so is the form.
et soit d’argent ou d’arain subtil ausi com uns coutelz:	and let it be of silver or of gold as some coins:
Cant tu presses la lengue a tout cest estrument, et tu vois l’aposteme, si pren l’oncine et lou fiche en l’amandre, et la trai fuer au desus plus que tu pues;	Can you press the tongue against all this instrument, and see the aposteme, if you take the oncid and the leaf in the amber, and the thread will be further than you think.
et trai aucune chose des toiles avec, puis la cope a l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme, que semble unes forces;	and take no thing with the spots, then lay the cape on the instrument, and see the form which seems some force.
et toutevoie li chief sont corbé, et l’un endroit l’autre, et sont molt agut, et est fait de fer inde ou d’andainne:	and the head is all wrinkled, and one place to another, and are very sharp, and is made of iron or steel.
Et se tu n’as cest estrument present, si lou cope as tenailles, de coi ci est li forme:	And if you do not have this instrument present, if it is sharp, then the form is like this:
Et soit trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part nom;	And be cutting from one part and another part name.
et quant tu as copeit l’une des amandres, si cope l’autre selonc cele meisme maniere, et aprés l’incision gargarize li malaides aigue chaude, et aigue et aisil, et se decorremens de sanc avient, si gargarize li malaides aigue, ou escorces de pomes grenates soient cuites, ou fuelles de mirte, et semblans choses, tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	When you have grasped one of the mandrills, if you grasp the other in the same manner, and after making an incision, heat the sharp, hot barbers' knife, and make it sizzle and sputter, and if the blood comes out, or if burns from pomegranate peels are cooked, or if blisters from mirte leaves are caused, and similar things, as long as they are not extinguished.
puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then the cure is until it is healthy.
et aucune fois naissent en la gorge autres apostemes que les II amandres, si les cope donques ensi com les II amandres igament.	And never do any other abscesses appear in the throat than the two mandrills, if they are cut out exactly like the two mandrills.
Et je medicinai une femme d’un aposteme que li estoit neis dedens la gorge, c’est a savoir I aposteme de petit sens;	And I treated a woman with an abscess that it was not dense in the throat, which means it is of little sensation.
et avoit jai bien pres close toute la gorge, si que li femme ne pooit expirer por le conduit qui estoit estoupez, et ne pooit ne mengier ne boivre, et fust morte s’elle demorast ensi I jor ou II.	and had indeed closed most of the throat, so that the woman could not breathe through the clogged pipe, and could not eat or drink, and died if she delayed for one or two days.
Et li apostemes estoit jai si montez qu’il avoit fuer mis II rains par les II pertuis dou neis.	And the abscess was so large that it had been opened twice by the two holes.
Je hastai donques tantost, et fichai en l’un I oncine, puis lou traï fuers, et en traï grant porcion de bowe;	I then made a deep incision, and opened the abscess, and took out a large portion of the bowel.
puis refis autreteil en l’autre pertus dou neis, et li ovrai la bouche et li pressai la lengue;	and then removed another part from another puncture, and opened the mouth and pressed on the tongue.
aprés fichai l’oncine en ces apostemes, et en copai une partie, et n’en issit fuers que un poc de sanc;	After the onion is cut into these slices, and a piece is taken out, it will only yield a drop of blood.
et ensi fut destoupez li conduis de la gorge la femme, et comensa maintenant a boivre aigue et puis vin, et ne cessai de taillier de cel aposteme par lonc tens;	And then the woman's leader was cut off, and she began to drink water and then wine, and did not stop cutting that slice.
et li apostemes recroissoit adés, et remplissoit lou leu que je avoie vuidiet, tant qu’il refut mout gros;	And the slice was dislocated further and filled the joint that I had emptied, so it refused to move.
adonques je l’engignai et lou cauterizai dedens la gorge:	Therefore, I engined and cauterized the joint from the girl's mouth.
ensi demora sens croistre;	It did not take long to heal.
et me partis de ces parties, et ne soi que Deus fist de li aprés moi.	And I left these parts, and I was only able to do what God willed after me.
de l’uve	Of the urethra
Quant reume dessent a l’uve, et elle est enflee et elle est longe, si est apelee «perpendiculaire»;	When the urine reaches the urethra, it is thin and long, and is called "perpendicular".
et s’elle est desoz grosse et reonde, si est apelee «uve».	and if it becomes too large and round, it is called the "urethra".
Quant elle est curee si com nos avons dit en la division, et li cure ne profite mie, et tu vois que li chaus apostemes est apaisiez, et elle est subtilz, si covient que tu la copes;	When it is treated as we have said in the division, and the treatment does not benefit, and you see that the inflammation has subsided, and it is softened, then you can touch it;
et celle qui est reonde assemblee et n’est mie longe;	and the one that is rounded and not long.
et elle est sanguine ou de fusse color ou noire, si covient que tu eschues l’incision de li.	and if it is bloody or of a purple or black color, then you should evacuate the incision from it.
Car il i a grant peril sus lou malaide.	For it poses great danger to the patient.
Il covient donques, quant tu la vois, selonc la maniere que j’ai dit, de sa blenchor et de sa longesce, que tu faices seoir le malaide devant lou soleil, et li presse la lengue a l’estrument dont nos avons fait la remembrance ci devant;	It is therefore necessary, as you see, according to the method I have described, of the patient's gallbladder and length, that you place the assistant in front of the sun, and press the tongue on the instrument we have mentioned before.
puis fiche l’oncine en l’uve, et la trai desoz, et la cope a I des II estrumens que j’ai dit en l’incision des II amandres.	Then, the onion is cut in the urethra, and the tail is removed, and the copper is placed in the two incisions that I mentioned in the incision of the two hamstrings.
Et covient que tu ne coper mie fuer que la superfluiteit qui est outre le termine natureil;	And it is necessary that you do not cut too much, only the excess that is over the natural end.
car se tu en copes plus, si grieves a la voix, et a la parolle;	For if you cut more, you will hurt your voice and speech.
et aprés l’incision, use de ceu que nos avons dit en l’incision des II amandres, et le cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And after the incision, use what we have said in the incision of two thumbs, and treat as long as it is healthy.
Et se li malaides a paor dou coper, si covient que tu i use d’engien a la cauterization de li sens paor.	If the patient has a high fever, then it is necessary that you use an engine for the cauterization of the affected part.
Et li maniere dou cautere si est aigue ague.	And the manner of cauterization is to make it hot and dry.
Et est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, et puis li presse la lengue a l’estrument que nos avons dit ou chapistre de cautere, et confis avec aigue vive chaus, si qu’elle ne soit mie trop espesse ne trop clere;	And the surgeon places the head in your mouth, and then presses the tongue on the instrument we have said in the chapter of cauterization, and confuses with live coal, if it is not too thick or too clear.
et en emple le chevement de cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme:	and by using this instrument, the form is:
Et ait ou chief une cheveure ou om met la medecine, si com li chevemens d’une cuillier, et met l’estrument a tout la medicine sus l’uve;	And if the head has a hair or puts medicine, like the hair of a mouse, and places the instrument in all the medicine on the eye;
et li malaides soit gisans sus son costeit, si que li salive et li muscillaige corre de sa bouche de la medicine dedens, si qu’ele ne dessende a la gorge, et lou blece;	When the patient's shoulder is dislocated, if it causes the saliva to flow and the mucous to drip from the mouth due to the medicine, if it does not descend to the chin and the throat.
puis tien ta main a tout la medicine et la presse sus l’uve, la quantiteit de la moitiet d’une houre, tant que tu la vois nercie et li mordications de la medicine soit apaisie;	Then hold your hand on all the medicine and press on the vein, as long as you see it is red and the sting of the medicine is calmed.
et se tu vues, pren coton et l’envoloupe sus aucun estrument, et moille lou coton en la medicine, et boute l’estrument a tout le couton en la cainne desus, tant que li coton s’aerde sus l’uve;	And if you see, take cotton and wrap it around no instrument, and moisten the cotton with the medicine, and tie the instrument all around the cotton in the vein, as long as the cotton is damp around the vein.
et fai ceu sovent, tant que li cauteres soit parfais, puis la laisse elle seche, et chiet aprés IIII jors ou V.	and do this until it is perfect, then leave it to dry, and it will be ready after four or five days.
Et se tu as mestier de rencomencier lou cautere de la medicine, si le rencomence, et aprés le cautere l’essue entor l’uve, de couton embut em burre, et mundifie ceu qui est entor de la medicine;	And if you have experience in restarting the fire cautery of medicine, if it restarts, and after the cautery cleanse the excrement around the urethra, wrap it with linen, and clean what is outside of the medicine.
et soit arosez d’aigue froide, et soit curez de gargarismes tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you have a fever of cold, and treat it with gargles as long as it is healthy.
Ceste cure est plus save de l’incision, ne que li cautere;	This remedy is safer than the incision, only the cautery.
s’elle est curee de fumigation selonc ceste maniere, pren calament et ysope et origanum et rue et camomille et avronne et semblans herbes, et les assemble toutes ou aucunes d’eles en I pot, et i met aisil, et fai bullir;	If it is treated with fumigation according to this method, take a lamp, oil, oregano, rosemary, chamomile, and mint, and assemble all or none of them in one pot, and put in ashes, and boil.
et li potz soit bien gluez de fort terre, et enmi le pot ait I estrument cheveit selonc ceste maniere:	And it may be well glued with strong earth, and it should have an instrument made according to this manner:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, et soit li uns des chiés boutez en la bouche dou malaide tant que li vapor monte a l’uve par la caine, tant que li uve soit mortifie;	And it should be of silver or gold, and the ends should be placed in the patient's mouth as much as possible until the vapor rises through the canal, as long as the canal is saturated;
aprés lou rencomence sovent, tant que li uve seche, et garde que tu ne faices ceu au comencement de l’avenement de l’aposteme chaut, car plusors choses i avienent;	after the wound has healed, as long as the canal is dry, and make sure you do not do this at the beginning of the onset of the abscess, because many things may come;
et ne faire mie ceu fuer que a la declination d’aposteme chaut.	and only do this if it is necessary for the onset of the abscess.
Et se cist estrument n’est presens, si pren une caine et met dedens lou chief une craiffe d’uef, si que li bouche au malaide n’ait mie trop chaut;	If this instrument is not present, then take a needle and make a hole in the cheek with it, if the mouth of the patient has not been too much bitten.
car li craiffe d’uef ne lait mie la vapor grever la bouche, et c’est bone cure ensamble salut.	For the needle's hole does not cause pain in the mouth, and it is a good cure together with the previous one.
Maintes fois s’aert a la gorge os ou espinee de poisson, ou aucune chose;	Many times have I seen bones protrude from the throat or fish spines, or nothing at all.
si covient donc que tu traies ceu que tu pues veoir, et li presse la lengue au soleil a tout l’estrument, si que tu voies mues la chose;	Therefore, if you must see what you see, and press the tongue against the sun with all the instruments, so that you can see the thing.
et ceu que ne t’apert mie et est reponus en la gorge, covient que tu faices vomir le malaide ainsois que li viande soit cuite en l’estomac;	And if it does not open at all and is stuck in the throat, then you must make the patient vomit unless the meat is cooked in the stomach.
par aventure si istra li chose aerse par le vomissement;	By chance, if the thing is achieved through vomiting;
ou li malaides englutisse une piece d’esponge, ou une piece de navel, ou une racine de laitue, ou I morceil de pain sec;	or the patient swallows a piece of sponge, or a piece of navel, or a root of millet, or a piece of dry bread;
et lie a l’esponge I fil, et puis la transglutisse;	and it attaches to the sponge thread, and then glues together;
et quant elle venra au leu, si s’aerdra, et puis trairas fuer;	and when it reaches the shoulder, if it sticks, and then it will be torn off;
et s’elle ne vient fuer de ceu que nos avons dit, si pren I estrument de plonc selonc ceste forme:	and if it does not come off from this, if we use the instrument of pulling according to this form:
Et soit li estrumens corbés au chief si qu’il puist plus legierement entrer en la gorge, et ait le chief en haut leveit;	And let the instruments be corbes at the head if it can more lightly enter the mouth, and have the head lifted up;
et warde que tu ne touchier l’epiglote, que li tous ne li viegne, ne ne bouter mie l’os dedens;	And if you do not touch the epiphysis, all will not live, and will not burden the bones too much.
et mues vaut que li malaides i boute l’estrument, por ceu qu’il seit mues ou li chose est aerse;	And it is better that the patient uses the instrument, because it is needed or the thing is there.
si la boute aval, ou il la traie fuer a tout l’estrument igalment, tant qu’elle soit fuer.	If the use is good, or he takes it further all the instrument correctly, as far as it goes.
de la sansue de la gorge	of the throat's loose skin
Aucune fois est medicinee li sansue, si com j’ai dit en la division, par la cure de medicines;	No time is wasted in medicine, if I have said it in the division, by the treatment of medicines.
et quant ceu ne profite mie, adonques regarde en la gorge dou malaide au soleil, puis que tu li presses la lengue a l’estrument que je t’ai dit.	And when it does not profit anything, then look in the eye of the patient towards the sun, then press the tongue to the instrument I have given you.
Et se tu vois la sansue, si la trai a tout I petit uncine, ou as tenailles subtilz que valent a ceu.	If you see the shoulder, if the bone is all in one piece, or if it has thin hairs that are worth nothing in this.
Et se ceu ne vaut, si pren une caine chevee, et la boute en la gorge dou malaide, puis boute ou chevement de la caine I fer chaut, et fai ce sovent.	And if it is not worth anything, then take a hair from the head of a woman, and tie it around the neck of the patient, and then pull or cut off the hair, and do this often.
Et se teigne li malaides d’aigue toute jor.	And the patient's scalp is sweating all the time.
puis pren plein I voirre d’aigue froide, et oevre la bouche, et la giete ens sens englutir, et la mueve a sa main sovent;	Then fill your mouth with cold water, and feel the saliva, and it often moves to your hand.
et si tost com li sansue sent l’aigue, si chiet.	And if the tongue feels the cold water, then stop.
Et s’elle ne chiet si com nos avons dit, si subfumige lou malaide d’asefetide, a l’estrument que j’ai dit en la fumigation de l’uve;	And if it does not stop when we have said, and if the helper smokes asafetida on the instrument we mentioned in the irrigation of the eye;
fai ceu maintes fois, car elle cherra sens targier.	Do this many times, because it feels like it is burning.
Et li maniere de la fumigation si est que tu preignes I pot ou il ait charbons vis, et soit li pos covert d’un coverseil perciet en mileu, et en celui pertus soit li chiés de l’estrument;	And the manner of the irrigation is if you preheat it or if there are charcoal bits, and it should be covered with a covering perch in the environment, and in the other end it should be the head of the instrument.
puis i giete ta fumigation, et li malaides mette lou chief de la cainne en sa bouche, et cloie la bouche, si que li fumee n’en isse mie, mais viegne jusc’a la sansue;	Then you gargle with the fumigation, and the patient places the head of the chain in their mouth, closes their mouth so that the smoke does not enter, but it comes out through the nose.
et la sansue cherra maintenant, et s’elle ne chiet, si rencomence la fumigation par maintes fois;	And now the patient will sneeze, and if it happens again several times, the fumigation is repeated.
et soffre li malaides soif, et menjuce choses salees et als, et ne boive point d’aigue;	And the patient suffers from thirst, and drinks salty and bitter things, and does not drink water.
et adonques li iert mestier qu’elle isse fuer par cest governement.	And therefore, the patient endures this treatment as ordered.
Et li forme de l’estrument a coi on trait la sansue, si est, quant on la puet veoir, semblans a tenailles corbés por mues entrer en la gorge;	And the form of the instrument used to treat the nose, if it is, when it can be seen, resembles combs that may enter the throat.
et ait semblance au bec de soigne, et i ait asperiteit de lime, si que ceu qu’elle prent, elle ne puet lassier;	and it seems like the beak of a surgeon, and it has sharpness like lime, so that whatever it takes, it cannot hold on.
et vez ci la forme:	and then comes the shape:
li chapistres des apostemes	The chapters of the sutures
Mout de semblances d’aposteme sont, selonc ceu que li remembrance vient ci aprés d’un et d’autre en cest livre, et sont diver en perforation et en taille;	The forms of apothegms are, according to what the remembrance comes after another in this book, and they are different in piercing and size.
et c’est en II manieres dont l’une est en sa semblance meisme, et de ceu qu’il tient moistor.	and it is in two ways that one is itself in its appearance, and because it has moisture.
Et li seconde maniere si est por les leus ou il sont au cors.	And the second way is if the limbs are lying down or at rest.
car li apostemes dou chief est autres que cil dou fondement, et li apostemes dou leu charnut est autres que cil qui vient en jointures, et chescuns ait son jugement en l’uevre.	For the head of the chief is different from that of the foundation, and the head of the lower limb is different from those that come in joints, and each has its own judgment in the work.
Et si a apostemes c’on ne doit mie percier, tant que li bowe est meure selonc son acomplissement;	And if in apothegms one does not have to cut deeply, as long as the bow is dead according to its completion.
et si a de telz qu’il covient percier quant il sont crut, et ne meurent mie selonc lor acomplissement, si com aposteme qui sont delez jointures.	If there are those who think they can discern when they should die, and do not die according to their completion, as amputations that are defective joints.
Car quant apostemes vient delez jointures, et on le laisse tant qu’il est porris entor, par aventure si sont corrumput li liien et li nerf de la jointure, par coi ce est cause de contraction en celui membre.	For when the head comes from difficult joints, and it is left as long as it is dry, by chance if the ligament and nerve of the joint are corrupted, because this is due to contraction in that member.
Ou li aposteme est delez lou membre principel, et se tu tardes la perforation tant qu’il soit meurez, si nuira au membre principeil;	If the amputation is defective, it is due to the principal limb, and if you delay the incision until the limb is dead, it will harm the principal limb.
ou il est delez lou fondement, si le perce on ainsois qu’il soit meurs;	If the foundation is defective, if the incision is not made when the limb is dead, it will harm the foundation.
et ne covient mie que tu perces aposteme crut sens digestion acomplie, fuers que celui qui est delez lou fondement, qu’il ne porrisse em parfont, et soit alongiez dedens, et i viegne fistule;	And it is only necessary to make the amputation when the limb is dead, as if the foundation is defective, it will not be able to pass through, and the wound will be long, and a fistula will form.
et ne puisse saner en grant termine.	and cannot be cured in a great amount of time.
Et covient que tu saiches l’oure de la perforation de l’aposteme qui est meur selonc l’acomplissement, et c’est quant li dolor est apaisie, et li departemens de la fievre, et l’amenuisement de la dolor et de la roujor, et dou debatement et de l’aguisement dou chief de l’aposteme, et les autres signes;	And it is necessary that you cut off the ear of the aposteme wound which bleeds according to the completion, and it is when the pain is eased, and the fever subsides, and the relief of pain and bruising, and the debate and aguishness of the aposteme, and the other signs.
et covient que tu faices seoir la perforation ou plus dependant leu de l’aposteme, et la ou il apert mues;	And it is necessary that you cut off the hole of the aposteme wound which is more dependent on the ear, and where it has opened.
et soit li perforation dou lonc dou cors, et se li apostemes est as mains ou as piez, ou en jointures et au ners et as arteres, et en toz leus igalz ou il n’a point de ploieure.	And if the hole of the aposteme wound is long and deep, and it opens with the hands or fingers, or in the joints and arteries, and in all of them equally or not, without any bleeding.
En ces que ploient, par selonc celui membre.	In those that are pricked, according to the pain of the member.
Et quant apostemes est en leu charnut, si vaut mues que tu laisses la perforation tant qu’il soit confermez en digestion acomplie, si com nos avons dit.	And when an abscess is formed in the member, if it is painful, then you should leave the puncture until it is confirmed to be well digested, as we have said.
Car se tu lou perces devant ceu, si iert alongiez li cors dou venim de lui, et est plains de mout d’ordure;	If you do not follow this instruction, I will have to stop translating the text.
et par aventure endurcissent les levres et li parfondetez de lui.	and by chance they harden the lips and make them appear more beautiful.
Et si a aucun aposteme que sont perciet selonc le large dou cors, selonc ceu que li membres en ait mestier.	And if there is no abscess that is felt according to the pain of the member, then it should be left according to the size of the blood.
Et covient que tu amenistres em petis apostemes, petis pertus;	And you must cut out small abscesses, small pustules.
et en grans apostemes, grans pertus, et maintes fendures selonc la semblance de la grandor de l’aposteme;	and in large abscesses, large pustules, and multiple incisions according to the size of the abscess.
et si a de tels apostemes ou il covient chever lou keur, et coper;	And if there are such abscesses or it is necessary to cut out the head, and close it.
quant il est jai devenus ausi com I drapelz, et est amortis, si covient faire ausi com on fait as bubes:	When I have become so old as I am now, and I am weary, then it is necessary to do it in the same way as they make bubbles.
et si a de telz que sont fendut en III angles, et si a de telz dont on cope ausi com la fuelle de mirte, si com apostemes des angres;	If it is of those that are cut at three angles, and if it is of those that are cut like the thorn of a mirror, as well as those that are cut like the thumbs.
et si a de telz ou on fait une reonde taille, et autres tailles et semblant copeure.	If it is of those that are cut into a specific size, and other sizes and appearances are coped with.
Cil qui n’ont point de chief, si com aposteme souef superficial, il covient que tu lou perces plainnement;	Those who have no head, if it is like a superficial wound, you must cut it through gradually.
et covient quant li apostemes est gros, et il a coillit grant bowe, et tu lou perces, si ne traire mie toute la bowe en celle houre, mais en trai une partie;	And when the wound is large, and it has a great bowel, and you cut it, if you do not dig out all of the bowel in that hour, but dig out a part.
puis estoupe l’aposteme jusc’a l’autre jor, puis en trai aucune chose derechief;	Then comes the aposteme (stitch) to the other side, then no right thing is done.
fai ceu par maintes fois de greit en greit, tant que li bowe isse toute;	Do this many times with great care, until the bowel is all.
meismement se li malaides est de foible vertut, ou femme portans, ou petis enfes, ou viez hons decrepites.	Meanwhile, if the patient is of weak constitution, or a woman carrying, or pregnant women, or old men.
Car li esperis tressaut aucune fois avec l’issue de la bowe, que par aventure muert li malaides, et tu ne t’en persois.	For the expectoration there is no time with the issue of the bowel, that by chance dies the patient, and you do not blame yourself.
Eschuez donques cest chapistre par grant cautele, et quant tu as perciet ton aposteme, si essue la plaie, et regarde se li plaie de l’aposteme est petite;	Avoid this chapter with great caution, and when you have found your stitch, if the wound is bleeding, look at whether the wound of the suture is small.
et se c’est une tailleure plainne, si amenistre tentes de lin ou de viez coton;	And if it is a flat measuring, then use threads of linen or cotton.
et se c’est uns grans apostemes, et il i a mout de pertus, si covient que tu boutes en chescun une tente si qu’ele viegne l’une contre l’autre;	If it is many abscesses, and there is fever, then it comes that you make a tent in each one so that they do not fight against each other.
et se tu as copeit en l’aposteme une partie dou cuir, et tu l’as cheveit entor, si covient que tu l’emplisses de viel couton ou de rasure de dras de lin sens moistor, et le lie jusc’au tier jor;	If you have opened an abscess partly in leather, and it is healed, then it comes that you fill it with fine cloth or rough linen, and the limb will be better;
puis l’oste, et le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then the bone, and the treatment of ointment as long as it is healthy.
Et se decorremens de sanc avient a ton ovraige, si amenistre aigue froide et aisil, et moille I drapeil, et met sor le leu decorrant par maintes fois.	And if the evacuation of blood comes to your vein, if it is cold and wet, and the arm hangs down, and you gently put it on the bed many times.
Et se li decorremens de sanc persevere, se i amenistre governement et cure, et les poudres que j’ai dit em mains leus en cest livre, et se c’est ou tens d’iver, et li leus ou li apostemes est est mout nervous, si couvient que tu mettes sus tentes et drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile chaut;	And if the patient has lost much blood, and there is no relief, and the government and treatment are not effective, and the powders that I have said in my hands in this book, and if there is pain, and the abscess is nervous, then it comes that you make tents and fold the softened cloth in wine and olive oil;
et se c’est en esteit, et li leus est charnus, si covient que tu mes sus drapelz moilliez en aigue et en oile, ou en vin et en oile froit, jusc’au tier jor, si com nos avons dit;	If this is the case, and the leus is charnus, then it comes to pass that you must moisten your cloths in cold water and oil, or in wine and oil vinegar, just as we have said.
et puis deslie l’aposteme et l’essue et le cure, si com il covient, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And then remove the abscess and pus, if it comes to pass, as soon as it is healthy.
Et ceu covient il conoistre universement en cures des apostemes:	And it comes to pass that you understand completely in the treatment of abscesses:
or vos ai dit coment on doit aler avant as cures des apostemes, et vez ci le chapistre.	Or do I say what you must go before the treatment of abscesses and then this chapter?
des soros	of sore
Ou keur dou chief vienent petis apostemes, et sont manieres de nous que sont en toiles, ausi com li josier d’une geline, et mout en i a de semblances.	When the head of the shoulder comes to many abscesses, and they are like ours, as if the thread of a grapevine, and there are some that seem like this.
Il en i a de gras et de telz ou il a moistor ausi com poulz;	It is either too fat or too wet, or both like pouls.
et si a de telz qui sont dur et pierous au taillier, et n’i a point de doutance se li artere n’i fait contraire.	And if there are those who are hard and rough to cut, and there is no doubt that the patient will not bleed, then it does not matter.
Et li ovraiges de la taille si est que tu esprueve a tout I estrument qui est apelez «entromissoire», de coi li forme vient ci aprés, quel chose il contient.	And the measurements of the size if it is that you prove to all the instruments that are called "entromising," by which form comes after, what thing it contains.
Car s’il contient moistor, si lou fent par desus dou lonc.	For if it contains moisture, they make it longer by adding more.
Et quant li moistor est vuidie, si escorche sens rien laissier la peil qui contient celle moistor, car il revient adés quant on i laisse rien;	And when the moisture is seen, then shave off the hair that contains the moisture, because it will return to its original position as soon as it is left alone.
puis plonge coton en oignement egiptien, s’il est presens;	Then dip cotton in Egyptian ointment, if it is present.
se ceu non, en aigue et en seil, et en emple la plaie, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	if not, use vinegar and linen, and apply the wound, and leave it until the next day.
et ceu corront ceu qui est demorez dou nit.	and keep the part that is more painful at night.
Et pues rencomence lou coton, si com devant, le second jor, et lou tier, tant que tu saiches bien qu’il ne demoure point dou nit;	And then resume the thread, as before, the second day, and the pain, so long as you feel well but it does not last all night.
puis cure la plaie d’oignement a ceu convenauble, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the wound with ointment according to the appropriate method, as long as it is healthy.
Et se li apostemes tient I nout gras, si le cope selonc ceste forme, dou lonc;	And if the abscess holds fat, and the grip is according to this form, then it will be long.
et i giete tes oncines, et l’escorche de toutes pars, et met toute ta cure de traire fuer la cotte ou il gist;	And you gnaw your bones, and scrape off all parts, and use all your care to draw out the pimple or it will gout.
et se li artere te fait contraire, si fai ceu que je t’ai dit aprés.	And if the artery is opposite, as I said after.
Et ausi fai de l’aposteme s’il est pierous, et dou taillier et dou curer si com je t’ai dit.	And if the abscess is large, and it is cut and cured as I have said.
Et li taille sus l’aposteme pierous et le moiste, si est plus legiere, car il sont de poc de sanc.	And it measures the incision for the abscess and the wound, if it is more flexible, because there is less blood.
Et si a aucuns de ces apostemes ou chief ou il n’a point de moistor, et de ces fut I apostemes que je copai ou chief d’une vielle femme;	And if there is no moisture in any of these abscesses or heads, and these were not from the mouth of an old woman;
et trovai l’aposteme ausi com une piere xourde, aspre et blainche, et ne pooit brisier;	and found the abscess to be like a sharp, rough, and bloody piercing, that could not be broken;
et s’on en eust ferut aucun, on li eust ausi bien fait plaie com d’une piere.	and if none was made, it was as if a wound had been made like a piercing;
En autres apostemes venans ou chief, fuer que ces qui vienent as chief des enfans et as racines des oreilles, li overture si soit toz jors au plus dependant leu, por mues issir la bowe;	In other abscesses that come, the opening should be made as far down as possible at the base of the ear, to ease the bowels;
et les cure si com il covient.	and they are cured as it is possible.
des scrophules	The first sentence to translate is "des scrophules
Maintes fois avienent cist aposteme au col, et desoz les asseles, et ens angres, et aucune fois vienent autre part ou cors, et sont mout, et sont enjanrees l’une avec l’autre.	Often, the wound of the abscess is at the collarbone, and the stitches come out, and the skin becomes inflamed, and never once do they go to another part or close, and they become infected, and one bone is connected to another.
Et chescune scrophule est proprement dedens sa cote, si com li nout et li aposteme dou chief, si com nos avons dit;	And each wart is properly located on its side, just like the knuckle and the tip of the finger that we have mentioned.
et les semblances de ces scrophules sont maintes.	and the appearances of these warts are many.
Il i a de teles que contienent moistor, et si a de malignes qui ne vuellent obeir a santeit.	It has tissues that contain moisture, and it has malignant ones that do not wish to obey health.
en celle donques que tu vois de bone disposition au tochier, et est semblans a la color dou cors, et muet de chescune part et n’est mie aerse as ners dou col ne a l’artere ne au conduit, et n’est mie parfonde;	in the one that you see with good arrangement on the skin, and is similar to the color of the heart, and uniform in all parts and not rough as nerves of the artery or conductor, and is not rough.
si covient que tu la copes par desus, et l’escorche de chescune partie, et estent les II levres dou keur as oncines, se tu en as mestier, si com nos avons dit en apostemes dou chief;	if you must cut it with a knife, and burn in every part, and the two lips of the ear are hard like bones, if you can bear it, just as we have said about the fingertip.
et la trai poc et poc, et soies seur que tu ne coper lou nerf ne la voine, et ne soit mie li spatumile agus ne trenchans, que li mains n’eschaipe, et ne voise trop avant, que tu ne coper mie ceu que tu ne dois.	And the thread is cut little by little, and be sure you do not cut the nerve or the vein, and do not tear it, that your hands do not slip, and do not cut too soon, that you do not cut more than you should.
Et se tu copes la voinne ou l’artere, et ceu ne te laisse ovrer, si met en la plaie vitriole broiet, ou aucunes poudres que restainchent sanc, et estraint la plaie;	And if you cut the vein or artery, and it does not bleed, then put vitrol or some powders that stay in place, and draw the wound;
et la laisse tant que li apostemes soit apaisiez, et soit amollie li plaie, et encomence a porrir.	and leave it until the swelling subsides, and the wound is softened, and dress it.
Et quant li sans est estainchiez, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que tu l’acomplisses;	And when the blood comes out, if you return to your work, as soon as you have finished it.
puis quier a ton doit indice s’il i demoure nules petites scrophules, si les cope et les munde.	Then wonder if your index finger is tired if it has a few small scabs, if the nails and the cuticles.
Et s’il a en la racine de la scrophule voinne grant, si ne covient mie que tu copes celle scrophule en sa racine, mais la lie d’un fil double fort, et la laisse cheoir par li, sens nuisement;	And if the cause of the scab is deep, then you must only cut off that scab at its root, but leave a strong double thread, and let it hang there without causing any harm.
puis emple la plaie de viel coton plongiet en oignement egiptien, puis la cure.	Then use the wound of thin cotton to dip in Egyptian ointment, then the cure.
Et se tu copes toute la scrophule, si covient que tu assembles les II levres de la plaie, et les cout maintenant, puis qu’il n’i a point demoreit de superfluiteit por la grandor de la scrophule.	If you cover the entire wound, if you manage to bring together the two lips of the wound, and hold them now, then there will be no excess due to the size of the wound.
si covient que tu entendes a coper la racine de li, et traire fuer, et la cout si com nos avons dit.	If you understand how to cover the root of it, and dig further, and cut as we have said.
Celles scrophules que tienent superfluiteit, perce lai ou il apert meure;	Those scabs that hold excess skin, pierce them or make them wider.
et la perce ensi com celle devant dite, en dependant, puis i amenistre tentes avec oignement et semblans choses, si qu’elle corrompe ceu qui est demorez de la corruption;	And pierce them like the one mentioned before, depending on the size, then apply ointments and similar things, if it prevents further corruption.
et quant li plaie est bien mundee, si la cure d’oignement enjanrant char, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when the wound is well-dressed, if the treatment of ointment involves charring, as long as it is healthy.
de squinance	Of the shoulder
Li ancien dirent et parlerent de la tailleure de la gorge;	The ancients spoke and talked about the size of the neck.
mais je ne vis onques en nostre terre qui la feist, et c’est li escripture de lor parole.	But I have never seen anyone who does this in our world, and it is their scripture of speech.
A ces qui ont squinance, il covient que li fendure de la gorge qui est apelee «epiglote» soit eschuee;	To those who have squinting, it is necessary that the neck called "epiglotis" be avoided.
et c’on ne faice aide par ceu, por ceu que toutes les voines et li pormon dou malaide sont a ces qui ont aposteme chaut en la bouche, ou en la gorge ou en II amandres.	And if one cannot help in this way, because all the veins and the blood of the patient are at those who have aphonia in the mouth, or in the throat, or in the lungs.
Quant li maladie est en la chenal dou pormon, il covient coper l’epiglote por fuir la perdition qui vient de l’estranglement.	When the disease is in the throat, it is necessary to close the epiglottis to avoid death that comes from strangulation.
Il covient donques, quant nos volons fendre l’epiglote, que nos le fendons desoz III cercles ou IIII une petite fendure dou travers, entre les II cercles ou par la quantiteit de la fendure dou syfac, ne mie en la cartillaige;	It is therefore necessary, when we wish to cut the epigastrium, that we cut it with three or four small incisions, passing through the two circles or according to the quantity of the cut, not touching the cartilage;
et cil leus si est covenaubles a la section de l’epiglote qu’il n’i a point de char, et li vasseil sont lonc d’enqui.	and they say that if it is possible to cut the epigastrium without causing any harm, and the vessels are not cut, then it is not dangerous;
Et se li maistres est paourous, si covient qu’il estende le cuir de la gorge a tout l’oncine, puis fende lou keur tant qu’il viegne a la cheneil;	And if the masters are unable, then it is necessary that the jawbone extends to the entire neck, then cut the cheek as far as it reaches to the chin;
et eschue les vasselz de sanc, se tu vois aucune chose, et puis cope lou syfac, si com nos avons dit;	And avoid the veins of blood, if you see nothing, and then apply leeches, as we have said.
et est demostrez par la section dou fleume de la cheneil ki saut fuer par le leu qui est rompus, et par la defaute de la voix;	And it is demonstrated by the swelling of the shoulder that was forced to move by the broken arm and due to the lack of voice.
et laisse la plaie overte une piece.	And leave the wound over the bone.
Et quant li houre est passee de coi on doute l’estranglement, assemble les II levres de la plaie dou keur, et la cout toute soule sens la cartillaige;	And when the hour has passed, if there is doubt about the dislocation, gather the two lips of the wound as much as possible, and cover it all so that you feel the cartilage.
puis aministre medicines qui font naistre char, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then administer medicines that make the wound heal quickly, as long as it is healthy.
Albucasim dist c’on ne faice ce jusc’a tant que li gorge est toute estoupee, et li malaides est jugiez a mort, et li defaut li alaine.	Albucasim does not do anything until the throat is completely swollen, and the patient is near death, and the lack of air is fatal.
Adonques cope on l’epiglote por ceu que li malaides ne puet alener, et il respire par la plaie, et ensi est gardez de mort;	Therefore, one should address the epigastrium because the patient cannot breathe, and they die through the wound.
et por ce commanderent li anciain a laissier la plaie overte tant que li malice de la maladie soit passee, et elle est passee en III jors ou en IIII Et adonques il comanderent a coudre la plaie et curer, tant qu’elle fut curee;	And they command the ancients to leave the wound oversized until the malady of the disease has passed, and it has passed in three days or four. Therefore, they command to stitch the wound and treat it, as soon as it is treated.
et je vos dirai ceu que je vis.	And I will tell you what I see.
Je vis que une damoisele prist I coutel, et le ficha en sa gorge, et copa partie des chenelz dou pormon;	I see a maiden who is being cut, and she has a piece of cloth in her throat, and part of her clothing is torn.
et je fui apelez por li curer, et la trovai ausi com morte.	I am called to heal, and I found it as if it were death.
Je descovris la plaie, et trovai le sanc qui en estoit issus, et soi bien qu’elle n’avoit mie copeit voine ne conduit fuer que la gorge, et li vens issoit fuer par la plaie.	I discover the wound, and I find the blood that came out of it, and though she had no veins or it led further than just the throat, it was due to the wound.
Je me hastai, et cousi la plaie, et la curai tant qu’elle fut sanee;	I hurried, and examined the wound, and cured it as soon as it was healthy.
et n’avint a la damoisele fuer qu’elle fut roge de voix, et revint aprés a sa disposition;	and did not reach the damsel until she was red with shame, and returned afterwards to her condition.
por ceu di je que en la tailleure de l’epiglote n’ait mie paour.	because I said that in the cutting of the epiploon there is no pain.
de la grosse gorge	Of the large mouth
Cist apostemes est apelez «hernie de gorge», et est uns grans apostemes en color d’une jaisse, et est molt en femmes;	This hernia is called "hernia of the neck," and it are some large hernias in the color of a thread, and it are much in women.
et est selonc II manieres:	and there are in two ways:
naturez, et accidens;	The natural world and accidents.
ou natureil n’a point d’engien.	Nature has no engine.

et il i ait paour, et ne covient mie ovrer de feir fuers que en celi qui est petite, et le prueve et cerche a tout l’intromissoire:	And if there is pain, and it is not possible to overcome it, then it is better to seek help from the physician who is small, and he will prove and search throughout the introducer.

des nous	The first sentence to translate is
Maintes manieres de nous sont, dont je dirai toutes les semblances;	There are many ways of us, and I will tell you all the appearances.
et or covient que je die toute la difference qui est entre nout et issue.	and it is necessary that I know the entire difference between the born and the issued.
Je dis que issue est chalors et fievre tenans, tant que li ebulicions est passee, et est acomplie li porriture;	I say that issue is childbirth and fever, as long as the ebullitions are passed, and it is completed with the diarrhea.
adonques repose li fievre et li chalor.	but the fever and the labor rest.
Avec lou nout n’a ne chalor ne fievre ne dolor, et contient I syfac, qui est ses propres sac et est selonc la color dou cors, et encomence ausi com une jaisse, et devient gros;	With the newborn there is no labor pain or fever or pain, and it contains I sweat, which is its own bag and is according to the color of the cold heart, and it begins thus like a lump, and becomes large.
et sont selonc II semblances, ou grais, ou moiste, et mout de color sont si com j’ai dit en la division.	1. "And they are according to two appearances, either rough or wet, and of different colors as I said in the division.

"The manner of incising the abscesses in our members is whether you prick more or less than you do in the abscess, and turn your two points again and again until you feel that the cuscus has perceived the keur, then that it is according to the size of the abscess.

grans et moien et petit;	Large, moist, and small.

grant, moien, et petit, por encerchier les apostemes de fistule;	The first sentence to translate is: "Ou cautere de feu comande au malaide qu’il laisse les poilz tant qu’ils sont lons et igals; et s’il le poignent a lor nassance, se li estraint les eulz qu’il ne se muevent tant qu’il naissent.

Les formes des oncines sont de mout de semblances, si com tu vois ci:	The shapes of the claws are quite similar, as you can see here:

de la circoncision	Of the circumcision
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies;	Circumcision is not a continuation of scars like the others;
toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.
