Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens;	For when you press your hand, if it measures evenly in I, then you hold all of it.
mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir;	but that the thread is well stretched over the leather.
et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;	And so the manner of the first opening if you think the child understands, that you do not tie the thread too tightly only, and then I will loosen it in all the ways you please.
puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens;	Then I will tie it all right in your hands, and place the forces between your hands or on your fingers that the child does not see, and no one of the threads.
puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens;	Then put your hand on the bone and blow or suck, and draw it up as much as the head of the bone is in.
puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz I poc a I autre liien;	Then clean well the assembly of the waste, then tie the head of the bone with a double thread, then tie it opposite to the other line.
et la tien as II dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les II liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge;	And the tie you need for the second reading in the pouch and the index, pass between the two loops, then gently lift the handle at high speed and pull the head of the nail.
puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres;	Then leave the blood pouch alone, as it is the most difficult.
et met poudre sus et sus la poudre I drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And sprinkle powder on it and on the powder, with a damp piece of cooked beef, cut into thin slices and marinated in olive oil and vinegar, and let it sit for a day, and treat it again until it is healthy.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste:	The form of the forces at worlding if this is:
li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	The head of the shoulder is dislocated, and it cannot stay in place. It should be reset as soon as possible.
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision;	The error of mutilation occurs if the edges escape through the incision.
donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme;	Therefore, you must extend the wound to your finger, otherwise it will result in gangrene.
et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	And it should be held correctly, and if you do not hold it with your finger, then the wound will be lost, and then the cope.
Et s’il trespassent III jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement;	And if the wounds persist for three days, and the surrounding area is swollen, then it should be left alone until gangrene occurs, and then it should be lightly burned.
si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	If the cautery is as you see it, and you hold it from the part of the ginger, it will not harm you.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point;	Treat the shoulder with things made of sour powder, which we have said or treated with powders, and if it cope well enough, it will be cured, otherwise it will not work.
cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Treat the shoulder as we have said, as long as it is healthy.
dou retenement de l’urine	Retention of urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	The retention of urine if it is from opalescent wounds, or scabs, or bowels, or gallstones, or similar things, as we have said in the division.
et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz;	And if the urine is not discharged, and you see that it is retained by the urethra which is either at the top or bottom of the bladder, then it comes that the patient's pain is caused by the catheter being placed on his groins.
et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet;	And the catheter is placed on the side of the belly, and the abdomen is extended from the part below the back, and the patient's pain is reduced as much as possible.
et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	And therefore the bladder is constrained to express the urethra at the bottom, because the urine is discharged.
et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme:	And if it does not come, as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you must administer an extraction of all the instrument called "siringue", and its form is like this:
et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil;	and let silver thin hair be like the tail of a squirrel.
et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	and let the leash of a long and half palm tree be thin at the end.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue;	And the manner of the urine's issue if it is that you take a double thread, and tie at the end of the wool or linen, and cut the end of the thread with the snare of the ingerence.
et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;	and cut the excess of the wool and cut the end of the ingerence, then anoint the ingerence with oil or burr and urine of beef, and make the patient sit on the seat, and the woman's vessel and the verge moist with olive oil and olive oil and German tincture.
puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude;	Then lightly place the thread at the edge, as it reaches the root of the edge, then double the edge towards the side of the bulge.
puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors;	Then pull the thread before it reaches the bladder, and feel the patient's pain coming from the empty thing, and this is done according to this order because either the conductor or the one who will be guided is turned.
puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine;	Then the thread is all over the hair, and the urine follows the hair, then I take it further, and make the urine flow.
et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	And repeat the thread as soon as the bladder is empty, and alleviate the patient's pain.
des maladies de la vessie	Of diseases of the bladder
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When there are scorching or bloody discharges in the bladder, or when an abscess is formed and you see water and medicines distilling, then use all the instrument called "cathoscopy", and it is shaped like this:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus:	She is closed, and if there is III pulsation:
II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois;	On one hand, and on the other, if you see;
et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	and the wound is read by the physician, who knows it is well healed without addition, if we can treat the moisture, and bind as soon as possible;
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens;	And when you see your medicines running in the uterus, place the head of the steel needle in the moisture, and withdraw it at the point where it is;
si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens;	If you draw the moisture with the steel needle, and then tightly bind the point where it is;
si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	If the moisture enters the uterus, and comes to the uterus now, if it feels the pain;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie:	And it is the form of a delicate caustic whose use is to scarify the uterus.
si est ci:	If it is, then:
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut;	And it is made of silver or lead, and it is the head above.
et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet;	and does not adhere to the skin or the flesh.
puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu;	Then take a sheep's bladder and apply the moisture that you have used to scarify the uterus, then place it between the two breasts to form a double-layered poultice, and heat the moisture over the fire.
puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	Then cut the head of the caustic along the edge, then squeeze your hand over the uterus with all the moisture that comes out, as long as the patient feels that the moisture is entering the uterus.
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor;	and if you do not have a gauze, then take a piece of linen, and make a circle, and pierce it around the hole.
puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument;	then insert a strong thread in these wounds, then assemble the circle as we do with a nail, and put oil, sweat, and vinegar on it, and tie it in the instrument.
et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	and do as you have done with the gauze, pressing with your hand until the moisture reaches the gauze.
de la piere	From the incision
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines;	We have said in the division of wounds, and in assembling remedies.
et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille;	and I said the difference between a piercing and an incision, and the signs, and in what size we must over it.
et en la vessie, et en la verge;	and in the bladder, and in the vulva.
et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	and I will tell you openly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit;	I say that the wound which is dislocated in the bladder often occurs in children, and it is a sign that the inflammation of the bladder is becoming more acute.
et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist;	and if it is opened, and the vulva is grated, and it can be done many times, and then it becomes inflamed.
et a mout de ces saut li fondemens;	and at the end of these wounds, they become infected.
et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont IIII ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece;	and the cure is light for children until they are four years old, and it is grievous in the winter, and it is much more so in the spring, for those who are between winter and spring.
et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	And the cure is less severe for those with large incisions than for those with small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to the cure, if we cover the patient with cloths dipped in cold water, we must cleanse all the insides.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	For it never closes the wound.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut;	Then take the patient by the shoulders and stand up, and move to the side, if the incision descends to the front of the bladder, and does not once reach the top of the leg.
puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval;	Then place the patient between your hands in a comfortable position, and your hands should be above their knees, if the bladder is entirely tilted downwards.
puis la quier et la touche dedens;	Then gently and carefully touch it.
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	If you feel the incision in the spaciousness, then cut it now at the incision.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis;	And if she does not feel any pain when touched, if your index finger is oiled with oil from the left hand, or if it is dry, if the other fingers are well-oiled.
et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie;	and the wound in its foundation, and want to pierce it, and when you feel with your finger at the top of the vagina.
puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	Then press with your finger, and the wound should be in the direction that you see it is cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille;	And instruct the minister to press the vagina with his hand, and he commands that he extends with his right hand the curls at the top, and with his left hand to grasp the hair that is loose at the part where the cut is made.
puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	Then he cuts the stump coping, of which this is the form:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre;	And they make between those who are between the corners and the foundation, not with a mill but at the side of the right shoulder.
et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	And it should be above the incision, and the stitches should be either at the foundation or below, and the size should be large enough so that it covers the wound as much as possible, and should not be too tight.
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail;	by chance the pressure if it is at the foundation, which will jump further during work.
et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges:	and you should check if it has part of the incision or angle, and margins.
si est griés a issir;	If it is cold outside.
et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	And if the part that is wet appears as a glowing, and moves, whose exit is light.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant;	If it has angles and margins, make the size larger.
et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe;	And if it does not hold, then you must pull on the nails that are as sharp as a needle in the head, so that the piercing does not slip.
ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief;	Or if you break the delicate instrument pointed at the head.
et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	And if you do not break it in time, then the wound will widen and if it is not cracked, then pull on it with vitriol.
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	And if there are more piercings, if the largest one is at the top of the vagina, then cut it off, then pull it out, and the small ones afterward, if there are more.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	If it is not treated promptly, it can lead to a large wound and further injury.
Car II choses avienent au malaide:	For two things come to the patient:
ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder;	or he dies, or the urine comes out without being able to close it;
mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	but you should try to draw it out, or use tweezers to remove the hairs, as long as you draw it out in pieces;
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut;	and when you have completed your work, if you use the wound of incense and aloe and dragon's blood, and draw it out, and then put on soft cloth soaked in oil and vinegar, or oil and rosewater and cold water, to ease the post-extraction soreness;
puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	Then the patient tilts his head, and does not loosen the knot of the thread.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	When you dislocate it, if the joint is well oiled with oil and sage, then the cure of ointment dyefacient and basilic ointment, until it is healthy.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine:	And if the abscess comes in the wound and corrosions, and the blood is blocked in the vein, and it is held by the urine, which is in a similar way that without jumping with the urine:
boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	Bites that are deep into the wound, and remove the pus, because if it remains, it will cause the vein to rupture, and bleed.
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then cleanse the wound with warm water and salt, and aid it in every way that you know, as long as it is healthy.
et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	And it is necessary that all the wounds that you treat, that you lie the thighs, and gather the medicines on the leg.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir;	And if the piercing is small, and it is directed by the bone, and it is not broken, and the urine cannot be discharged.
si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	If the treatment of what I say does not satisfy you, that you cut it many times, is an excuse for the size of this treatment.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I have already done that.
Pren I foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a III angles fichiees en I tison:	Prepare to forge according to this form and make it at a third angle, one ton.
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie;	Then take the file and pull the ligature around the edge of the wound, so that it does not get caught in the vein.
puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere;	Then lightly cut the wood along the edge of the wound, until it reaches the piercing.
et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part;	And turn the wood in your hand at the piercing, as much as you can, until you feel the other side of the piercing.
si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	If a lot of urine comes out, then press your hand on the part that is being pulled away from the piercing that is being loosened by the edge.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	If it breaks, and it falls with the urine, and it causes pain to the patient.
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie;	And if you do not do this for any reason, if the child's leg is not cut and the other is, then they make a groove between the two limbs, then the stitch is taken out, and the sewn-up wire is removed, and cleanse the frozen blood that is in the wound.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and care for it until it is healthy.
de la piere des femmes	of the piercing of women
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por III choses:	Only one piercing should be made in women, and if there is none at all, if the care is grievous and defended by three things:
l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge;	one is that by chance the woman is virgin;
et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	and the second is that one cannot find a well-behaved woman who has been deceived by mirrors, even when she is young;
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains;	And the third method, if by chance one cannot find a skilled woman in this art of hands.
et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil;	And the fourth method, if by chance the woman's wound is more than the man's, because it requires a more profound size. And if you must dismember, then choose a skilled hand and cut along the vein, and if you cannot find one, then use a subtle knife.
et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	This is a wise practice in the life of women, or a woman who knows part of the art, and she commands that she does what you command of the examination of the wound.
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge:	and look well, see if the woman is a virgin:
adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere;	and then it is necessary to set the bone or the nail and prick the hole;
et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	and if she is tight, then the bone is loosened and she should set her bone or the nail with the helper, and she should press and hold her left hand on the vagina;
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse;	if she is tight, then it is necessary to loosen her bone so that she can move it slightly from the entrance of the vagina until she reaches the root of the thigh;
puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie;	then, press on the hole in the thigh at the root of the thigh against the soft tissue, where it is most painful, and feel the hole in that part;
et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	and does not move his shoulder away from the incision or socket, and it should be the first small one.
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont:	then cut the skin in that size, if you feel the wound is deep enough that the hole can come out further, and consider that many methods of holes are:
c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	it is to know, small and large, sharp and smooth, long and rounded, and which have veins:
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	If you want to know the appearance to know the end.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if it is not sharp, if you put vitriol on the bone, and hold it for an hour until it is not burned:
puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	then return to your work, until the hole is out, and have stitches that I told you in the extraction of the hole to help you in your work:
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide;	And if it is not set without pain, and that is the artery that is cut, if one puts powder on the shoulder and stretches it tightly and does not continue this, and leaves the wound and does not touch it, by chance the patient will die.
puis cure la plaie.	Then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the pain of the wound is eased, and it is read, if you return to your work, as long as the wound is healing.
de hernie carnouse	of hernia caruncle
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef;	Wet is nothing but an assembly of moisture or white soap, which contains the urine of the beast.
et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit I autre oef;	And is called "soap" and has never been properly in the urine of the beast, if one cares that it is another animal's urine.
et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit;	And that is the flesh between the white smoke that we have spoken of.
et ceu n’avient se poc non.	And there was nothing else.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the generation of this sweat is due to the lack of it coming from the bladder, and it is expanded that matter.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors:	And never does it come from percussion on the flesh, and this moisture is of many colors.
ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	Or it is flushed, or without red, or black, or white water, and it comes more.
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	And this is the sign to assemble it, for if it is white smoke that we have spoken of, and the wounds are long as we have said, and it does not open the flesh, for it is moist throughout.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	If it is moist in its own cloth, and the abscess is closed with a part of the bladder, and because they think it is other ointments.
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien;	and if the moisture is between the hide of the thighs and the white ointment, and it is felt well.
donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	then when you see the color of the moisture, if you press on all the introducer, with what form it is before.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	According to what comes after the introduction, judge whether it is dependent or independent.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors;	And when we cauterize by fire, if it comes that the patient is healthy according to what could be and the fullness of his chest.
puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	Then the sowing on his back, with something high, and then put him to sleep with clothes.
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions;	If the patient feels pain on their side, and commands the attendant to pull to the other side, extend the finger at one of the two ribs closest to the knee.
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	Then take the spatula, and cut the tendon between the two long ribs until you reach the point of the finger, and make sure your fingers are straight and facing upwards, marking the tendon with white fat, and scrape it gently so as not to cause pain.
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont;	Then pierce the white fat with a sharp needle at the large opening, remove all the fat, and then put your shoulders, and stretch the white fat.
et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement;	And do not touch the curvature of the bones, but only the sutures.
cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	Coping all or by pieces at once the costal cartilage of him, if you do not know how to do it well, then it will return the ague.
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac;	And if the head falls on your shoulder, then reset it in the shoulder as soon as you have completed the operation on the suture.
puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then assemble the two halves of the curvature of the bones with a suture, then treat it as you would other wounds, until it is healthy.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc;	And if you find the head corrupted by another disease, then cut the veins that are suspended, doubting the dislocation of the sutures.
puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	Then pull the ring on all the suspensors, and remove the nail, and treat it as we have said.

si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	if you pull the other part as you did the first dislocation, then put the blood in the wound, and put fine oil on it;
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	and put another fine linen on vine and oil, and put it on the two suspensors, and doubled strips of cloth, and tie it to all the part that is according to this form:
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil;	Then take the strips, and use the lace made according to this appearance and are assembled by sewing on the waist of the braies, and one of the heads is pricked at the back, and the other at the part that is pointed;
et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	And the other two heads are situated on the other two sides, and all the restriction is restricted in the loop of the bow.
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	And no time is there for this fire cautery in the sharpness of the leather, and it is that you use the subtle cautery cultell, and cut the hair of the fingers, and it should be washed as we have said, if the white fluid that contains the ague is discovered.
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	If you take the cautery according to this form, and pierce that white fluid with the bones, and burn at this subtle cautery cultell.
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout;	And cut in all the ways you can think of, as long as you are careful with everything.
et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef;	and keep the testicles from being touched by the hand
et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve;	and consider this work to be more beneficial;
et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	and keeps away from evacuation of blood, and makes sure the size is correct;
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	and if nothing else causes harm, such as an abscess or evacuation of blood, or anything else, then treat what is causing the harm according to what has been said;
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit;	And if the patient is not strong, and does not want to wait for this work because of its horrible nature, then if there is perforation, as I have said, and you are sure about the meanings we have said that the head of the shoulder is the first to be set, then place the patient on their side;
pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors;	Because the aposteme is at the end of the part of the bone that is large for all the cartilage, and the perforation is long and narrow.
et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	And if the perforations are wide, then all the wounds will heal quickly.

de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of the boils
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	Sharpen the edges of this ramification in several ways, because it seems to me that you should leave it alone.
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	And I will tell you the work and the appearances of the abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions;	I say that all abscesses come from corruption and also from cold.
et c’est par mout de cas.	and it is for the most part true.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	It is to be known by excessive sweet and acrid humor, which is expanded by cold or by percussion.
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors;	And the color of the suture according to the color of the corpse.
et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	And there is no pain, and the suture is grievous.
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	And by chance, some sutures are grievous and painful, of a strange color, and no veins or arteries are ever found.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	When it is from an artery, then it is known by the arrangement of the suture, when you press on it with your fingers.
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	And it is necessary that you touch it.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	That which is made of veins is known by its arrangement in expression, and can be quite well made according to this shape, and according to the others.
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	And when you catch the head of the shoulder, then it is the hip that moves up, and the arm is pushed down with white sugar, and deliver the suspensory from all parts of the hip.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	If the hip is already swollen with these charms, then it is necessary to draw the hip, and catch the shoulder.
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	And if it is stuck with sugar, or in the veins that are dilated, then it is necessary to deliver all of this, and the shoulder catches up again.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the birth of the child is from below, and it is stuck, and you manage to free it all, as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when your work is completed, if you use the smooth woolen wound with oil of rose and wine, then apply other cures as needed until it is healthy.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of the boils
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait;	These are some abscesses enveloped in an envelope similar to the bog, with the softening of the joints, and the patient groans as it goes.

car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz;	For there is no harm in this, and all the surgeons come to see, so it is necessary to treat the wounds on all the surgeons.
si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	If he loses his strength due to the incision of the veins, and they become dry and cannot be helped.
de la routure dou syfac	Of the rupture of a sinew
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	The effects of this operation are that it comes by section or scar, or extension to the belly in the part of the angles, because the intestines hang down from that rupture to one of the groins.
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes:	And this rupture is either by scar or extension of the intestine, and these two methods cause the following:
ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	or by percussion, or jumping, or burning, or lifting of the groin, and in similar ways.
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	And the signs when it is extension by scar are that it comes with small and small openings, in long tents, and there is no sudden coming.
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	And it remains equal until it reaches the stomach, because the food presses on the intestines.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the signs are when it is rupture of the tendon, which makes pain come at the beginning, and it is the grief faix appearing divers times, not far from the skin, and it is because of the exit of the intestine and the wound at the end of the tendon.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And no time does the circles descend with the intestine, and it is held back, and great pain is suffered by the patient, even when pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	In these treatments of iron for pain, because it cannot be escaped.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	And the manner of the incision if you command or the helper to put the intestine in their hand at the edge in the wound, if they can enter.
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	Then it is severed between your shoulders, between your hands, and gently pull on the cords.
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	Then the neck is cut at the base, and cut all the hair of the long coat.
puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	Then cut the tendons of the legs according to what you have experience in opening the wound, and they should be able to enter.
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	Then the scorched skin that is full of hairs, as long as the white skin is not discovered in all parts.
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac;	Then place your index finger in the area where the hair is taught, between the white skin that is full of hairs and the second skin, and go until you reach the end of the thigh, and then between the second skin.
et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	And then remove the left hand from the hair of the thigh, and the white skin is at the top of your right hand, and gently pull the leg towards the tail.

Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	For no time is this cauterized the white skin that we have said, after the incision, due to fear of the evacuation of blood.

et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	And if it is late in the evening, and if it is heated with hot water, and it is applied as we have said, then it will grow.

de hernie carnouse	of hernia caruncle
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this matter, I have never seen anyone who has made the cure by fire.

Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The scar is bound, and has no appearance in the healing, and the cauterization is more effective at a distance from the wound, and closer to health.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	of the softening of the leather of the bones.
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	Many times the hair of the eyebrows is plucked in men, because the strings that are densened are softened, and it can be seen.

Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	Since scarring is forbidden in our law, and because I think it would be best not to mention this in this book.

Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	This is also a strange thing, and they don't live long, they have no name.
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know that they are multiplied, and they are destroyed by the wicked one who decides them, which is bound to the abscess.
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	And never have they come naturally as all at once, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they come seriously, if the cure is as we have said, and it is the subtle dance, and it is done quickly and lightly what it does.
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	and do it as it should be saluted.
de plusors enfans	Of more children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	1. No time are formed in the marriage I or II or III or IV or V or VI or VII, or more than XV, and are all formed in the form of a child by the measurement of the sweet glorious wheat, and cover that the wild dance covers everything, as if by chance something similar happens.
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	2. If it is done according to what is necessary.
de l’enfant mort	Of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	3. When you treat the woman who has given birth to a stillborn child or is in her belly, as I have said in the division, and it does not come out, and you are forced to deliver with your hands;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	4. If it is necessary that you cut that the woman is of healthy virtue and has no accident or dies;
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	If it comes to pass that the woman is pregnant on her back, and her head is inclined downwards, and her legs are raised.
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	and the midwife applies the second degree burn, or if she is in bed if she is not treated for the descent of the child.
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	Then anoint the mouth of the midwife with moist oils of olive, mustard, and fenugreek, and the seeds of flax, then take her hands away from these oils and these ointments.
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	Then lightly bind her wrists, then let the legs be loose or she bites the nails that are capable of being bent at this time, and wait until the child is descending from its head.
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	If the shoulder bone is seen in the arm, or in the neck, or in the mouth, or in the ear, or on the beard, or in the eyelid, or near the ribs, and if it is felt to be stuck, then it should be freed with care and the costal cartilage.
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	And it is necessary to scrape the shoulder bone with your left hand, and place the feather between the thumb and index finger of your right hand, and gently pull it, and free the shoulder bone from any of the places we have mentioned until it fits into the empty state.
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	And this is the shape of the shoulder bone:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	Then find another bone, or if you are skilled enough, if the extraction is equal;
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	and then the joint is aligned by moving from both sides, and the patient's hand should be held firmly, if like this is the shape:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if a part is loose, if there are any of its two oils on that side, and take out the other side, and handle the other part:
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	And if it does not come loose, then put this bone or higher up, and do as much as it comes out completely:
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	And if one hand comes before the other, and it cannot be returned by traction, then it should be wrapped around as much as possible, until it is completely:
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	Then the copious application is in the joint of the heel or elbow, and it is necessary that you apply it with the other hand, and then put on the shoe.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	And if the child's head is large and comes out with difficulty, or there is a crowning present, then you must separate the sharp spatula between your two hands, and pull the head and remove the crown.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	or you can put it in the instrument called "almidach", if the form comes with the forceps or the cauterization that follows it.
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	and then you can apply the child naturally with a large head.
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	Then, treat the bones with nails, and if the head of the shoulder jumps out, it is pulled by force as much as possible, even if it is bent, until the moisture that caused it comes out.
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	And if it cannot be extracted, if it sticks to the skin as you pull,
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	And if it is bent at the belly or the ribs, then you must push it as much as possible until the moisture corrects it.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the child is among its flock, if it is the light attraction, and the milk of the mother is light.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is twisted at the belly or the anus, then you must twist it loose with your hand.
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	And if you stretch the belly or the anus as much as possible, until the moisture corrects it.
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	And if the other member becomes inflamed, and the shoulder is swollen, if the pain is great, then the person draws their hand back from the joint, and pulls it out of the mouth of the joint.
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	Then they either cut or split, and they take it out.
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	And if the mouth of the joint is narrowed by the wound that it has come from, and there is no way to open it, then it must be managed with moist and light things.
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	And the management is applied, and it is softened and made moist and cool.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the child is crying on its chest, and you put it down equally, then manage it as we have said in the live child.
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	If it is not possible, if the bone breaks into pieces, and leave nothing of the second part.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, make sure to follow the instructions we have given for the aftercare.
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	And if blood comes out, if it is put in a washcloth to stop the bleeding, and other treatments are made.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut I autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I see a woman in whose belly some children had died, then consulted another and was told that it would die, the other.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After long time came some abscesses in the flesh, and inflamed as soon as they were opened, and began to cause great pain.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called for the cure, and I thought long time, and could not soothe the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I used strong astringents for great attraction, and after some days more.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was surprised much, because the belly has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	If you thought that it was bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I want the wound, and with my hands I will treat it as much as the woman was in better condition.
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	and the woman held her breath for a little while, and there was a little blood;
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	and I did not remember this chapter to be because when the master saw an extraordinary thing, he thought to help.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	To bring the dislocation back to its place.
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	Here comes the first sentence to translate:
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	and at the turning of the head of the shoulder.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	However, the corner should be more subtle and narrow, and should be flat or rounded.
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and the mouth should be of a due length, and the margins of the trees should be long, and half as long as a palm.
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and the shoulders should be of two joints of this same bone, which are closed on one side and open on the other, half a palm long or a little more.
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	and these joints are closed in the mouth of the shoulder to open when turning the head corners.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, more subtle and lighter in appearance, is made of flat board or beech, according to the appearance of the tacks.
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	and it has two joints, as you see, of a palm of long wood, and they must be wide.
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	and when you see the mare open wide with all the instruments, if you place the woman on her side and the thighs over, then adjust the joints together in the mare, and hold the end of the instrument's handle between your fingers.
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	then use your hand on all the instruments, as you have done with the tacks evenly, according to the amount you see open the mare's mouth, until it stops making noise that you can hear.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	These instruments are all around us, and their appearances are multiplied.
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	And when you look at them, the more they work, the higher they become in number.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	2. If you do not despise the instrument that you have not yet examined, because its needs are not easily satisfied.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the second child is retained in the womb, if you command the midwife to release the hair, and then the placenta comes out, and your hands are forced to the mouth and nose.
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	And if she jumps for joy at this, it is well.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, then I can, and make a pincushion or cupping glass, and put herbs that may open the mouth of the child, such as calamine, rose, anise, chamomile, cascarilla, and century plant.
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	All these herbs, or none of them, must be cooked or placed on fire.
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	Then place a cain or pertus that can be burned, and the other end in the mouth of the mare, and heat it until the vapors come out of the mare.
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	Then the dressing is applied, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If the second part is fast.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	And if it remains after this treatment, and is not worse, then order the physician to take her left hand in oil of sesamum or musk, and then blow into the mouth, and then apply the second one.
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	And when she finds it, if she pricks and extends it little by little, so that the mare does not resist the extraction.
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	but the goal is to move lightly to the left and right, then pull it out.
si venra et se desaerdra.	if it comes and comes out.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the mouth of the wound is closed, we have said the treatment is to suture and fumigate with herbs.
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	And if it is not all of what we have said, then keep that you do not pull out;
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but what is in the mouth of the wound, you should tie it to the woman's thigh, then dress with ointment tetrafarmacone.
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	if it is purged and reset, and it comes out correctly.
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	But if it comes out with bad smell from the stomach and head, and pierces the physician.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	If then come fumigations suitable to this:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	no one of the old has experienced fumigations of garlic and dry figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The form of the instrument is such that it burns the woman with the retention of flowers and the second wind if this is:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it seems like a dog, and puts it on the head subtly in nature, and the large ones under the fire.
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and if the fumigations are on the coals, and the ash as it is, and another one begins again.
de percier lou fondement	to perceive the foundation
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born who have not felt the foundation, but it has been swept with some subtle soap.
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	If it comes to the point that he cannot cut through the flesh with his blade, and does not cut with a sharp one, and roughens the skin without touching it, then...
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then he should grind his blade on vine and oil, and apply the ointment as soon as it is sharp.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it does not stay, if you put a catheter in its place and leave it hands free, and it is able to move when the child sees them going into the rooms.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	And never comes a wound or abscess that is soothed by salt.
si covient coper celui soudement:	If it comes to soothe that wound or abscess with salt...
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	If you apply it, as we have said of the dog's bite.
de la fistule dou fondement	of the fistula with great foundation.
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	Fistulas that come from the foundation are nodulation, and grow when they come from the delve of the foundation, or in the space between the two parts, if there is one or more.
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	When that node is old, if it is worked on, and the moisture is removed with soft flaps or subtle bows, and they are never formed into fistulas.
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	They are known by the fact that they are caused by either elimination or ventosity when the patient evacuates, and by chance, some fall.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	And if the fistulas are in the bladder and half in the vagina.
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	and reach the joint of the thigh and the knee.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And it is known that the fistula is not present at its base, and does not have a fistula.
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	And it is that you cut your index or foundation, and insert a small needle of iron or silver into the fistula when it has no kinks.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if it has kinks, then insert a small tent of silk or horsehair, as soon as you feel the tent or hair in your hand.
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	And if you do not feel it, and there is no bleeding, no vomiting, or wind, as we have said.
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	Make sure it does not pierce through.
si te haste dou curer.	If you feel pain.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula is present in the bladder or conducted from the urine, if it leaks and cannot be stopped by medicines.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	And if it pierces through the joint of the thigh, as soon as it reaches the knee.
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	If it does not have twisting and the cause of the pain is not known, then it is because there is no remedy for it, and no medicine can be applied to alleviate it.
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	And in these Persian fistulas, there is no cure other than labor and the vanity of the proud who enter into them.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	In the one that is not Persian and not ancient, there is hope for health through iron, as I have experienced, and it is that the physician's hand is between your hands on his back.
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and he gently lifts the legs up to his thighs, and has his thighs inclined towards his belly.
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	Then cut around the hair, or if it is knotted, as long as you can until the tent comes off.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	If the patient feels pain at the foundation, it means that the tent has been cut too short, so you should cut it off.
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	And if you feel between your fingers the hoof or the horn, then cut it off, and check that it is straight.
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	If you cannot trim it with a knife, do not try to cut it off.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	It is difficult to say whether one can cut it all, but this is rare.
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	And if it helps, if you make the fire cautery subtle according to the size of the fistula, as described earlier.
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	and the bone is very hard in the fistula as it approaches the foundation.
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and do this two or three times until you feel that these points must be assisted, which resemble a pen of feathers;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then the treatment of tented wounds is rolled in burrs, as long as it stays open, then the treatment of ointment is poured on and allowed to dry.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If it is healthy, so good.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If this is done, no other remedy can be found.
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	And if it is tried in, and does not pierce the foundation, which is either the base or the head, and cover the opening with a thick layer of char or soot, and you see the fistula coming out that shows the covering dust;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	If the head of the fistula, and it comes out before the tent, and then the cauterization afterward, as long as it reaches the tip of the tent.
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	and will be delivered from the tent, and will cause pain.
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	Then the deformed ones that seem like a feather of a hummingbird, and there will be none left.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	If it does not harm you, and cuts between you and the flesh, whether by fire cauterization or medical boiling.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	For the fire cautery, it assembles two things:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	it is to know, the surety of these deformed ones, and the stopping of blood and the treatment of moisture.
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	Then the treatment of soft tents in burrs or in the throat as long as it does not gutter, and it will be the deformed ones to enter the gutter.
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	Then treat the wound of the sulfurous ointment with dry heat, and the medicines are dry.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, if it is healthy and does not return again.

dou fremit	The first sentence to translate is "dou
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	Furuncle is a small appearance that should be removed from the body and goes away in front.
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	And never the wound does not heal, and it is felt as if it were dead, and comes throughout the body, and more with the hands than other parts.

de la forme dou clistere	The form of the fire cautery
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	No time has been made where a clasp of silver or an archaut, or a melted or hammered iron, has been made.
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	And no time has been made where these small and large bites are made, according to the ones that are stolen from them.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Therefore, in the treatment of children who are weak and painful, they are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of the fire clistery is small and large if it is made wide, or the belly is made in this way:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	and if it has a deviation or the belly is lied, as you see, and the head is dislocated perceived.
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	and if it has an injury or one of the ribs is fractured, and the other is not.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	and if it is in the belly or a vessel of beef or cheese is inserted, and all the wounds are seen through, and there must be a spice between each wound, then pour through these wounds a strong thread made of thread crooked in X or along the edge, and assemble the belly as if it were a hedgehog.
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	and when the medicine is given, if the string is to the instrument before a strong thread, then close it.
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	And it is the form of a circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the medicine not be too hot or too cold, and anoint the head with oil or ointment made of urine or something similar, then apply it lightly.
