Et quant tu l’avras mise igal, si met sus l’emplaustre, puis met sus une estele de fust ou de keur, et estraint la briseure, si qu’ele ne se mueve;	And when you have placed it evenly, then place a rule of flax or leather, and tighten the string, if it does not move.
et emple le leu desoz les costes, tant que li lieure soit igalz.	and use the leather as far as the cost is even.
Et comande au malaide k’il dorme sus son costeit sain, ou sus son dos.	And instruct the patient to sleep on his healthy side or on his back.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si n’i tochier, tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et met sus ceu que nos avons devant dit;	And if abscesses appear, and they come, if they are not pricked, as long as the abscess is not pricked, and place what we have already said before.
et puis revien a la restauration, et l’estraint si com il covient, s’il n’i a nul mavais accident;	and then return to restoration, and tighten as it is possible, if there is no other accident.
et c’est li maniere.	And that is the way.
de la brisure de l’ajutoire	Of the shoulder dislocation
Li adjutoires est ceu qui est entre lou coute et lou chief de l’espaule, et s’il est brisiez, si le doit on restorer selonc l’une des II manieres:	1. The auxiliary is that which is between the upper and lower part of the shoulder blade, and if it is broken, it must be restored according to one of the following two methods:
dont l’une est que tu pren I fust plain de moiene groissor, selonc ceste forme:	2. The other method is to use a thin, straight piece of bone, according to this form:
Et lie as II chiés II liens, et les pent en haut, et siece li malaide sus I siege;	3. And then fasten the heads of the bones, and hold them in place, and put the surgeon on the seat:
puis li giete som bras brisiet sus le fust, tant qu’il viegne a l’aissele, et ait em mi une corbeure de fust, puis pent sus aucune pesant chose ou li ministres l’estende aval;	4. Then the arm that is broken at the shoulder must be placed on the seat, as it goes to the narrow part, and has a piece of bone in the middle, then can hold any heavy thing or extend the muscles:
puis mette li mires la briseure igal a ses mains ensamble, tant que li briseure retorne si com il covient.	Then place the forceps evenly in your hands, as long as the forceps returns to its original position as intended.
Et li autre maniere si est que on sovine le malaide sus son hatereil, et li lie la main a son col, puis comande a II ministres que li uns teigne ceu qui est sus la briseure a ses mains, et li autres teigne desoz a tout I liien, et estende chescuns a sa partie.	And the other way is if one holds the patient down while they are in pain, and lays their hand on their collarbone, then commands the ministers to touch the parts where the bracelet is on their hands, and touches the others lightly all over the limb, and spreads each to its part.
Et se tu vues que li estraction soit plus fors, si estraint I liien desoz la briseure, et sus la briseure, et estende chescuns des ministres a sa part.	And if you see that the extraction is more difficult, then force the limb to move against the bracelet, and move the bracelet, and stretch each of the ministers to their part.
Et se li briseure est prochiene au chief de l’espaule, si covient que tu mettes I liien moien desoz l’assele, et I autre vers lou coute, desoz la briseure;	And if the forceps is bent at the shoulder blade, then you must tighten one string on the back and the other on the front, away from the forceps.
et ausi se li briseure est devers lou coute, si i covient mettre I liien legierement, sens labor, tant que li briseure soit igalz sus lou leu, et sus lou coute;	And if the forceps is bent towards the elbow, then you must tighten one string lightly, in the direction of labor, as long as the forceps is even with the shoulder blade and the elbow.
puis met igal la brisure, si com il covient, et l’estraint, se apostemes chaus n’i vient.	Then place the forceps as intended, as long as it is correct, and tighten it, hold your breath until no pain comes.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si ne l’estraindre mie jusc’a VII jors, et met sus lainne moillie en aisil et en oile roset, tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez;	And if the inflammation comes, if it is not strained too much within seven days, and it is put on with fine thread and olive oil, as long as the inflammation is calmed.
puis l’estraint, et li maniere de l’estraindre si est que tu mettes l’emplaustre sus la briseure, puis assemble le bras sus l’ajutoire, et met ta main sus l’espaule ou sus lou sein;	Then the strain, and the way of the strain if you put the splint on the wrist, then assemble the arm with the helper, and place your hand on the shoulder or on the chest.
et met le drapeil, et estraint sus l’ajutoire, et sus lou bras, si que li bras soit en leu d’esteles, s’aucune chose ne le te deffent, ou se li os n’est muez.	And tie the bandage, and strain on the helper, and on the arm, if the arm is in its place, nothing should prevent it, or if the bone is not moved.
Et se tu doutes que li os ne se mueve, si use d’esteles, et met sus la brisure une estele plus large et plus fort des autres, et ait entre chescune estele I doi d’espaice, et soit chescune estele si grans qu’elle passe la briseure III dois de chescune part;	If you doubt that the bone does not move, then use these, and place the incision with a wider and stronger needle than the others, and let there be one space between each needle and two spaces between the parts; and each space should be as large as it passes through the incision three times.
puis estrain sus les esteles, ensi com j’ai dit au comencement dou chapistre sus la briseure, plus fort et moins en aloignant.	Then draw out the needles, as I said at the beginning of this chapter, making them stronger and not moving them.
Et se tu vois l’assise des esteles, et l’estrignement, si com nos avons dit, en l’oure que tu restoures le membre brisiet, et tu doutes l’aposteme chaut, si le laisse a liier jusc’a septime jor, si com nos avons dit;	And if you see the seat of the needles and the traction, as we have said, in the direction you are restoring the broken member, and you doubt the abscess, if it is left alone for nine days, as we have said.
puis regarde chescuns III jors lou lien, que prurite ne enfleure n’i viegne au leu, ou li norrissemens ne puist venir au membre por ceu k’il est trop estrois.	Then look at every third year's link, whether the itch does not inflame or it does not reach the limb because of its being too tight.
Si l’adrece, si com nos avons dit.	If the address, as we have said.
Et se nulz telz accidens n’i vient, si ne lou desliier fuer que aprés III jors ou plus, et dorme li malaides sus son dos, et ait ses mains sus son stomac;	And if no such accidents occur, then it should be done after three or more years, and the patient lies on his back, and has his hands on his stomach.
et met desoz l’ajutoire I cussin plain de laine igalment, et regarde chescune houre dou jor ou de la nut, que li figure dou membre brisiet ne se mueve, ou ne soit amollis li liiens;	And put the helper in a simple linen bandage, and observe every hour or half an hour, that the broken limb does not move, or is not loose in the joints.
si l’adrece par la vertu de medicine, et li done la viande que nos avons devant mis, en teil maniere que li viande soit au premier subtilz;	If it is addressed by the virtue of medicine, and the meat is cut in this manner, so that the meat is first divided into small pieces.
et quant il comance a reprendre, si soit grosse.	And when he wants to take it back, if it is large.
Et est costume que li ajutoire et li jambe doient estre repris en XL jors dou tout;	It is customary that the helper and the leg should be returned in XL jors all the time.
et adonques lou doit on desliier et aministrer bain et medicines d’oignemens por le leu adrecier.	and therefore it must be deslided and given baths and ointments for the leg to be cared for.
Et se li estricture est laide et emboee, si demore a desliier L jors ou II mois.	And if the structure is stiff and thick, it should be eased and delayed for 40 days or 2 months.
de la brisure du bras	of the fracture of the arm.
Li bras est compos de II os, qui sont apelez li dui «foscile», de coi li uns est petis, et est cil qui enseut le pouchet;	The arm is composed of two bones, which are called the "foscile" ones, and some are smaller, and it is this that forms the pouch.
et li autres est grans, et est cil qui est desoz, devers lou petit doi;	and the others are large, and it is this that is opposite to the small one.
par aventure brise li grans foscile soulement, ou li petis, et par aventure andui ensamble.	by chance, only the large bone breaks, or the small one, and by chance they come together.
Quant li petis fosciles est brisiez, li restaurations est legiere, et li sanations;	When the child's teeth are broken, the restoration is light and the healing.
et quant li grans est brisiez, si est li sanation male, et plus griés que quant il sont brisiez andui ensamble.	And when the large ones are broken, if it is not a good healing, and more crooked than when they were broken together.
Se c’est li petis foscile qui est brisiez soulement, si le covient poc estendre legierement, et mettre igal.	If it is only the small teeth that are broken, then it will be sufficient to extend lightly and put even.
Et se c’est li grans foscile, si le covient estraindre plus fort;	And if it is the large tooth, then it must be tightened more strongly.
et l’estende sus I cussin, et teigne le pouchet de la main plus haut des autres, et li petis dois plus bas des autres dois, et soit li malaides croisiez sus lui meisme, et I cussin devant lui plus haut, que li malaides ne soffre nule labor;	And extend it over the fingers, and raise the palm of the hand higher than the others, and the teeth must be lower than the others, and it should be crooked on itself, and the cusps in front of it higher than the others, so that the patient suffers no pain.
puis estende li ministres som bras a la partie desoz a sa main, ou a I liien, et uns autres ministres a I autre au desus.	Then extend the ministers of his arm to the opposite side of his hand, or to the other side of the elbow, and some other ministers to the other side.
Et puis le mette li mires igal, selonc sa millor forme.	And then he places the bone in its place, according to its best form.
Et se en la brisure a pieces, si met chescune en son leu, et s’il en i a nule desevree ke poigne lou keur, et tu ne la pues restorer en son leu, si fent sus et l’oste, si com nos avons dit devant.	And if it is in pieces, then he puts each piece in its place, and if there are no loose ends that point to the bone, and you cannot restore it to its place, then as we have said before, set the bone and the fracture.
Et se avec la briseure a plaie, je en ai parleit au chapistre singuler;	And if with the force of the wound, I have spoken to the single chapter.
si pren la cure.	If it is taken care of.
Et se en l’encomencement dou restorement sorvient apostemes chaus, si glue I drapeil de cerote fait d’oile roset et de cire blainche, que ne soit mie ne trop durs ne trop molz;	And if at the beginning of restoration, post-operative scars appear, which are made from ointment made of rose oil and warm wax, which is neither too hard nor too soft, nor too sticky.
et lie I drapeil par sus subtilment, tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez.	and it is gently covered until the post-operative scars are soothing.
Et puis oste lou cerote, et i met l’emplaustre de la poudre dou molin avec abun d’uef, pues met les esteles, et soit li estele de la briseure adés plus fors, et un poc plus large que les autres;	And then the bone is cut, and he puts the template of the powdered flour with a lot of urine, because it sets the stitches, and it should be the shoulder of the bracelet that is larger than the others.
et saiches que il doit avoir VI esteles ou bras em plusors dispositions:	and he asks if it needs six stitches or arms in more positions.
soit que li briseure soit en l’un des os, soit en II;	So that the bracelet is either in one of the bones, or in two.
et estraint plus sus la briseure que autre part, et toz jors moins en aloignant, si com j’ai dit au comencement dou chapistre;	And it is drawn more on the bracelet than elsewhere, and less by moving it away, as I said at the beginning of this chapter.
et soient li drapelz que sont sus la briseure molz et moistes, et ne soient mie dur ne aspres;	And the clothes that are on the bracelet are wet and slippery, and are not hard or rough.
et soit li filz, dont il est estrains, de lin, ne trop gros ne trop menus, si com nos avons dit.	And let the child, whose parents are far away, be born with a large or small body, as we have said.
Et rewarde lou membre et lou liien aprés aucuns jors.	And reward the member and the limb after some years.
Et se aucuns mavais accidens vient au membre, si com prurite ki vient au membre, si covient que tu aroses lou membre d’aigue chaude, tant que cil prurites soit apaisiez;	If any accidents come to the member, if itching comes to the member, and you must heat the member with hot water as long as the itching is calmed.
et laisse le membre ne mie estroit reposer.	and let the member rest without being stretched.
Et puis rencomence l’estrignement, et se li liiens est amolis et li os desevrez, et semblant chose, si l’adresce.	And then resume the stretching, and if the limbs are softened and the bones are exposed, and it seems like something, if it is removed.
Et se pren warde se li norrissemens ne puet venir au membre, por ceu qu’il est trop estrois, si covient que tu l’amollisses I poc, et laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant que li norrissemens i corre, et puis l’estraint.	And if the knots do not come to the member because it is too tight, because of which it is necessary that you loosen it immediately, and let it rest for a while until the knots are untied, and then stretch it.
Et se nules de ces choses que nos avons dit ne vient au malaide, si ne lou desliier jusc’a XX jors.	And if none of these things happen to the patient within twenty years, it is not our fault.
ou enqui entor, puis li pent les mains a son col, et soit ses cols igalz, et se warde de movement et de degitement, et dorme sus son dos;	Or if you are in pain, then you can put your hands on your chest, and make sure your shoulders are level, and move slowly and gently, and sleep on your back.
et saiches que ceste briseure est restoree en XXX jors ou en XXXV, et par aventure en XX jors, selonc les compositions et les complexions des vertus.	And this cauterization is restored in XXX years or XXXV years, and by chance in XX years, according to the compositions and complexions of the virtues.
de la brisure de la main	of the shoulder dislocation
Saiches que au dos de la main et as nous des dois avient poc de briseures, et n’i vient mais que ploieure maintes fois.	Be cautious that on the back of the hand, and in the wrist, there are few dislocations, and only slight pain comes from it, many times.
Et quant li plante de la main est brisie ou ploie, si covient que li malaides siece croisiet, et siet droitement devant lui igalement;	When the bone of the hand is broken or crushed, if the patient is able to hold it steady, and holds it firmly in front of them.
puis met sa main sus la toie estendue, et estende li ministres les os brisiez, et les mete igalz li mires, tant qu’il soient bien joint;	Then the patient places their hand on the extended bone, and extends the fingers of the broken bones, and places them evenly in the joints, as long as they are well connected.
et met l’emplastre et les estoupes, se apostemes n’i vient, puis i met une estele selonc la quantiteit dou leu;	And they apply the plaster and bandages, if necessary, and then place an elephant according to the quantity of the limb.
et soit envoloupee en I drapeil de lin.	And it is wrapped in a single layer of linen.
Et se li briseure est au pardedens entor lou ventre de la plante, si fai une spere de drapelz, et comande au malaide qu’il l’estrigne a sa plante brisie;	And if the fracture is at the side of the plantar arch, I make a spool of linen, and instruct the patient to stretch it over their broken plant.
et puis l’estrain d’un lonc drapeil, et soit li estele de keur souef ausi grans com li plante de la main, et l’estraint, si com il covient.	and then the strain of a long loose hair, and it is the weight of the hair as heavy as that of the hand, and it is stretched, if it can be.
Et se li brisure est au defuer, si covient que tu mettes une estele sus, et une autre desoz en la plante, si que li mains soit overte et droite, puis le lie tot entor la main, et estanche lou liien entre les dois.	If the fracture is at the hip, then if you can place a splint on it, and another in the foot, if the hand is straight and erect, then the leg will be completely fixed between the two.
Et se li briseure vient a aucun des nous des dois, se c’est li pouchés, si le met igal, si com il covient;	And if the cauterization comes to none of us on both sides, if it is closed, then it is tightened, if it can be;
et l’estraint avec la plante, et se tu vues si met une estele droite petite por lever la briseure, et ne se mueve;	and it is stretched with the hand, and if you see if it makes a right small thumb to raise the cauterization, and does not move;
et se li brisure est as autres dois, si com en l’indice ou l’un des autres, si le met igal, et lou lie avec lou doi sain qui est aprés;	and if the cut is on both sides, if it is as in the index or one of the others, if it is tightened, and it is held with the healthy hand that follows;
ou tu les lie toz en I tenant, que mues vaut, ou tu met sus une estele, si com ou pouchet;	If you tie them all in one place, according to their value, or if you put them on a scale, as you would;
et pren warde en la restauration et en la disposition d’aposteme chaut, et secor ceu qui i vient, si com j’ai dit.	and take care in the restoration and positioning of the incised abscess, and cut off what comes, as I have said.
de la cuixe brisie	Of the broken joint
Li os de la cuixe est maintes fois brisiez, et bien le voit on quant elle torne devant et derrier;	The bone of the thumb is often broken in many places, and it can be seen when it turns forward and backward.
et li restauration si est c’on lie I liien desus la briseure, et I autre desoz.	and the restoration if it is tied with the pieces of the fracture, and the other is loose.
Et li malaides gise sus sa faice, puis estende chescuns ministres son lien a sa part igalment;	And the patient lies on their face, then extends each member of its link to their equal part;
et c’est quant li brisure est emmi l’os.	And it happens when the fracture is broken from the bone.
Et se li brisure est prochiene a la racine de la cuixe, si soit li uns des liiens devers lou poignil, et li autres liiens desoz la briseure.	And if the break is near the root of the joint, then one or more of the ligaments will be torn in the direction of the point, and the others will be left alone.
Et ausi s’elle est prochiene au genoil, et adonques soit li liens delez lou genoil, et soit li extension aval;	And as it reaches the joint, then loosen the knot of the knee, and also extend the leg.
puis mette li mires l’os igal a ses II mains, tant qu’il soit selonc sa figure natureil, et puis met l’emplaustre, et lou lie, se apostemes chaz n’i vient.	Then place the bones of the bone equally in both hands, according to its natural shape, and then place the splint, and the patient should not move.
Et s’il i a aposteme chaut, si le laisse apaisier puis revien a ton ovraige et a ta cure;	And if it has stopped bleeding, then let it rest for a while and return to your work and your care.
li lieure est faite en teil maniere.	The bandage is made in parts.
Il covient que tu envoloupes sus la briseure I bendeil dur doublé en II ou III, et en demoure li superfluitez, puis torne la jambe tant que li talons veigne a la racine de la naige, et boute I fil lonc entre la cuixe et la jambe, delez lou genoil desoz, et veignent li chief dou fil au desus;	It is necessary that you wrap it around the fracture, doubling it in II or III, and removing the excess, then bend the leg until the heel comes to the root of the nail, and tie the long end between the thighs and the leg, loosening the knee joint, and they should come together at the knee;
puis torne sus la jambe et sus la cuixe le bendeil, puis met sus la briseure esteles, et met une estele sus l’os de la jambe;	Then turn the leg and the thigh of the leg, then put the splint on, and put a bandage on the bone of the leg.
puis emple le leu vuit entre la jambe et la cuixe de drapelz souef por mettre igal l’estrignement, puis comence a liier forment III tors ou IIII sus la briseure;	Then use the fifth leg between the thigh and the thigh of the cloth so that it fits evenly under the bandage, then begin to tie the knots three or four times on the splint.
et quant plus vas en sus de la briseure, et moins l’estraint;	And as more is added to the splint, the bandage loosens less.
puis enten as II chiés dou fil que tu as bouteit entre la jambe et la cuixe, et en lie III esteles que sont desus, puis revai au desoz au chief dou fil, tant que tu veignes delez le piet;	Then take the second pair of ropes that you have tied between the thigh and the thigh, and tie three knots on the ones that are already there, then return to the end of the cord at the foot of the second pair, as long as you see the pulley.
et l’estraint, si qu’il ne se mueve de son leu, puis le laisse ensi, puis k’il n’i vient ne aposteme ne enfleure n’autre semblant.	And if it does not move from its place, then let it go, and then it will not have any abscess or swelling or other sign.
Et s’il i avient, si le deslie, et adresce ceu que i vient, si com nos avons dit maintes fois;	And if it comes, and it is addressed as it comes, just as we have said many times.
et se il i a pieces de l’os que poigne, si le covient ewer, s’om puet;	And if it has pieces of bone that prick, then it can be set; and it can be done.
et s’on ne puet, si covient fendre le leu, et traire fuer;	And if it cannot be, then the shoulder must be cut, and drained.
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant k’il soit sanez.	And the treatment will be as we have said, as long as it is healthy.
Et aucune fois est brisie li cuixe ensi c’on i met esteles, si com en l’ajutoire et ou bras;	And never has the elbow been broken in place when we put the splint on it, as in the shoulder and arm.
toutevoie, en la restauration ensi faite ne cloche mie li malaides.	The first sentence to translate is: "Toutevoie, en la restauration ensi faite ne cloche mie li malaides.
Et saiches que li cuixe est restoree en L jors, ou poc moins ou poc plus, selonc les diversitez des complexions.	And advises that the cheek is restored in L years, or less than less, according to the different complexions.
de la ruelle dou genoil	Of the right knee joint
Saiches que en la ruelle dou genoil avient poc brisure, mais elle ploie maintes fois.	It is said that in the right knee joint there is little fracture, but it bends many times.
Et s’elle brise, si n’est mais c’une fendure, ou I pertus, et avient a tout plaie, et sens plaie, et ce sent om bien.	And if it breaks, whether it is only a sprain or a puncture, and it comes to all wounds and hurts, and it feels well.
Et li restauration si est c’on mette igal ceu qui est rons a ses dois, tant qu’il soit assemblez mues c’on puet;	And the restoration is when you put the hair back in its place as soon as it has grown evenly on both sides, as long as it can be gathered together.
puis met l’emplaustre, et i met une estele reonde, se tu en as mestier, et l’estraint si com il covient, puis rewarde toutes les dispositions que nos avons dit ens autres briseures, si com aposteme chaut et autre semblant;	Then apply the cautery, and use a round stylus, if you are skilled at it, and pull on it as necessary, then reward all the adjustments we have mentioned for other fractures, such as wounds and other appearances.
si met a chescun accident ceu k’il li covient, tant qu’il soit sanez.	if you apply to each accident what is necessary, as long as it is healthy.
de la brisure de la jambe	Of the break of the leg
Saiches que en la jambe ait II os, de coi li uns est apelez par droit non «mustelz», et li autres est apelez «foscile»;	It is said that in the leg there are two bones, of which one is called by right "muscatel" and the other is called "fascicule.
et avient tout auteil briseure com il vient au bras, et por ceu est li restauracion si com celle dou bras igalment, et li ovraiges est tout i. Et se li dui os sont brisiet ensamble, si torne li jambe de toutes pars.	When the wrist is broken, as it comes to the arm, and for this reason, it is restored in the same way as the other arm. If both bones are broken together, then turn the leg of all parts.
Et se li os subtilz est brisiez, si torne devant.	And if the subtle bones are broken, then turn forward.
Et se li gros os est brisiez, si sent on grant dolor, et le voit on bien;	And if the large bones are broken, it feels great pain, and one sees that it is well.
et torne desoz.	and turn around.
Adonques amenistre extension, et le met igal, et lie les esteles igalement;	After stretching it, put it in place, and straighten the limbs evenly.
mais toutevoie, il covient se li brisure est laide, et il i a plusors pieces, que li extension soit menor et plus legiere;	But it is necessary to make the fracture look good, and if there are more pieces, then the extension should be less severe and lighter.
et l’alige selonc ta vertu.	And the alige according to your virtue.
Et quant tu as tout acomplit ton ovraige, si pren II faixes de fust chevees que porpreignent la jambe d’une part et d’autre, et soient dou lonc de la jambe des le genoil jusque desoz;	And when you have completed your work, if you take two pieces of twisted hair that prick the leg on both sides and are long enough to reach from the knee to the ankle.
puis envoloupe en II leus I bendeil desus et desoz, et le lie em mileu ausi, et a ceste lieure ne pora li jambe decliner a destre ne a senestre, et ensi est bien;	Then wrap the leg with II the bend and from the knee to the ankle, and tie it tightly, and at this time do not let the leg sway to the right or left, and it is well.
et aucun i aministrent I bers dou lonc de la jambe, et s’est de fust, et i met on la jambe por warder de movement, et proprement fait on ceu en la brisure ou il a plaie;	And no one maintains the length of the leg, and it is of hair, and it is tied on the leg to prevent movement, and this is done properly at the fracture or wound.

si le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	if the treatment is healthy.
de la brisure des os dou piet	Of the break of the bones of the shoulder
A la cheville ne vient point de brisure, mais as os dou piet vient aucune fois brisure et as dois poc, et n’i avient fuer que quassure em plusor dispositions.	At the ankle, there is no break, but the bones of the shoulder never break and must be very strong, and they only crack in more positions.
Et s’il avient as os dou piet brisure, et tu vois ces os sormonter l’un l’autre, si mette si malaides som piet sus la terre, ausi com s’il voloit aler, et puis met maintenant ton piet sus lou sien, lai ou li os sont levez, puis le presse tant k’il reveignent en lor leus;	And if there are many broken bones, and you see the bones thrusting against each other, if you put them in the earth as much as possible, just like when you run, then place your foot on the ground, and then lift the bones as much as they can fit in their sockets;
puis met l’emplaustre et estoupes sus, et met desoz lou ventre dou piet une petite tauble a II chiés plains, puis l’estraint au piet avenanment, puis que tu as envoloupez drapelz entor, et autres choses dont tu as mestier.	then place the splint and stitch it on, and then make a small tableau at the bottom of the chest, then pull it to the foot, then wrap the cloth around the foot, and other things that you have skill in.
Et quant III jors ou IIII seront passez, si deslie lou liien, car tu troveras les os igalz, soient brisiez, soient desaluez.	And when three or four days have passed, if the bone is not healed, for you will find that the bones are broken and dislocated.
Et s’il i a aucuns des dois brisiez, si les restoure, si com nos avons dit as dois de la main;	If there are any of the two breaks, if they are restored, if we have said so, you must do it with your hand.
puis met au doi brisiet une estele selonc la longesce dou doi, et soit un poc plus large, puis met desoz le piet celle tauble que j’ai dit, et l’estrain avenanment;	Then place the other end of the stitch according to the length of the first, and make a larger pocket, then pull the thread that I have mentioned, and tighten it evenly.
et s’il en i a II ou III, ou plus, brisiez, si met sus chescun doi une estele selonc sa quantiteit, envoloupee en I drapeil de lin, et estraint la tauble desoz lou piet;	And if there are more than two or three breaks, if you place one stitch according to the quantity of each, wrapped in a single layer of linen, and tighten the knot of the thread.
et soit estans sus lou chief de la tauble defuer lou ventre dou piet, si qu’il le teigne bien.	And if you are hanging the end of the stitch below the belly of the knot, so that it does not burn.
Et covient que tu n’oblier mie les autres choses que j’ai dit as autres briseures, des que nos avons dit;	It is necessary that you do not overlook the other things I have said about other fractures, as soon as we have said them.
et secor chescun accident si com il covient.	And cut off every accident as it comes.
de la brisure de l’os dou poignil	of the fracture of the small finger
Quant li os de la nature la femme est brisiez, si la fai seoir enlargie, puis l’encline a la partie dou dos, et soit tenue par derrier;	When the bone of the female pelvis is broken, if it is made larger, it then leans towards the painful side, and should be held by the buttocks.
puis emplisse li baile la nature de la malaide de couton, et en i mette ausi gros com I sto;	Then fill the gap in the nature of the cloth-making woman's leg with a thick piece as I have.
puis deboute la femme, et lieve lou dos poc et poc, et adonques saut li coton, tant qu’il vient a l’entree de la nature, et revient li os avec lou sto;	Then bend the woman, and gently bend the back little by little, and then pull out the cloth-making woman's leg as much as it enters the nature, and return the bone with the thick piece.
et quant elle vuet pissier, si oste lou coton, et quant elle a pissiet, se li remette, et ensi faice VII jors ou entor:	And when it sees blood, if the bone is loose, and when it bleeds, it is reset, and then it takes seven days or more to heal.
si sera restoree li brisure, et se tu vues, pren une vessie de berbis, et lie au pertus une cainne, et boute toute la vessie en la nature;	If the fracture is reset, and if you see, take a bowl of milk, and tie it around the wound, and pour all the milk into the nature.
puis soffle en la cainne forment, tant que li vessie soit enflee dedens:	Then blow into the bandage as much as the milk is absorbed from the wound.
la nature si revenra li brisure;	The nature will then heal the fracture.
puis soit emplie de coton, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then it should be filled with cotton, and left alone for seven days, as long as it is healthy.
Et quant li os dou poignil de l’ome est brisiez, ou de la femme, si le restoure ensi com nos avons dit en l’os de la hainche;	When the bone of the arm is broken, or of the woman, if it is restored as we have said in the bone of the thigh.
et ne sont mie occultees ces briseures prochienes a celui qui i met son estude et son us, et entent mon livre.	These fractures are not uncommon to those who study and use it, and they read my book.

de brisure avec plaie	Of a fracture with wound
Il covient a celui qui a brisure avec plaie, meismement s’elle est grans, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire ou semblant, qu’il soit sainiez maintenant, si que les sainies que nos avons dit le tesmoignent.	It is necessary for the one who has a fracture with wound, even if it is large, whether it is the bone of the shoulder or the helper, or seeming, that they are now healthy, if those wounds that we have said testify.
Et se li plaie saine, si la restainche de vitriole, se tu n’as autre chose, puis rencomence a restorer la briseure en cele meisme houre, ou celui jor, se apostemes chaus n’i vient.	And if the healthy wound is that it re-bleeds, if you have nothing else, then continue to restore the fracture in the same hour, or the next day, if the patient does not die.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si laisse la restauration jusc’a nuevime jor, tant que li apostemes soit apaisiez, et n’i touchier ne au tier jor ne au quart, car tu i feroies venir malvais accident.	And if the patient does not die, then leave the restoration for the next day, as long as the patient is calm and does not touch it again on the third or fourth day, because you will cause other accidents to happen.
Et se li os brisiez est aparans sus lou keur descovert, si covient que tu lou mettes a point legierement a tes mains, a extension petite.	If the bone is broken, it is located at the point discovered, so you should place it lightly in your hands, with a small extension.
Et se li extensions ne t’est apareillie por mettre igal a tes mains, si le ramoine a cest estrument qui est de fer, qui a VII dois ou VIII de lonc, et li largesce est selonc la quantiteit de la plaie;	And if the extensions are not apparent for you to make them even with your hands, if the rammer has this instrument which is of iron, which is seven or eight inches long, and the size is according to the quantity of the wound.
et por ceu est mestier au mire qu’il empreigne III ou IIII, selonc ceu qu’il en ait mestier en chescune cure de briseure;	and therefore it is necessary to prick three or four times, according to how much he has experience in each case of fracturing.

et le boute a une fois, tant k’il reviegne, et soit igalz l’un encontre l’autre.	And the bone heals once, as long as it regrows, and it is even in comparison to the other.

The second line of the text is translated as: "And if the fracture is subtle, and the bandages cannot well hold the bone, then it is necessary to cover the top of the bone with the bandage, as long as the bandages have power.

When you see after the first or second day that the wound has healed completely, and if you have used antiseptic cream on it, and you have applied a salve to relieve pain, which is a safe and effective remedy, then proceed with the following steps.

par aventure cherra par lui aprés XX jors ou XXX, puis cure la plaie, se tu pues;	by chance heals by him after 20 years or 30, then treat the wound, if you can.
et se tu ne pues, si la laisse.	and if you cannot, then leave it.
des brus qui vienent sor la sodure	The first sentence to translate is "des brus qui viennent sortre la sodure". The translation is
Nous vienent maintes fois aprés la santeit de la briseure, meismement quant c’est pres de la jointure, et laide chose est a veoir li figure dou membre;	Many times after the fracture of the break, but when it is near the joint, and one should see the appearance of the limb.
et par aventure ne puet faire li membres ses ovraiges naturelz.	And by chance, it cannot make the limbs its natural position.

si li aministre medicines stiptiques, si com aloes, encens, et mirre, et sarcocolle, acaice, et semblans autres, ensi que tu preignes aucune de ces choses, ou toutes ensamble, et les confit avec vin stiptique ou avec abun d’uef ou avec aisil;	If you have applied friction medicines such as aloes, incense, and myrrh, and senna, and similar others, if you do not take any of these, or all together, and mix them with warm wine or with enough beer or with vinegar;

ou tu estrain sus une piece de plonc bien faite;	If you strain a well-made piece of cloth.
car li proprietez dou plonc si est qu’il oste toutes les enfleures desus les membres;	Because the property of the cloth is that it all the folds of the members.
et se li nodation est ja convertie en durteit ausi com piere, et il est besoing de l’oster, si la cope desus, et fent la superfluiteit apparent;	And if the nodding is already converted into hardness as a piercing, and it is sore to the finger, then the crown of it, and makes the superfluity appear.
ou tu la reis a aucun raseur, tant qu’ele soit ostee, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee.	Or you shave it as soon as it is healed, and the care as soon as it is healthy.
dou membre qui est foibles aprés la garison	The first sentence to translate is "dou membre qui est foibles après la garison". The translation is: "the
Quant li brisure de l’os est restoree, et demoure aprés li membres foibles et subtilz, si avient por mout de causes:	When the fracture of the bone is restored, and it becomes less after the weak and subtle members, if it comes from various causes.
de coi l’une est por ceu qu’il fut liiez trop estroit, et ne fut mie liiez si com il covenoit;	If one of the bones is because it was too tightly tied, and was not properly cut as it should be.
ou por ceu qu’il i ot trop de liiens, et ne pooit venir li norrissemens au membre;	Or because it had too many knots, and could not come to the joint of the member.
ou por multitude d’arosement;	Or due to a large number of knotting.
ou por trop grans movements, ne mie en son houre;	Or because of too many movements at once, he did not hold his breath well.
ou por ceu qu’il a poc de sanc en son cors, si est foibles.	Or because there was little blood in his chest, which is weak.
Et li cure si est que tu faices mengier le malaide, et faire le cors tendre, tant que li sans soit multipliiez en lui;	And if the treatment is that you make the patient lie down and tighten the cloth around the chest until it no longer multiplies in him.
et li aministre bain, et li done joie et liesce;	And he is given water, and he then feels better and relieved.
puis met poix sus le membre, si que li poix atraie a li grant norrissement, et l’arose sovent d’aigue tede, tant que li norrissement corre au membre;	Then he places salt on the member, if it draws out the swelling, and the blisters often form at the great pain point, until the swelling reaches the member.
et reviegne a sa figure natureil.	and he is reshaped to his natural shape.
dou membre tort aprés la santeit	The dislocated limb after the injury
Quant li membres est tors aprés la restauration, et li os brisiez apert, et li forme dou membre est laide, toutevoie ne pert mie son ovraige natureil:	When the limbs are twisted after reshaping, and the bones are broken open, and the formed member is crooked, it does not follow its natural shape.
si ne croire mie les folz qui dient c’on doit brisier lou membre tout de noveil, et maint fol mire ont ce fait en nostre terre;	If one does not believe the words of those who say that the limb must be broken in several places, and many others have done this in our land.
et cist ovraiges est blamez, et en vient grans malz, et par aventure li mors;	And the first part of the treatment is blamed, and great harm comes to it, and by chance the patient dies.
toutevoie, se li nodations et li torture sont fres, si covient k’il soient arosez d’aigue chaude, ou herbes mollifians soient cuites, si com foilles de vismalve, et racines, et mellilote, et semblans choses;	However, if the wounds and tortures are fresh, and they are not washed with hot water, or herbs that soften are cooked, like figs of vismalk, and roots, and honey-like substance, and similar things;
et li fai I emplaustre mollificatif, si com dyaquilon bien fait, et tu pren le muscillaige de vismalve, et la confit avec graisse de geline ou oile de sisament, et fai emplaustre sus;	and the second part of the treatment is a mollifying agent, if well made, and you take the vismalk fat, and cook it with linseed oil or sesamum oil, and apply it;
ou tu pren figues graisses, et les broie avec fien de colon, et semblans medicines que amenuisent le soudement.	or you take fat figs, and roast them with animal fat, and similar medicines that reduce the saliva;
Et aucune fois est ostee li nodacion por froter continuelment et longement a mains moistes.	And never is there a stop to the node when it is continued and long with wet hands.
Et soit amenistrez movement au membre chescune houre.	And let there be no movement in the limb at all hours.
Et se li tortuositez est enveillie et endurcie, ausi com piere, et besoins est de l’oster au fer, si la covient coper jusc’a l’os, a l’incisoire subtil legierement;	When the tortuosity is aroused and made rigid, as with an incision, and it is needed for the bone, if it comes close to the bone, under the subtle and light cut.
et mettre cusenson et estude en la cure.	and put on bandages and study in the treatment.
Ci encomence li livres des dislocations	This begins the book of dislocations.
Dislocations est issue d’aucune jointe de son leu, por coi il ne se puet muevre, et est li membres mal figurez, et sent li malaides grant dolor et grant lesion.	Dislocations occur when a joint moves out of its place, which prevents it from moving, and the limb is misaligned, causing the patient great pain and injury.
Quant dislocation vient a aucun, si le covient maintenant ramener sens targier.	When dislocation comes to none, if it comes now to bring sensation to the arm.
Car s’on tarde, si enfle li leus, et par aventure si le remet on a poines au leu;	For if we are late, if it swells, and by chance if we put it back on the shoulder.
por ceu ne covient mie c’on le mueve a l’oure k’il est enflez:	because it does not matter how we move it on the arm when it is swollen.
maintes fois fait venir spame et autres dolors;	Many times brought to vomit and other pains.
toutevoie, quant ce avenra, si fai sainier lou malaide, puis le laisse, tant que li apostemes chas soit apaisiez;	Indeed, when this happens, if I make the patient better, then let him leave, as long as he is calm.
puis arose le membre d’aigue chaude et d’oile, puis le ramoinne legierement, et cure chescun membre si com li cure venra en son leu.	Then the hot and oily member was raised, then it was gently reset, and each limb was treated as the patient's own limb had been treated.
Et j’ai ordenez les chapistres des dislocations des lou chief jusc’a piez.	I have ordered the chapters of shoulder dislocations by the pieces of bone.
des mandibules	by the mandibles
Poc avient que les mandibules soient desaluees andous, et li dislocations d’ambedous est selonc II manieres:	There came when the mandibles were dislocated, and the dislocation of both was in two ways:
ou elles sont un poc ostees de lor leus, et mollifies un poc;	either they are a small piece of their bones, and are made soft;
ou elles sont desaluees entierement, et pendent vers lou pis, et cort li salive de la bouche qu’il ne la puet tenir, ne ne puet clore sa bouche, et envoloupe sa langue avec la parole.	either they are entirely dislocated and hang downwards, and cut the saliva from the mouth that cannot hold it, nor can it close its mouth, and wrap around the tongue with speech.
Quant li dislocations est petite, si revient par li em plusors disposicions.	If the dislocation is small, it can return to its original position through various adjustments.
Et s’elle est entiere et acomplie, si covient que tu la ramoinne hastanment, et ne targier mie;	And if it is entire and accomplished, then you must reset it as soon as possible, and do not struggle.
et en tel maniere que li ministres teigne le chief dou malaide, et boute li mires som pochet de l’une de ses mains en la racine de la dislocation de la mandibule dedens la bouche, se li dislocations est de II pars;	And in such a way that the minister marks the head of the patient, and pokes the eyes with a small part of one of his hands at the root of the dislocation of the mandible, which causes the mouth to be closed by II parts;
et li autre doi des mains soient defuer, por mettre igal;	And the other two hands are deformed to make them equal.
et comande au malaide qu’il les amollisse, ses mandibules, et les mueve de toutes pars.	And instruct the patient to smooth out his cheeks, mandibles, and move them from all parts.
Et li mires la mete igal, tant qu’elle reveigne en son leu.	2. And the teeth are placed evenly, as they should be in his mouth.
Et se li ramener est griés, meismement se ce sont les II mandibules ensamble, si les arose d’aigue chaude et d’oile, tant que les ramoinnes legierement;	And if the cheek is twisted, then it is the same as the two mandibles being assembled, which are oiled with hot and oil blisters, until they are lightly twisted.
ne ne targier mie dou ramener, si com nos avons dit.	1. There is no need to force it, as we have said.
Et quant elles sont ramenees igalment, et li bouche dou malaide clot bien sens mollifiier, si met sus drapelz moilliez en cerote fait d’oile roset et de cire, puis le lie legierement de molz liiens;	6. And when they are returned in their place, and the patient's mouth feels relaxed, if you cover it with soft cloth made of oilcake and wax, then lightly bind it with threads;
et dorme li malaides sus son dos, et ses chiés soit estans entre II cussins, si qu’il ne lou mueve ne a destre ne a senestre, ne ne s’efforce mie de maixier, mais preigne legiere viande, tant que les dolors soient ostees, et soient noees les mandibules;	10. And let the patient sleep on his back, and the head between two pillows, if he does not move to the right or left, and does not strain himself, but eats light meat, as long as the pain is tolerable and does not affect the jaws;
et puis menjuce ce qu’il vuet legierement, et ne se travaille mie d’ovrir la bouche au mengier et au boivre, tant que li mandibule soit bien noee et sanee.	And then he cuts what he can see lightly, and does not strive to open the mouth with his finger and drink, as long as the mandible is well nourished and healthy.
Et se les II mandibules ne pueent estre remises a point a une houre, et ne sont mie converties a lor leus, si en vient fievres et sode acostumees, et par aventure solution de ventre, et par aventure vomist cole pure.	And if the two mandibles cannot be reinserted at once in an hour, and are not converted to their original shape, then if fevers and customary colds come on, and by chance the abdomen becomes distended, and by chance vomiting of pure bile occurs.
Et quant tu verras ceu, adonc saiches que c’est perdicions;	And when you see this, then you will know that it is a mistake.
et maintes fois muert cil cui il avient, en VIIII jors.	and many times died those who came, in nine years.
de la forcelle	of force.
Li forcele ne puet desaluer dou costeit dedens la continuation de li et dou pis, et est desaluee aucune fois au defuer, et bien le sent on.	The force cannot be dislodged from the cost, due to the continuation of the effort and the pain, and it is never loosened at the end, and it is felt to be so.
Et li restauration si est que li malaides gise sovin sor son dos, et estende ses bras;	And the restoration is that the patient lies on his back, and extends his arms.
et puis presse le leu forment a ta palme, et elle revenra;	and then press the limb firmly with your palm, and it will return.
puis met sus l’emplaustre et lou bendeil, et l’estraint;	then put on the splint and the bandage, and tighten it.
et li chiez qui est devers lou coute ne puet desaluer;	The head of the shoulder that is towards the chest cannot be reset.
se poc non, et se il desalue aucune fois, si le ramoinne a son leu, si com nos avons dit;	However, if it does not move at all, and if you reset it on your shoulder, as we have said.
puis met sus l’emplaustre et le bendeil, et l’estraint, et coumande au malaide qu’il se repose tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then place the cauterant and the bandage on it, and tighten it, and instruct the patient to rest as soon as they are able.
et ensi meisme est ramenez li chiés de l’espale, quant il est desevrez de son leu.	And then you should return the head of the shoulder to its place when it is out of your shoulder.
de la dislocation de l’espaule	Of the dislocation of the shoulder
Saiches que li espaule n’est desaluee fuer que selonc III manieres:	It is said that the shoulder is not dislocated unless it follows three methods.
de coi l’une est qu’ele desalue a la partie de l’assele au desoz;	The first method is that it dislocates at the part of the bone near the socket.
et li seconde est a la partie dou pis;	The second sentence translates to: "and it is at the lower part of the foot.
et par aventure desalue a la partie desus, et ceu avient poc;	The third sentence translates to: "and by chance it was dislocated in the heel, and it happened little.
et ne desalue mie derrier por l’espaule, et ne desalue mie dedens por les ners;	The fourth sentence translates to: "and did not dislocate the shoulder or the arm from the elbow.
et plusors fois desalue desoz vers l’assele, meismement a ces qui ont poc de char, car a ces saut ele fuer hastanment;	The fifth sentence translates to: "and more often it dislocated the knee towards the ankle, even those who have little strength, because in this jump it was most dangerous.
a ces qui ont assez char, saut ele a poines, et rentre a poines.	The sixth sentence translates to: "for those who had some strength, the jump was not high, and it returned low.
Et par aventure avient a aucuns homes percussion ou casseure, et enfle li espaule d’un aposteme chaut, et cuide qu’elle est desaluee par ceu.	And by chance it happens to some men that they strike or crush their shoulder, and stretch out the shoulder with an abscess, and take care to have it dislocated by this.
Il covient donques que tu l’esprueves, tant que tu en soies certains;	It is necessary that you try it, as long as you are sure.
et adonques encomence la cure.	And therefore, begin the treatment.
Et est conue li dislocations quant il est aval vers l’assele, et met difference entre l’espaule malade et la saine, et tu troveras entre lor diversiteit manifeste;	And when the dislocation occurs as it moves towards the axle, and you make a distinction between the diseased shoulder and the healthy one, and you will find between them a clear difference.
et troveras au chief de l’espaule une fosse, et desoz l’assele au tochier le chief de l’espaule, ausi com se ce soit uns oes;	and you will find at the head of the shoulder a fissure, and then pull the axle towards the head of the shoulder, as if it were some ones;
et ne puet li malaides ramener sa main a son neis, ne movoir de nulz movemens;	and the patient cannot bring his hand to his side, and make no movements;
et ausi, s’elle est desaluee en haut, si n’est mie occultee, car tu le trueves manifestement au tochier;	and if it is dislocated above, then it is not hidden, because you can clearly see it at the axle;
et ceste maniere de dislocation n’est mie fors a ramener, quant elle est novele, ou se li enfes est malaides.	For this manner of dislocation is not difficult to correct when it is new, or if the child is healthy.
Et li maniere est que li ministres lieve la main dou malaide en haut, puis met tes peuchas desoz l’assele, et lieve la jointure a force en haut au leu;	And the manner is to gently hold the hand of the sick child at the top, then pull your thumbs apart, and gently bend the joint at the top of the arm.
et li ministres lieve la main, et l’estende en haut, pues le mette desoz;	And he holds the hand gently, extends it upwards, then places it apart.
si venra hastanment.	If help comes.
Et s’elle ne vient si com nos avons dit em mains jors aprés, si covient ke li malaides soit baigniez en aigue chaude;	And if it does not come as we have said in our hands, then it is necessary that the child be bathed in warm water.
et li amenistre arosement mollifiant et assouajant, si com decoction de altee et de fenugrec et de mellilote en aigue, et soit amenistree;	And the ointment is made of soft and soothing ingredients, such as honey and fenugreek and honey in warm water, and it is applied.
puis soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos, et mette on desoz l’assele un sto de lainne igal, ne trop mol ne trop dur, puis mette li mires son talon sus le sto, et lieve le chief de l’espaule vertuousement, et traie la main dou malaide;	Then let the patient lay down on his back, and place a pillow under his head evenly, neither too hard nor too soft, then place the foot of his leg on the pillow, and gently lift the shoulder of the upper arm, and hold the hand of the patient.
et uns autres ministres teigne lou chief dou malaide, si qu’il ne se mueve aval;	and some other assistants smooth the shoulder of the upper arm, if it does not move at all.
celle espaule revient tout maintenant, et se tu vues si le ramoinne selonc ceste maniere:	That shoulder is now back, and if you see that the dislocation is reset in this way:
et est que tu faices estre present I home qui soit plus grans que li malaides;	and it is that you are present with homes that are larger than the shoulders.
et soit drois devers lou costeit, et boute s’espaule desoz l’assele dou malaide, et lieve l’assele en haut, si que li malaides pende en l’ar;	and it is that there are two directions to the costeit, and bolt the shoulder under the pillow of the patient's arm, and gently lift the pillow above the shoulder, so that the shoulders hang in the arm.
et uns autres ministres traie la main dou malaide aval devers lou ventre.	And some other hands treat the patient's hand down towards the belly.
Et se li malaides est trop legiers, si pent avec lui aucune chose pesant, et li dislocation revient maintenant.	If the patient is too light, and there is nothing heavy with it, then the dislocation returns now.
Et le ramoinne on ausi en autre maniere:	And it is also done in another way:
et est c’on fiche I lonc tison en terre, dont li chiés soit ausi reons com I pistal, et ne soit ne trop gros ne trop graile;	And it is also done by cutting a long thick thread, whose ends are tied like a pistil, and not too large or too thin:
puis soit mis desoz lou malaide, mais k’il ait drapelz souef sus, et li malaides soit estans dou lonc dou fust;	Then it is placed on the patient's hand, but if it has been too long, and the hand is too long and thin:
puis soit estendue sa main aval d’autre part forment, et li jointure revenra en son leu hastanment;	Then it is extended from the other side of the hand, and the joint returns to its original position:
et s’elle ne vuet revenir por toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si fai ceste cure:	And if it does not return to its original position for all these things that we have said, then this cure is not effective:
pren I tison de II bras de grant et IIII dois de large, qui ait le chief reont por mues entrer em parfont desoz l’assele, selonc ceste forme:	The first line of the text can be translated as: "Take two strips of cloth from the left arm, four inches wide, which will fit around the ankle, according to this form:".
puis lie sus le chief dou fust drapelz souez, que li fust ne blece lou malaide, puis le met desoz l’assele dou malaide;	The second line of the text can be translated as: "Then wrap it around the ankle, making sure it is not too tight on the patient, then place it below the ankle".
et estende som bras sus le fust dou lonc, et lie l’ajutoire sus le fust, et lou bras au chief de la main, puis met le bras sus I eschillon d’une eschiele dou large, et soit estendue li mains aval, et soit laissiez li cors pendans d’autre part:	The third line of the text can be translated as: "And extend the arm above the elbow, then wrap the aid around the elbow, and the other end of the arm, then tie it with a large buttonhole, and leave the chest hanging from the other side".
li jointure reva ens maintenant.	The joint now reveals itself.
Et quant elle est ens, en quel maniere que ce soit, si covient que tu mettes desoz l’assele une spere de laine igal, puis met l’emplaustre aparilliet de poudre dou molin, avec encens et aubun d’uef, sus toute l’espaule et entor, puis l’estrain desoz l’assele avenanment, et torne le liien sus l’emplaustre, et embraice la main a son col, et soit li mains demorans ensi.	And when it is in place, in whatever way that may be, if you happen to put the palm of your hand a linen thread as even as possible, then place a sprinkle of flour on the mill with incense and wool all over the shoulder and around, then tighten the thread on the palm again, and turn the lace on the sprinkle, and wrap your hand around the arm at its collar, and let the hands remain still.
Et covient qu’il menjuce poc, tant que li membres soit confortez, car il sanera plus tost;	And it is necessary to dress it as little as possible, until the limb is comfortable, because it will heal faster.
et puis menjuce plus aprés V jors ou VII, et le mueve;	and then dress again after 5 or 7 days, and move it.
et s’il est fermeis et il n’est mollifiez, si est sanez.	And if it is tight and not softened, it will be cured.
Et se li jointure est fuer de leu por moistor que i est venue, ou por autre cause, si covient que tu i aministres cauteres a III pertus, si com il est mis devant ou chapistre des cauteres.	If the joint is swollen due to moisture or another reason, and it has not subsided after three days, then it is necessary to apply a cauterization at the third position, as shown in the chapter on cauterizations.
Et se tu fais tout ceu, et il deslie aprés VII jors, et li jointure ne se tient, et ne puet lever som bras amont, adonc saiches que li nerf au chief de l’espaule sont copeit ou estendut ou amollis;	And if you follow all of this, and after 7 weeks, the joint does not hold, and you cannot raise your arm forward, then you should suspect that the nerve at the top of the shoulder is compressed or extended or softened.
et saiches que li jointure n’iert jamais fichie en son leu.	And you should suspect that the joint never returns to its place in the shoulder.
Li dislocation qui est devers lou pis, et les mameles, ou derrier, si est faite par impulsion, et estendement de mains, et i aministre on autre lieure;	The dislocation that is towards the knee, and the thighs, or the buttocks, if it is made by impulse, and extension of hands, and it is maintained by another application;
et cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and be cured as soon as it is healthy.
Et se aprés la sanation vient grietez au membre, et tardemens em movement, si use li malaides bain maintes fois, tant que celle grietez soit alegie, et reviegne a sa premiere nature.	And after the healing comes pain in the limb, and later in movement, if the patient uses cold water many times, as long as that pain is not relieved, and returns to its original state.
de la dislocation dou coute	of the dear dislocation
Saiches que li jointure dou coute est desaluee a poinnes, et a poinnes revient;	If the joint that is difficult to move is dislocated several times, and it is dislocated again;
et s’est desaluee de toutes pars, et meismement devant et derrier, et li dislocations n’est mie reponue, car on la voit bien et sent bien;	and has become dislocated from all sides, and even front and back, and the dislocation is not well repaired because it is seen well and felt well;
et desalue selonc chescune figure.	and is dislocated according to each figure;
Et quant tu joins le coute malaide avec lou sain, si le pues veoir apertement.	And when you join the male member with the female, if you see it open wide.
Car li jointure est chevee, et ne puet ploier lou bras, ne touchier son espaule a tout.	For the joint is weak, and cannot grip the arm, nor touch the shoulder with anything.
Et covient que tu le ramoinnes ainsois que apostemes chaus i viegne, car se apostemes chaus i venoit, si seroit grief li ramener;	And it is necessary to reset it every time, even if the arrowhead comes out, because if the arrowhead comes out, it would be difficult to put it back in;
et par aventure ne puet estre ramenez dou tout en tout, meismement quant ele est au derrier;	And by chance, it cannot be returned to its original position, indeed when it is at the bottom.
si vaut pis que les autres dislocations, et est de plus grant dolor, et par aventure i vient li mors.	If it is worse than other dislocations, and it causes more pain, and by chance it comes to death.
Et li restauration si est, quant elle est telz c’on la puet ramener, que tu li estendes sa main a tes II mains;	And the reduction if it is, when it can be returned, you can extend your hand to your two hands.
et ses bras soit espandus, et les mains dou mire selonc le coute entor, desor et desoz, et boute la jointure a ses peuchas ensamble, ou a la racine de sa palme, tant qu’ele reviegne a son leu.	And the arms are expanded, and the hands are stretched according to the cost, from the top to the bottom, and the joint is held at its nook or at the root of the palm, as it returns to its place.
Et se li dislocations est au devant, si revient quant il double sa main a sa main, et fier de la racine de la palme lou coute qui est desaluez.	And if the dislocation is in front, then it returns when it doubles its hand to its hand, and proud of the root of the palm tree that is dislocated.
Et s’il ne vuet revenir au leu, si aministre fort extension;	And if it does not return to its place, apply strong extension.
et est que dui ministre estendent le bras, et le teignent dui ministre, si qu’il ne se mueve a l’estension;	and it is that two servants extend the arm, and hold it with two servants, so that it does not move during extension.
puis torne le bras de chescune part, puis que tu as envoloupeit un drapeil double lonc et large;	then turn the arm in each part, then wrap a long and wide strip around it.
et quant li mires a jointe la jointure a sa main, si l’oigne d’aucun oile por amolir la jointure, puis boute la jointure forment, tant qu’ele reviegne;	and when you see the joint of the joint in your hand, if there is no oil to lubricate the joint, then break the joint formation, as it reforms.
et quant elle est au leu, si met sus emplaustre sec avec aubun d’uef, et l’estrain forment, et pent le bras au col dou malaide, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le deslie.	and when it is at the shoulder, if it is covered with dry powder with beef dripping, and the formation is made, and the arm is tied at the neck of the patient, and some jors are left, then it is removed.
Et se li jointure est ferme en son leu, si deslie lou liien, et le laisse;	If the joint is closed in its place, and it is left alone, and it does not move.
et se tu vois que li jointure n’estrigne bien, si rencomence l’emplaustre et lou lien, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit fermement mis;	If you see that the joint is not tightening well, and it resumes the cauterization and the ligament, and it leaves for a while until it is firmly fixed.
puis le deslie.	Then it is left.
Et se il sent grieteit aprés le ramenement de la jointe, et elle se muet, si le baigne et frote bellement, et presse tant qu’il soit assouagiez;	If the patient feels pain after the dislocation of the joint, and it becomes still, if it is bathed and cleaned well, and pressed until it is calmed.
ou tu met sus la jointure une naige de mouton grasse, puis la laisse I jor et une nuit, puis l’oste, et lou fai entrer ou bain;	Or you can put a fat sheep's wool around the joint, then leave it for one night and the bone, and let it enter into a bath.
et quant il sue, se li frote la jointure tempreement, puis remet la naige sus, et puis entre ou bain;	When it happens, he should clean the joint immediately, then put on the splint again, and then take a bath.
et ensi fai II fois ou III, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And then repeat this 2-3 times until it is healthy.

si revenra a sa disposition.	if it returns to its original position.
li dislocation de la main	The dislocation of the hand.
Li jointure de la main desalue, et li revenue est legiere, plus que les autres jointures.	The shoulder joint dislocates, and the return is lighter than the other joints.

des dislocations de la hainche	Of dislocations of the shoulder
Saiches que as jointures de la hainche et as jointures de l’espaule ne vient fuers que dislocacions soulement, ne n’i vient mie si com as autres jointures;	Experienced that the joints of the shoulder and the elbow are only dislocations, and they do not come with other joints;
et li jointure de la hainche est desaluee selonc IIII parties:	And the joint of the elbow is dislocated according to four parts:
dedens et defuer ,et devant et derrier;	First, the muscles and tendons are stretched, and then in front and behind.
et plus dedens c’aillors, et poc desalue devant et derrier.	And more muscles are stretched, and it becomes dislocated in front and behind.
Et li conoissance de sa dislocations dedens si est que quant on joint la jambe malaide avec la sainne, si est plus longe, et apert plus li malaides genous que li sains, et ne puet li malaides doubler son genoil au feu;	And the knowledge of its dislocations is clear if, when the injured leg is joint with the healthy one, it is longer and more open, and the injured bone can double its girth at the fire;
et est li leus qui est delez enflez d’aposteme chaut, por ceu que li chiés de la cuixe vient lai.	And it is the one that is deformed due to strangulation of the wound, because the head of the bone comes out.
Et li signe de celui cui il vient au defuer, si est que cist accident sont contraire a ces devant.	And the sign of him who comes to the forge, if this accident is contrary to these fronts.
Et li signes de celui cui avient au devant, si est qu’il estent bien sa jambe selonc l’acomplissement;	And the signs of him who comes to the front, if they are well according to his completion,
toutevoie, ne double mie le genoil sens dolor, et s’on le vuet faire aler, si ne puet avant, et retient son urine, et enfle li angre, et quant il vait, si passe sus le talon.	there is no need to multiply the genital sensation with pain, and if you see him doing so, before, and retain his urine, and it will be discharged, and when he goes, it passes through the anus.
Et li signes de celui cui il avient derrier, si est qu’il ne puet espandre son genoil, ne doubler, et est celle jambe plus torte de l’autre, et li angre est mollifié, et est li chiés de la cuixe au leu desoz les costes.	And the signs of him who came to the rear, if he cannot expand his gentle, and double, and that leg is more tense than the other, and the anus is softened, and the head of the shoulder is raised against the costal bones.
Li ramenemens de ceste semblance de dislocation si est que tu rewarde se li dislocations est anciainne, et elle demore selonc sa disposition, si n’i a nule cure;	The symptoms of this kind of dislocation are that if you reward it with the dislocations, they are ancient, and they depend on its position, if there is no cure.
et n’i covient mie qu’il ait presumption.	and it only requires presumption.

par aventure si revenra, et n’a mestier d’autre cure.	If by chance it returns, and there is no other cure.

et uns autres ministres estende sa main desus en teil maniere qu’il boute ses mains desoz ses asseles, puis l’estrigne d’un souef liien sus la cuixe;	and some other supports extend your hand in this way that it covers your hands with its nails, then straighten the leg by pulling with a line below the knee.

Ceste maniere d’estension si est commune as IIII semblances, et se li dislocation est revenue, si com nos avons dit, c’est bien.	This manner of extension is common to four appearances, and if the dislocation returns, as we have said, it is well.
Se ceu non, si covient mettre cure a sa semblance.	If this is not the case, then it is necessary to provide care for his appearance.
Quant li dislocations est au pardedens, si covient que tu sovines le malaide sus son costeit sain, puis met le liien sus la racine de la cuixe, et le leu qui est desoz l’angre, puis estent le liien en haut devers l’angre, et devers la forcele;	If the dislocation is at the shoulder, then it is necessary to bring the patient to the surgeon's care if the costal cartilage is still intact, then tie the ligament around the root of the clavicle, and the bone that is dislocated, then tie the ligament towards the angle and towards the force;

et ceste maniere de dislocation est plus legiere des autres.	and this method of dislocation is lighter than the others.

de la dislocation dou genoil	Of the dislocation of the shoulder
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres:	The shoulder is dislocated in three ways.
c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier;	It is known to be dislocated from the front, back, and side.
et ne desalue point devant.	and do not move away.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;	And the signs are that you command the patient to bend their knee at the ankle, and if the heel does not touch the ground, it is dislocated.
et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;	And the restoration is that you make the patient lie on their side, and extend the leg if possible, and place your back on theirs, and place your hand on theirs.

de la dislocation dou talon	of the dislocation of the big toe
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The big toe is never used, and it is never completely dislocated, and it is bent and twisted.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:	And signs if the ankle is swollen, and try before the part where it is dislocated:
li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	If the limb is light, and it should be gently stretched with one's hands as soon as possible.

s’elle revient, c’est bien;	If it returns, that's good.
se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	If not, if the evacuation does not return, because it comes back.

puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors;	Then the bandage is changed every three days or four, and the patient should use the splint for fourteen days.
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	And if it does not improve by the end of the treatment, it is a sign that it will continue to dislocate.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If the wound becomes inflamed and comes, if it is necessary to calm it, as we have said elsewhere, until it is healthy.
des dois	Of two things, one is that the
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	If both are dislocated, and they are able to be extended gently in the work, it is a light thing.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	And if the dislocation is in no way near the shoulder blade or collarbone, it is necessary to put the splint on the upper part of the shoulder or on the .ie. table, and place your hand on the open joints, then press firmly with your hand until it re-emerges.
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie;	When it is equal and it does not open, if he puts his thumb on the point of the shoulder at the head of the humerus, then the dislocation forms and he leaves it alone for three days, then he removes it.
et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and he makes him rest, as long as he is healthy.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	Of wound and dislocation together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	When a wound comes with the dislocation, and it is seen to be restored, often the patient dies.
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	If you are not presumptuous in the cure, if you are not skilled in the art and have not used it long, and if you are piteous and merciful and slow, do not be harsh.
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	and use at the beginning of things reassuring aphorisms to calm the patient, and leave the patient in the hands of God, if you do not see hope for health.
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	and when you see hope, now reset the member in its place, otherwise the dislocation will worsen.
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	and when the member is in its place, apply reassuring things reassuring aphorisms to calm the patient, and treat the wound, if necessary, with desiccants.
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	and if the dislocation is a fracture, and the bones are broken, then the bones, and do what we have said in simple diseases.
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	You must not enter the path of despair, according to what I said, for this is good for you according to your Creator, and by the wisdom of your arm and heart.
